 <hr><center><h1>Shri Guru Granth Sahib: Raag Maaroo</h1></center>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 001</h2></center>
  Raag Maaroo, First Mehl, First House, Chau-Padas:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. Truth Is The Name. Creative Being Personified. No Fear. No Hatred. Image Of The Undying. Beyond Birth. Self-Existent. By Guru's Grace:<br>
  Shalok:<br>
  O my Friend, I shall forever remain the dust of Your feet.<br>
  Nanak seeks Your protection, and beholds You ever-present, here and now. ||1||<br>
  SHABAD:<br>
  Those who receive the call in the last hours of the night, chant the Name of their Lord and Master.<br>
  Tents, canopies, pavilions and carriages are prepared and made ready for them.<br>
  You send out the call, Lord, to those who meditate on Your Name. ||1||<br>
  Father, I am unfortunate, a fraud.<br>
  I have not found Your Name; my mind is blind and deluded by doubt. ||1||Pause||<br>
  I have enjoyed the tastes, and now my pains have come to fruition; such is my pre-ordained destiny, O my mother.<br>
  Now my joys are few, and my pains are many. In utter agony, I pass my life. ||2||<br>
  What separation could be worse than separation from the Lord? For those who are united with Him, what other union can there be?<br>
  Praise the Lord and Master, who, having created this play, beholds it. ||3||<br>
  By good destiny, this union comes about; this body enjoys its pleasures.<br>
  Those who have lost their destiny, suffer separation from this union. O Nanak, they may still be united once again! ||4||1||<br>
  Maaroo, First Mehl:<br>
  The union of the mother and father brings the body into being.<br>
  The Creator inscribes upon it the inscription of its destiny.<br>
  According to this inscription, gifts, light and glorious greatness are received.<br>
  Joining with Maya, the spiritual consciousness is lost. ||1||<br>
  O foolish mind, why are you so proud?<br>
  You shall have to arise and depart when it pleases your Lord and Master. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Abandon the tastes of the world, and find intuitive peace.<br>
  All must abandon their worldly homes; no one remains here forever.<br>
  Eat some, and save the rest,<br>
  if you are destined to return to the world again. ||2||<br>
  He adorns his body and ress in silk robes.<br>
  He issues all sorts of commands.<br>
  Preparing his comfortable bed, he sleeps.<br>
  When he falls into the hands of the Messenger of Death, what good does it do to cry out? ||3||<br>
  Household affairs are whirlpools of entanglements, O Siblings of Destiny.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 002</h2></center>
  Sin is a stone which does not float.<br>
  So let the Fear of God be the boat to carry your soul across.<br>
  Says Nanak, rare are those who are blessed with this Boat. ||4||2||<br>
  Maaroo, First Mehl, First House:<br>
  Actions are the paper, and the mind is the ink; good and bad are both recorded upon it.<br>
  As their past actions drive them, so are mortals driven. There is no end to Your Glorious Virtues, Lord. ||1||<br>
  Why do you not keep Him in your consciousness, you mad man?<br>
  Forgetting the Lord, your own virtues shall rot away. ||1||Pause||<br>
  The night is a net, and the day is a net; there are as many traps as there are moments.<br>
  With relish and delight, you continually bite at the bait; you are trapped, you fool - how will you ever escape? ||2||<br>
  The body is a furnace, and the mind is the iron within it; the five fires are heating it.<br>
  Sin is the charcoal placed upon it, which burns the mind; the tongs are anxiety and worry. ||3||<br>
  What was turned to slag is again transformed into gold, if one meets with the Guru.<br>
  He blesses the mortal with the Ambrosial Name of the One Lord, and then, O Nanak, the body is held steady. ||4||3||<br>
  Maaroo, First Mehl:<br>
  In the pure, immaculate waters, both the lotus and the slimy scum are found.<br>
  The lotus flower is with the scum and the water, but it remains untouched by any pollution. ||1||<br>
  You frog, you will never understand.<br>
  You eat the dirt, while you dwell in the immaculate waters. You know nothing of the ambrosial nectar there. ||1||Pause||<br>
  You dwell continually in the water; the bumble bee does not dwell there, but it is intoxicated with its fragrance from afar.<br>
  Intuitively sensing the moon in the distance, the lotus bows its head. ||2||<br>
  The realms of nectar are irrigated with milk and honey; you think you are clever to live in the water.<br>
  You can never escape your own inner tendencies, like the love of the flea for blood. ||3||<br>
  The fool may live with the Pandit, the religious scholar, and listen to the Vedas and the Shaastras.<br>
  You can never escape your own inner tendencies, like the crooked tail of the dog. ||4||<br>
  Some are hypocrites; they do not merge with the Naam, the Name of the Lord. Some are absorbed in the Feet of the Lord, Har, Har.<br>
  The mortals obtain what they are predestined to receive; O Nanak, with your tongue, chant the Naam. ||5||4||<br>
  Maaroo, First Mehl,<br>
  Shalok:<br>
  Countless sinners are sanctified, attaching their minds to the Feet of the Lord.<br>
  The merits of the sixty-eight places of pilgrimage are found in God's Name, O Nanak, when such destiny is inscribed upon one's forehead. ||1||<br>
  SHABAD:<br>
  O friends and companions, so puffed up with pride,<br>
  listen to this one joyous story of your Husband Lord. ||1||<br>
  Who can I tell about my pain, O my mother?<br>
  Without the Lord, my soul cannot survive; how can I comfort it, O my mother? ||1||Pause||<br>
  I am a dejected, discarded bride, totally miserable.<br>
  I have lost my youth; I regret and repent. ||2||<br>
  You are my wise Lord and Master, above my head.<br>
  I serve You as Your humble slave. ||3||<br>
  Nanak humbly prays, this is my only concern:<br>
  without the Blessed Vision of my Beloved, how can I enjoy Him? ||4||5||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 003</h2></center>
  Maaroo, First Mehl:<br>
  I am Your slave, Your bonded servant, and so I am called fortunate.<br>
  I sold myself at Your store in exchange for the Guru's Word; whatever You link me to, to that I am linked. ||1||<br>
  What cleverness can Your servant try with You?<br>
  O my Lord and Master, I cannot carry out the Hukam of Your Command. ||1||Pause||<br>
  My mother is Your slave, and my father is Your slave; I am the child of Your slaves.<br>
  My slave mother dances, and my slave father sings; I practice devotional worship to You, O my Sovereign Lord. ||2||<br>
  If You wish to drink, then I shall get water for You; if You wish to eat, I shall grind the corn for You.<br>
  I wave the fan over You, and wash Your feet, and continue to chant Your Name. ||3||<br>
  I have been untrue to myself, but Nanak is Your slave; please forgive him, by Your glorious greatness.<br>
  Since the very beginning of time, and throughout the ages, You have been the merciful and generous Lord. Without You, liberation cannot be attained. ||4||6||<br>
  Maaroo, First Mehl:<br>
  Some call him a ghost; some say that he is a demon.<br>
  Some call him a mere mortal; O, poor Nanak! ||1||<br>
  Crazy Nanak has gone insane, after his Lord, the King.<br>
  I know of none other than the Lord. ||1||Pause||<br>
  He alone is known to be insane, when he goes insane with the Fear of God.<br>
  He recognizes none other than the One Lord and Master. ||2||<br>
  He alone is known to be insane, if he works for the One Lord.<br>
  Recognizing the Hukam, the Command of his Lord and Master, what other cleverness is there? ||3||<br>
  He alone is known to be insane, when he falls in love with his Lord and Master.<br>
  He sees himself as bad, and all the rest of the world as good. ||4||7||<br>
  Maaroo, First Mehl:<br>
  This wealth is all-pervading, permeating all.<br>
  The self-willed manmukh wanders around, thinking that it is far away. ||1||<br>
  That commodity, the wealth of the Naam, is within my heart.<br>
  Whoever You bless with it, is emancipated. ||1||Pause||<br>
  This wealth does not burn; it cannot be stolen by a thief.<br>
  This wealth does not drown, and its owner is never punished. ||2||<br>
  Gaze upon the glorious greatness of this wealth,<br>
  and your nights and days will pass, imbued with celestial peace. ||3||<br>
  Listen to this incomparably beautiful story, O my brothers, O Siblings of Destiny.<br>
  Tell me, without this wealth, who has ever obtained the supreme status? ||4||<br>
  Nanak humbly prays, I proclaim the Unspoken Speech of the Lord.<br>
  If one meets the True Guru, then this wealth is obtained. ||5||8||<br>
  Maaroo, First Mehl:<br>
  Heat up the sun energy of the right nostril, and cool down the moon energy of the left nostril; practicing this breath-control, bring them into perfect balance.<br>
  In this way, the fickle fish of the mind will be held steady; the swan-soul shall not fly away, and the body-wall will not crumble. ||1||<br>
  You fool, why are you deluded by doubt?<br>
  You do not remember the detached Lord of supreme bliss. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Seize and burn the unbearable; seize and kill the imperishable; leave behind your doubts, and then, you shall drink in the Nectar.<br>
  In this way, the fickle fish of the mind will be held steady; the swan-soul shall not fly away, and the body-wall shall not crumble. ||2||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 004</h2></center>
  Nanak humbly prays, if the Lord's humble servant dwells upon Him, in his mind of minds, with his every breath, then he drinks in the Ambrosial Nectar.<br>
  In this way, the fickle fish of the mind will be held steady; the swan-soul shall not fly away, and the body-wall shall not crumble. ||3||9||<br>
  Maaroo, First Mehl:<br>
  Maya is not conquered, and the mind is not subdued; the waves of desire in the world-ocean are intoxicating wine.<br>
  The boat crosses over the water, carrying the true merchandise.<br>
  The jewel within the mind subdues the mind; attached to the Truth, it is not broken.<br>
  The king is seated upon the throne, imbued with the Fear of God and the five qualities. ||1||<br>
  O Baba, do not see your True Lord and Master as being far away.<br>
  He is the Light of all, the Life of the world; The True Lord writes His Inscription on each and every head. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Brahma and Vishnu, the Rishis and the silent sages, Shiva and Indra, penitents and beggars<br>
  - whoever obeys the Hukam of the Lord's Command, looks beautiful in the Court of the True Lord, while the stubborn rebels die.<br>
  The wandering beggars, warriors, celibates and Sannyaasee hermits - through the Perfect Guru, consider this:<br>
  without selfless service, no one ever receives the fruits of their rewards. Serving the Lord is the most excellent action. ||2||<br>
  You are the wealth of the poor, the Guru of the guru-less, the honor of the dishonored.<br>
  I am blind; I have grasped hold of the jewel, the Guru. You are the strength of the weak.<br>
  He is not known through burnt offerings and ritual chanting; the True Lord is known through the Guru's Teachings.<br>
  Without the Naam, the Name of the Lord, no one finds shelter in the Court of the Lord; the false come and go in reincarnation. ||3||<br>
  So praise the True Name, and through the True Name, you will find satisfaction.<br>
  When the mind is cleaned with the jewel of spiritual wisdom, it does not become dirty again.<br>
  As long as the Lord and Master dwells in the mind, no obstacles are encountered.<br>
  O Nanak, giving one's head, one is emancipated, and the mind and body become true. ||4||10||<br>
  Maaroo, First Mehl:<br>
  The Yogi who is joined to the Naam, the Name of the Lord, is pure; he is not stained by even a particle of dirt.<br>
  The True Lord, his Beloved, is always with him; the rounds of birth and death are ended for him. ||1||<br>
  O Lord of the Universe, what is Your Name, and what is it like?<br>
  If You summon me into the Mansion of Your Presence, I will ask You, how I can become one with You. ||1||Pause||<br>
  He alone is a Brahmin, who takes his cleansing bath in the spiritual wisdom of God, and whose leaf-offerings in worship are the Glorious Praises of the Lord.<br>
  The One Name, the One Lord, and His One Light pervade the three worlds. ||2||<br>
  My tongue is the balance of the scale, and this heart of mine is the pan of the scale; I weigh the immeasurable Naam.<br>
  There is one store, and one banker above all; the merchants deal in the one commodity. ||3||<br>
  The True Guru saves us at both ends; he alone understands, who is lovingly focused on the One Lord; his inner being remains free of doubt.<br>
  The Word of the Shabad abides within, and doubt is ended, for those who constantly serve, day and night. ||4||<br>
  Above is the sky of the mind, and beyond this sky is the Lord, the Protector of the World; the Inaccessible Lord God; the Guru abides there as well.<br>
  According to the Word of the Guru's Teachings, what is outside is the same as what is inside the home of the self. Nanak has become a detached renunciate. ||5||11||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 005</h2></center>
  Raag Maaroo, First Mehl, Fifth House:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  Day and night, he remains awake and aware; he never sleeps or dreams.<br>
  He alone knows this, who feels the pain of separation from God.<br>
  My body is pierced through with the arrow of love. How can any physician know the cure? ||1||<br>
  Rare is that one, who as Gurmukh, understands, and whom the True Lord links to His Praise.<br>
  He alone appreciates the value of the Ambsosial Nectar, who deals in this Ambrosia. ||1||Pause||<br>
  The soul-bride is in love with her Husband Lord;<br>
  the focuses her consciousness on the Word of the Guru's Shabad.<br>
  The soul-bride is joyously embellished with intuitive ease; her hunger and thirst are taken away. ||2||<br>
  Tear down skepticism and dispel your doubt;<br>
  with your intuition, draw the bow of the Praise of the Lord.<br>
  Through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, conquer and subdue your mind; take the support of Yoga - Union with the beautiful Lord. ||3||<br>
  Burnt by egotism, one forgets the Lord from his mind.<br>
  In the City of Death, he is attacked with massive swords.<br>
  Then, even if he asks for it, he will not receive the Lord's Name; O soul, you shall suffer terrible punishment. ||4||<br>
  You are distracted by thoughts of Maya and worldly attachment.<br>
  In the City of Death, you will be caught by the noose of the Messenger of Death.<br>
  You cannot break free from the bondage of loving attachment, and so the Messenger of Death will torture you. ||5||<br>
  I have done nothing; I am doing nothing now.<br>
  The True Guru has blessed me with the Ambrosial Nectar of the Naam.<br>
  What other efforts can anyone make, when You bestow Your blessing? Nanak seeks Your Sanctuary. ||6||1||12||<br>
  Maaroo, Third Mehl, First House:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  Wherever You seat me, there I sit, O my Lord and Master; wherever You send me, there I go.<br>
  In the entire village, there is only One King; all places are sacred. ||1||<br>
  O Baba, while I dwell in this body, let me sing Your True Praises,<br>
  that I may intuitively merge with You. ||1||Pause||<br>
  He thinks that good and bad deeds come from himself; this is the source of all evil.<br>
  Whatever happens in this world is only by the Order of our Lord and Master. ||2||<br>
  Sexual desires are so strong and compelling; where has this sexual desire come from?<br>
  The Creator Himself stages all the plays; how rare are those who realize this. ||3||<br>
  By Guru's Grace, one is lovingly focused on the One Lord, and then, duality is ended.<br>
  Whatever is in harmony with His Will, he accepts as True; the noose of Death is loosened from around his neck. ||4||<br>
  Prays Nanak, who can call him to account, when the egotistical pride of his mind has been silenced?<br>
  Even the Righteous Judge of Dharma is intimidated and afraid of him; he has entered the Sanctuary of the True Lord. ||5||1||<br>
  Maaroo, Third Mehl:<br>
  Coming and going in reincarnation no longer exist, when one dwells in the home of the self within.<br>
  He bestowed the Blessing of His treasure of truth; only He Himself knows. ||1||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 006</h2></center>
  O my mind, remember the Dear Lord, and abandon the corruption of your mind.<br>
  Meditate on the Word of the Guru's Shabad; focus lovingly on the Truth. ||1||Pause||<br>
  One who forgets the Name in this world, shall not find any place of rest anywhere else.<br>
  He shall wander in all sorts of reincarnations, and rot away in manure. ||2||<br>
  By great good fortune, I have found the Guru, according to my pre-ordained destiny, O my mother.<br>
  Night and day, I practice true devotional worship; I am united with the True Lord. ||3||<br>
  He Himself fashioned the entire universe; He Himself bestows His Glance of Grace.<br>
  O Nanak, the Naam, the Name of the Lord, is glorious and great; as He pleases, He bestows His Blessings. ||4||2||<br>
  Maaroo, Third Mehl:<br>
  Please forgive my past mistakes, O my Dear Lord; now, please place me on the Path.<br>
  I remain attached to the Lord's Feet, and eradicate self-conceit from within. ||1||<br>
  O my mind, as Gurmukh, meditate on the Name of the Lord.<br>
  Remain attached forever to the Lord's Feet, single-mindedly, with love for the One Lord. ||1||Pause||<br>
  I have no social status or honor; I have no place or home.<br>
  Pierced through by the Word of the Shabad, my doubts have been cut away. The Guru has inspired me to understand the Naam, the Name of the Lord. ||2||<br>
  This mind wanders around, driven by greed, totally attached to greed.<br>
  He is engrossed in false pursuits; he shall endure beatings in the City of Death. ||3||<br>
  O Nanak, God Himself Himself is all-in-all. There is no other at all.<br>
  He bestows the treasure of devotional worship, and the Gurmukhs abide in peace. ||4||3||<br>
  Maaroo, Third Mehl:<br>
  Seek and find those who are imbued with Truth; they are so rare in this world.<br>
  Meeting with them, one's face becomes radiant and bright, chanting the Name of the Lord. ||1||<br>
  O Baba, contemplate and cherish the True Lord and Master within your heart.<br>
  Seek out and see, and ask your True Guru, and obtain the true commodity. ||1||Pause||<br>
  All serve the One True Lord; through pre-ordained destiny, they meet Him.<br>
  The Gurmukhs merge with Him, and will not be separated from Him again; they attain the True Lord. ||2||<br>
  Some do not appreciate the value of devotional worship; the self-willed manmukhs are deluded by doubt.<br>
  They are fillled with self-conceit; they cannot accomplish anything. ||3||<br>
  Stand and offer your prayer, to the One who cannot be moved by force.<br>
  O Nanak, the Naam, the Name of the Lord, abides within the mind of the Gurmukh; hearing his prayer, the Lord applauds him. ||4||4||<br>
  Maaroo, Third Mehl:<br>
  He transforms the burning desert into a cool oasis; he transmutes rusted iron into gold.<br>
  So praise the True Lord; there is none other as great as He is. ||1||<br>
  O my mind, night and day, meditate on the Lord's Name.<br>
  Contemplate the Word of the Guru's Teachings, and sing the Glorious Praises of the Lord, night and day. ||1||Pause||<br>
  As Gurmukh, one comes to know the One Lord, when the True Guru instructs him.<br>
  Praise the True Guru, who imparts this understanding. ||2||<br>
  Those who forsake the True Guru, and attach themselves to duality - what will they do when they go to the world hereafter?<br>
  Bound and gagged in the City of Death, they will be beaten. They will be punished severely. ||3||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 007</h2></center>
  My God is independent and self-sufficient; he does not have even an iota of greed.<br>
  O Nanak, run to His Sanctuary; granting His forgiveness, He merges us into Himself. ||4||5||<br>
  Maaroo, Fourth Mehl, Second House:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  Suk-deva and Janak meditated on the Naam; following the Guru's Teachings, they sought the Sanctuary of the Lord, Har, Har.<br>
  God met Sudama and removed his poverty; through loving devotional worship, he crossed over.<br>
  God is the Lover of His devotees; the Lord's Name is fufilling; God showers His Mercy on the Gurmukhs. ||1||<br>
  O my mind, chanting the Naam, the Name of the Lord, you will be saved.<br>
  Dhroo, Prahlaad and Bidar the slave-girl's son, became Gurmukh, and through the Naam, crossed over. ||1||Pause||<br>
  In this Dark Age of Kali Yuga, the Naam is the supreme wealth; it saves the humble devotees.<br>
  All the faults of Naam Dayv, Jai Dayv, Kabeer, Trilochan and Ravi Daas the leather-worker were covered.<br>
  Those who become Gurmukh, and remain attached to the Naam, are saved; all their sins are washed off. ||2||<br>
  Whoever chants the Naam, all his sins and mistakes are taken away.<br>
  Ajaamal, who had sex with prostitites, was saved, by chanting the Name of the Lord.<br>
  Chanting the Naam, Ugar Sain obtained salvation; his bonds were broken, and he was liberated. ||3||<br>
  God Himself takes pity on His humble servants, and makes them His own.<br>
  My Lord of the Universe saves the honor of His servants; those who seek His Sanctuary are saved.<br>
  The Lord has showered servant Nanak with His Mercy; he has enshrined the Lord's Name within his heart. ||4||1||<br>
  Maaroo, Fourth Mehl:<br>
  The Siddhas in Samaadhi meditate on Him; they are lovingly focused on Him. The seekers and the silent sages meditate on Him as well.<br>
  The celibates, the true and contented beings meditate on Him; Indra and the other gods chant His Name with their mouths.<br>
  Those who seek His Sanctuary meditate on Him; they become Gurmukh and swim across. ||1||<br>
  O my mind, chant the Naam, the Name of the Lord, and cross over.<br>
  Dhanna the farmer, and Balmik the highway robber, became Gurmukh, and crossed over. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Angels, men, heavenly heralds and celestial singers meditate on Him; even the humble Rishis sing of the Lord.<br>
  Shiva, Brahma and the goddess Lakhshmi, meditate, and chant with their mouths the Name of the Lord, Har, Har.<br>
  Those whose minds are drenched with the Name of the Lord, Har, Har, as Gurmukh, cross over. ||2||<br>
  Millions and millions, three hundred thirty million gods meditate on Him; there is no end to those who meditate on the Lord.<br>
  The Vedas, the Puraanas and the Simritees meditate on the Lord; the Pandits, the religious scholars, sing the Lord's Praises as well.<br>
  Those whose minds are filled with the Naam, the source of nectar - as Gurmukh, they cross over. ||3||<br>
  Those who chant the Naam in endless waves - I cannot even count their number.<br>
  The Lord of the Universe bestows His Mercy, and those who are pleasing to the Mind of the Lord God, find their place.<br>
  The Guru, granting His Grace, implants the Lord's Name within; servant Nanak chants the Naam, the Name of the Lord. ||4||2||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 008</h2></center>
  Maaroo, Fourth Mehl, Third House:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  Take the treasure of the Name of the Lord, Har, Har. Follow the Guru's Teachings, and the Lord shall bless you with honor.<br>
  Here and hereafter, the Lord goes with you; in the end, He shall deliver you.<br>
  Where the path is difficult and the street is narrow, there the Lord shall liberate you. ||1||<br>
  O my True Guru, implant within me the Name of the Lord, Har, Har.<br>
  The Lord is my mother, father, child and relative; I have none other than the Lord, O my mother. ||1||Pause||<br>
  I feel the pains of love and yearning for the Lord, and the Name of the Lord. If only someone would come and unite me with Him, O my mother.<br>
  I bow in humble devotion to one who inspires me to meet with my Beloved.<br>
  The almighty and merciful True Guru unites me with the Lord God instantaneously. ||2||<br>
  Those who do not remember the Name of the Lord, Har, Har, are most unfortunate, and are slaughtered.<br>
  They wander in reincarnation, again and again; they die, and are re-born, and continue coming and going.<br>
  Bound and gagged at Death's Door, they are cruelly beaten, and punished in the Court of the Lord. ||3||<br>
  O God, I seek Your Sanctuary; O my Sovereign Lord King, please unite me with Yourself.<br>
  O Lord, Life of the World, please shower me with Your Mercy; grant me the Sanctuary of the Guru, the True Guru.<br>
  The Dear Lord, becoming merciful, has blended servant Nanak with Himself. ||4||1||3||<br>
  Maaroo, Fourth Mehl:<br>
  I inquire about the commodity of the Naam, the Name of the Lord. Is there anyone who can show me the wealth, the capital of the Lord?<br>
  I cut myself into pieces, and make myself a sacrifice to that one who leads me to meet my Lord God.<br>
  I am filled with the Love of my Beloved; how can I meet my Friend, and merge with Him? ||1||<br>
  O my beloved friend, my mind, I take the wealth, the capital of the Name of the Lord, Har, Har.<br>
  The Perfect Guru has implanted the Naam within me; the Lord is my support - I celebrate the Lord. ||1||Pause||<br>
  O my Guru, please unite me with the Lord, Har, Har; show me the wealth, the capital of the Lord.<br>
  Without the Guru, love does not well up; see this, and know it in your mind.<br>
  The Lord has installed Himself within the Guru; so praise the Guru, who unites us with the Lord. ||2||<br>
  The ocean, the treasure of devotional worship of the Lord, rests with the Perfect True Guru.<br>
  When it pleases the True Guru, He opens the treasure, and and the Gurmukhs are illuminated by the Lord's Light.<br>
  The unfortunate self-willed manmukhs die of thirst, on the very bank of the river. ||3||<br>
  The Guru is the Great Giver; I beg for this gift from the Guru,<br>
  that He may unite me with God, from whom I was separated for so long! This is the great hope of my mind and body.<br>
  If it pleases You, O my Guru, please listen to my prayer; this is servant Nanak's prayer. ||4||2||4||<br>
  Maaroo, Fourth Mehl:<br>
  O Lord God, please preach Your sermon to me. Through the Guru's Teachings, the Lord is merged into my heart.<br>
  Meditate on the sermon of the Lord, Har, Har, O very fortunate ones; the Lord shall bless you with the most sublime status of Nirvaanaa.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 009</h2></center>
  The minds of the Gurmukhs are filled with faith; through the Perfect Guru, they merge in the Naam, the Name of the Lord. ||1||<br>
  O my mind, the sermon of the Lord, Har, Har, is pleasing to my mind.<br>
  Continually and forever, speak the sermon of the Lord, Har, Har; as Gurmukh, speak the Unspoken Speech. ||1||Pause||<br>
  I have searched through and through my mind and body; how can I attain this Unspoken Speech?<br>
  Meeting with the humble Saints, I have found it; listening to the Unspoken Speech, my mind is pleased.<br>
  The Lord's Name is the Support of my mind and body; I am united with the all-knowing Primal Lord God. ||2||<br>
  The Guru, the Primal Being, has united me with the Primal Lord God. My consciousness has merged into the supreme consciousness.<br>
  By great good fortune, I serve the Guru, and I have found my Lord, all-wise and all-knowing.<br>
  The self-willed manmukhs are very unfortunate; they pass their life-night in misery and pain. ||3||<br>
  I am just a meek beggar at Your Door, God; please, place the Ambrosial Word of Your Bani in my mouth.<br>
  The True Guru is my friend; He unites me with my all-wise, all-knowing Lord God.<br>
  Servant Nanak has entered Your Sanctuary; grant Your Grace, and merge me into Your Name. ||4||3||5||<br>
  Maaroo, Fourth Mehl:<br>
  Detached from the world, I am in love with the Lord; by great good fortune, I have enshrined the Lord within my mind.<br>
  Joining the Sangat, the Holy Congregation, faith has welled up within me; through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, I taste the sublime essence of the Lord.<br>
  My mind and body have totally blossomed forth; through the Word of the Guru's Bani, I chant the Glorious Praises of the Lord. ||1||<br>
  O my beloved mind, my friend, taste the sublime essence of the Name of the Lord, Har, Har.<br>
  Through the Perfect Guru, I have found the Lord, who saves my honor, here and hereafter. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Meditate on the Name of the Lord, Har, Har; as Gurmukh, taste the Kirtan of the Lord's Praises.<br>
  Plant the seed of the Lord in the body-farm. The Lord God is enshrined within the Sangat, the Holy Congregation.<br>
  The Name of the Lord, Har, Har, is Ambrosial Nectar. Through the Perfect Guru, taste the sublime essence of the Lord. ||2||<br>
  The self-willed manmukhs are filled with hunger and thirst; their minds run around in the ten directions, hoping for great wealth.<br>
  Without the Name of the Lord, their life is cursed; the manmukhs are stuck in manure.<br>
  They come and go, and are consigned to wander through uncounted incarnations, eating stinking rot. ||3||<br>
  Begging, imploring, I seek Your Sanctuary; Lord, shower me with Your Mercy, and save me, God.<br>
  Lead me to join the Society of the Saints, and bless me with the honor and glory of the Lord's Name.<br>
  I have obtained the wealth of the Name of the Lord, Har, Har; servant Nanak chants the Lord's Name, through the Guru's Teachings. ||4||4||6||<br>
  Maaroo, Fourth Mehl, Fifth House:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  Devotional worship to the Lord, Har, Har, is an overflowing treasure.<br>
  The Gurmukh is emancipated by the Lord.<br>
  One who is blessed by the Mercy of my Lord and Master sings the Glorious Praises of the Lord. ||1||<br>
  O Lord, Har, Har, take pity on me,<br>
  that within my heart, I may dwell upon You, Lord, forever and ever.<br>
  Chant the Name of the Lord, Har, Har, O my soul; chanting the Name of the Lord, Har, Har, you shall be emancipated. ||1||Pause||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 010</h2></center>
  The Ambrosial Name of the Lord is the ocean of peace.<br>
  The beggar begs for it; O Lord, please bless him, in Your kindness.<br>
  True, True is the Lord; the Lord is forever True; the True Lord is pleasing to my mind. ||2||<br>
  The nine holes pour out filth.<br>
  Chanting the Lord's Name, they are all purified and sanctified.<br>
  When my Lord and Master is totally pleased, He leads the mortal to meditate in remembrance on the Lord, and then his filth is taken away. ||3||<br>
  Attachment to Maya is terribly treacherous.<br>
  How can one cross over the difficult world-ocean?<br>
  The True Lord bestows the boat of the True Guru; meditating on the Lord, Har, Har, one is carried across. ||4||<br>
  You are everywhere; all are Yours.<br>
  Whatever You do, God, that alone comes to pass.<br>
  Poor servant Nanak sings the Glorious Praises of the Lord; as it pleases the Lord, He bestows His approval. ||5||1||7||<br>
  Maaroo, Fourth Mehl:<br>
  Chant the Name of the Lord, Har, Har, O my mind.<br>
  The Lord shall eradicate all your sins.<br>
  Treasure the Lord's wealth, and gather in the Lord's wealth; when you depart in the end, the Lord shall go along with you as your only friend and companion. ||1||<br>
  He alone meditates on the Lord, unto whom He grants His Grace.<br>
  He continually chants the Lord's Chant; meditating on the Lord, one finds peace.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, the sublime essence of the Lord is obtained. Meditating on the Lord, Har, Har, one is carried across. ||1||Pause||<br>
  The fearless, formless Lord - the Name is Truth.<br>
  To chant it is the most sublime and exalted activity in this world.<br>
  Doing so, the Messenger of Death, the evil enemy, is killed. Death does not even approach the Lord's servant. ||2||<br>
  One whose mind is satisfied with the Lord<br>
  - that servant is known throughout the four ages, in all four directions.<br>
  If some sinner speaks evil of him, the Messenger of Death chews him up. ||3||<br>
  The One Pure Creator Lord is in all.<br>
  He stages all His wondrous plays, and watches them.<br>
  Who can kill that person, whom the Lord has saved? The Creator Lord Himself delivers him. ||4||<br>
  I chant the Name of the Creator Lord, night and day.<br>
  He saves all His servants and devotees.<br>
  Consult the eighteen Puraanas and the four Vedas; O servant Nanak, only the Naam, the Name of the Lord, will deliver you. ||5||2||8||<br>
  Maaroo, Fifth Mehl, Second House:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  The earth, the Akaashic ethers and the stars abide in the Fear of God. The almighty Order of the Lord is over the heads of all.<br>
  Wind, water and fire abide in the Fear of God; poor Indra abides in the Fear of God as well. ||1||<br>
  I have heard one thing, that the One Lord alone is fearless.<br>
  He alone is at peace, and he alone is embellished forever, who meets with the Guru, and sings the Glorious Praises of the Lord. ||1||Pause||<br>
  The embodied and the divine beings abide in the Fear of God. The Siddhas and seekers die in the Fear of God.<br>
  The 8.4 millions species of beings die, and die again, and are born over and over again. They are consigned to reincarnation. ||2||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 011</h2></center>
  Those who embody the energies of sattva-white light, raajas-red passion, and taamas-black darkness, abide in the Fear of God, along with the many created forms.<br>
  This miserable deceiver Maya abides in the Fear of God; the Righteous Judge of Dharma is utterly afraid of Him as well. ||3||<br>
  The entire expanse of the Universe is in the Fear of God; only the Creator Lord is without this Fear.<br>
  Says Nanak, God is the companion of His devotees; His devotees look beautiful in the Court of the Lord. ||4||1||<br>
  Maaroo, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  The five year old orphan boy Dhroo, by meditating in remembrance on the Lord, became stationary and permanent.<br>
  For the sake of his son, Ajaamal called out, "O Lord, Naaraayan", who struck down and killed the Messenger of Death. ||1||<br>
  My Lord and Master has saved many, countless beings.<br>
  I am meek, with little or no understanding, and unworthy; I seek protection at the Lord's Door. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Baalmeek the outcaste was saved, and the poor hunter was saved as well.<br>
  The elephant remembered the Lord in his mind for an instant, and so was carried across. ||2||<br>
  He saved His devotee Prahlaad, and tore Harnaakhash with his nails.<br>
  Bidar, the son of a slave-girl, was purified, and all his generations were redeemed. ||3||<br>
  What sins of mine should I speak of? I am intoxicated with false emotional attachment.<br>
  Nanak has entered the Sanctuary of the Lord; please, reach out and take me into Your embrace. ||4||2||<br>
  Maaroo, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  For the sake of riches, I wandered around in so many ways; I rushed around, making all sorts of efforts.<br>
  The deeds I did in egotism and pride, have all been done in vain. ||1||<br>
  Other days are of no use to me;<br>
  please bless me with those days, O Dear God, on which I may sing the Lord's Praises. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Gazing upon children, spouse, household and possessions, one is entangled in these.<br>
  Tasting the wine of Maya, one is intoxicated, and never sings of the Lord, Har, Har. ||2||<br>
  In this way, I have examined lots of methods, but without the Saints, it is not found.<br>
  You are the Great Giver, the great and almighty God; I have come to beg a gift from You. ||3||<br>
  Abandoning all pride and self-importance, I have sought the Sanctuary of the dust of the feet of the Lord's slave.<br>
  Says Nanak, meeting with the Lord, I have become one with Him; I have found supreme bliss and peace. ||4||3||<br>
  Maaroo, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  In what place is the Name established? Where does egotism dwell?<br>
  What injury have you suffered, listening to abuse from someone else's mouth? ||1||<br>
  Listen: who are you, and where did you come from?<br>
  You don't even know how long you will stay here; you have no hint of when you shall leave. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Wind and water have patience and tolerance; the earth has compassion and forgiveness, no doubt.<br>
  The union of the five tattvas - the five elements - has brought you into being. Which of these is evil? ||2||<br>
  The Primal Lord, the Architect of Destiny, formed your form; He also burdened you with egotism.<br>
  He alone is born and dies; He alone comes and goes. ||3||<br>
  Nothing of the color and the form of the creation shall remain; the entire expanse is transitory.<br>
  Prays Nanak, when He brings His play to its close, then only the One, the One Lord remains. ||4||4||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 012</h2></center>
  Maaroo, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Pride, emotional attachment, greed and corruption are gone; I have not placed anything else, other than the Lord, within my consciousness.<br>
  I have purchased the jewel of the Naam and the Glorious Praises of the Lord; loading this merchandise, I have set out on my journey. ||1||<br>
  The love which the Lord's servant feels for the Lord lasts forever.<br>
  In my life, I served my Lord and Master, and as I depart, I keep Him enshrined in my consciousness. ||1||Pause||<br>
  I have not turned my face away from my Lord and Master's Command.<br>
  He fills my household with celestial peace and bliss; if He asks me to leave, I leave at once. ||2||<br>
  When I am under the Lord's Command, I find even hunger pleasurable; I know no difference between sorrow and joy.<br>
  Whatever the Command of my Lord and Master is, I bow my forehead and accept it. ||3||<br>
  The Lord and Master has become merciful to His servant; He has embellished both this world and the next.<br>
  Blessed is that servant, and fruitful is his birth; O Nanak, he realizes his Lord and Master. ||4||5||<br>
  Maaroo, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Good karma has dawned for me - my Lord and Master has become merciful. I sing the Kirtan of the Praises of the Lord, Har, Har.<br>
  My struggle is ended; I have found peace and tranquility. All my wanderings have ceased. ||1||<br>
  Now, I have obtained the state of eternal life.<br>
  The Primal Lord, the Architect of Destiny, has come into my conscious mind; I seek the Sanctuary of the Saints. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Sexual desire, anger, greed and emotional attachment are eradicated; all my enemies are eliminated.<br>
  He is always ever-present, here and now, watching over me; He is never far away. ||2||<br>
  In peace and cool tranquility, my faith has been totally fulfilled; the Saints are my Helpers and Support.<br>
  He has purified the sinners in an instant; I cannot express His Glorious Praises. ||3||<br>
  I have become fearless; all fear has departed. The feet of the Lord of the Universe are my only Shelter.<br>
  Nanak sings the Praises of his Lord and Master; night and day, he is lovingly focused on Him. ||4||6||<br>
  Maaroo, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  He is all-powerful, the Master of all virtues, but you never sing of Him!<br>
  You shall have to leave all this in an instant, but again and again, you chase after it. ||1||<br>
  Why do you not contemplate your God?<br>
  You are entangled in association with your enemies, and the enjoyment of pleasures; your soul is burning up with them! ||1||Pause||<br>
  Hearing His Name, the Messenger of Death will release you, and yet, you do not enter His Sanctuary!<br>
  Turn out this wretched jackal, and seek the Shelter of that God. ||2||<br>
  Praising Him, you shall cross over the terrifying world-ocean, and yet, you have not fallen in love with Him!<br>
  This meager, short-lived dream, this thing - you are engrossed in it, over and over again. ||3||<br>
  When our Lord and Master, the ocean of mercy, grants His Grace, one finds honor in the Society of the Saints.<br>
  Says Nanak, I am rid of the illusion of the three-phased Maya, when God becomes my help and support. ||4||7||<br>
  Maaroo, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  The Inner-knower, the Searcher of hearts, knows everything; what can anyone hide from Him?<br>
  Your hands and feet will fall off in an instant, when you are burnt in the fire. ||1||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 013</h2></center>
  You fool, you have forgotten the Lord from your mind!<br>
  You eat His salt, and then you are untrue to Him; before your very eyes, you shall be torn apart. ||1||Pause||<br>
  The incurable disease has arisen in your body; it cannot be removed or overcome.<br>
  Forgetting God, one endures utter agony; this is the essence of reality which Nanak has realized. ||2||8||<br>
  Maaroo, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  I have enshrined the lotus feet of God within my consciousness.<br>
  I sing the Glorious Praises of the Lord, continually, continuously.<br>
  There is none other than Him at all.<br>
  He alone exists, in the beginning, in the middle, and in the end. ||1||<br>
  He Himself is the Shelter of the Saints. ||1||Pause||<br>
  The entire universe is under His control.<br>
  He Himself, the Formless Lord, is Himself by Himself.<br>
  Nanak holds tight to that True Lord.<br>
  He has found peace, and shall never suffer pain again. ||2||9||<br>
  Maaroo, Fifth Mehl, Third House:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  He is the Giver of peace to the breath of life, the Giver of life to the soul; how can you forget Him, you ignorant person?<br>
  You taste the weak, insipid wine, and you have gone insane. You have uselessly wasted this precious human life. ||1||<br>
  O man, such is the foolishness you practice.<br>
  Renouncing the Lord, the Support of the earth, you wander, deluded by doubt; you are engrossed in emotional attachment, associating with Maya, the slave-girl. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Abandoning the Lord, the Support of the earth, you serve her of lowly ancestry, and you pass you life acting egotistically.<br>
  You do useless deeds, you ignorant person; this is why you are called a blind, self-willed manmukh. ||2||<br>
  That which is true, you believe to be untrue; what is transitory, you believe to be permanent.<br>
  You grasp as your own, what belongs to others; in such delusions you are deluded. ||3||<br>
  The Kh'shaatriyas, Brahmins, Soodras and Vaishyas all cross over, through the Name of the One Lord.<br>
  Guru Nanak speaks the Teachings; whoever listens to them is carried across. ||4||1||10||<br>
  Maaroo, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  You may act in secrecy, but God is still with you; you can only deceive other people.<br>
  Forgetting your Dear Lord, you enjoy corrupt pleasures, and so you shall have to embrace red-hot pillars. ||1||<br>
  O man, why do you go out to the households of others?<br>
  You filthy, heartless, lustful donkey! Haven't you heard of the Righteous Judge of Dharma? ||1||Pause||<br>
  The stone of corruption is tied around your neck, and the load of slander is on your head.<br>
  You must cross over the vast open ocean, but you cannot cross over to the other side. ||2||<br>
  You are engrossed in sexual desire, anger, greed and emotional attachment; you have turned your eyes away from the Truth.<br>
  You cannot even raise your head above the water of the vast, impassable sea of Maya. ||3||<br>
  The sun is liberated, and the moon is liberated; the God-realized being is pure and untouched.<br>
  His inner nature is like that of fire, untouched and forever immaculate. ||4||<br>
  When good karma dawns, the wall of doubt is torn down. He lovingly accepts the Guru's Will.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 014</h2></center>
  One who is blessed with the medicine of the GurMantra, the Name of the Lord, O servant Nanak, does not suffer the agonies of reincarnation. ||5||2||<br>
  O man, in this way, you shall cross over to the other side.<br>
  Meditate on your Dear Lord, and be dead to the world; renounce your love of duality. ||Second Pause||2||11||<br>
  Maaroo, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  I have quit searching outside; the Guru has shown me that God is within the home of my own heart.<br>
  I have seen God, fearless, of wondrous beauty; my mind shall never leave Him to go anywhere else. ||1||<br>
  I have found the jewel; I have found the Perfect Lord.<br>
  The invaluable value cannot be obtained; in His Mercy, the Guru bestows it. ||1||Pause||<br>
  The Supreme Lord God is imperceptible and unfathomable; meeting the Holy Saint, I speak the Unspoken Speech.<br>
  The unstruck sound current of the Shabad vibrates and resounds in the Tenth Gate; the Ambrosial Naam trickles down there. ||2||<br>
  I lack nothing; the thirsty desires of my mind are satisfied. The inexhaustible treasure has entered into my being.<br>
  I serve the feet, the feet, the feet of the Guru, and manage the unmanageable. I have found the juice, the sublime essence. ||3||<br>
  Intuitively I come, and intuively I go; my mind intuitively plays.<br>
  Says Nanak, when the Guru drives out doubt, then the soul-bride enters the Mansion of the Lord's Presence. ||4||3||12||<br>
  Maaroo, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  You feel no love for the One who created and embellished you.<br>
  The seed, planted out season, does not germinate; it does not produce flower or fruit. ||1||<br>
  O mind, this is the time to plant the seed of the Name.<br>
  Focus your mind, and cultivate this crop; at the proper time, make this your purpose. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Eradicate the stubbornness and doubt of your mind, and go to the Sanctuary of the True Guru.<br>
  He alone does such deeds, who has such pre-ordained karma. ||2||<br>
  He falls in love with the Lord of the Universe, and his efforts are approved.<br>
  My crop has germinated, and it shall never be used up. ||3||<br>
  I have obtained the priceless wealth, which shall never leave me or go anywhere else.<br>
  Says Nanak, I have found peace; I am satisfied and fulfilled. ||4||4||13||<br>
  Maaroo, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  The egg of doubt has burst; my mind has been enlightened.<br>
  The Guru has shattered the shackles on my feet, and has set me free. ||1||<br>
  My coming and going in reincarnation is ended.<br>
  The boiling cauldron has cooled down; the Guru has blessed me with the cooling, soothing Naam, the Name of the Lord. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Since I joined the Saadh Sangat, the Company of the Holy, those who were eyeing me have left.<br>
  The one who tied me up, has released me; what can the Watchman of Death do to me now? ||2||<br>
  The load of my karma has been removed, and I am now free of karma.<br>
  I have crossed the world-ocean, and reached the other shore; the Guru has blessed me with this Dharma. ||3||<br>
  True is my place, and True is my seat; I have made Truth my life's purpose.<br>
  True is my capital, and True is the merchandise, which Nanak has placed into the home of the heart. ||4||5||14||<br>
  Maaroo, Fifth Mehl:<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 015</h2></center>
  The Pandit, the religious scholar, proclaims the Vedas, but he is slow to act on them.<br>
  Another person on silence sits alone, but his heart is tied in knots of desire.<br>
  Another becomes an Udaasi, a renunciate; he abandons his home and walks out on his family, but his wandering impulses do not leave him. ||1||<br>
  Who can I tell about the state of my soul?<br>
  Where can I find such a person who is liberated, and who can unite me with my God? ||1||Pause||<br>
  Someone may practice intensive meditation, and discipline his body, but his mind still runs around in ten directions.<br>
  The celibate practices celibacy, but his heart is filled with pride.<br>
  The Sannyaasi wanders around at sacred shrines of pilgrimage, but his mindless anger is still within him. ||2||<br>
  The temple dancers tie bells around their ankles to earn their living.<br>
  Others go on fasts, take vows, perform the six rituals and wear religious robes for show.<br>
  Some sing songs and melodies and hymns, but their minds do not sing of the Lord, Har, Har. ||3||<br>
  The Lord's Saints are immaculately pure; they are beyond pleasure and pain, beyond greed and attachment.<br>
  My mind obtains the dust of their feet, when the Lord God shows mercy.<br>
  Says Nanak, I met the Perfect Guru, and then the anxiety of my mind was removed. ||4||<br>
  My Sovereign Lord is the Inner-knower, the Searcher of hearts.<br>
  The Beloved of my soul knows everything; all trivial talk is forgotten. ||1||Second Pause||6||15||<br>
  Maaroo, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  One who has Your Name in his heart is the king of all the hundreds of thousands and millions of beings.<br>
  Those, whom my True Guru has not blessed with Your Name, are poor idiots, who die and are reborn. ||1||<br>
  My True Guru protects and preserves my honor.<br>
  When You come to mind, Lord, then I obtain perfect honor. Forgetting You, I roll in the dust. ||1||Pause||<br>
  The mind's pleasures of love and beauty bring just as many blames and sins.<br>
  The Name of the Lord is the treasure of Emancipation; it is absolute peace and poise. ||2||<br>
  The pleasures of Maya fade away in an instant, like the shade of a passing cloud.<br>
  They alone are dyed in the deep crimson of the Lord's Love, who meet the Guru, and sing the Praises of the Lord, Har, Har. ||3||<br>
  My Lord and Master is lofty and exalted, grand and infinite. The Darbaar of His Court is inaccessible.<br>
  Through the Naam, glorious greatness and respect are obtained; O Nanak, my Lord and Master is my Beloved. ||4||7||16||<br>
  Maaroo, Fifth Mehl, Fourth House:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  The One Universal Creator Lord created the creation.<br>
  He made all the days and the nights.<br>
  The forests, meadows, three worlds, water,<br>
  the four Vedas, the four sources of creation,<br>
  the countries, the continents and all the worlds,<br>
  have all come from the One Word of the Lord. ||1||<br>
  Hey - understand the Creator Lord.<br>
  If you meet the True Guru, then you'll understand. ||1||Pause||<br>
  He formed the expanse of the entire universe from the three gunas, the three qualities.<br>
  People are incarnated in heaven and in hell.<br>
  In egotism, they come and go.<br>
  The mind cannot hold still, even for an instant.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 016</h2></center>
  Without the Guru, there is only pitch darkness.<br>
  Meeting with the True Guru, one is emancipated. ||2||<br>
  All the deeds done in egotism,<br>
  are just chains around the neck.<br>
  Harboring self-conceit and self-interest<br>
  is just like placing chains around one's ankles.<br>
  He alone meets with the Guru, and realizes the One Lord,<br>
  who has such destiny written on his forehead. ||3||<br>
  He alone meets the Lord, who is pleasing to His Mind.<br>
  He alone is deluded, who is deluded by God.<br>
  No one, by himself, is ignorant or wise.<br>
  He alone chants the Naam, whom the Lord inspires to do so.<br>
  You have no end or limitation.<br>
  Servant Nanak is forever a sacrifice to You. ||4||1||17||<br>
  Maaroo, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Maya, the enticer, has enticed the world of the three gunas, the three qualities.<br>
  The false world is engrossed in greed.<br>
  Crying out, "Mine, mine!" they collect possessions, but in the end, they are all deceived. ||1||<br>
  The Lord is fearless, formless and merciful.<br>
  He is the Cherisher of all beings and creatures. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Some collect wealth, and bury it in the ground.<br>
  Some cannot abandon wealth, even in their dreams.<br>
  The king exercises his power, and fills his money-bags, but this fickle companion will not go along with him. ||2||<br>
  Some love this wealth even more than their body and breath of life.<br>
  Some collect it, forsaking their fathers and mothers.<br>
  Some hide it from their children, friends and siblings, but it will not remain with them. ||3||<br>
  Some become hermits, and sit in meditative trances.<br>
  Some are Yogis, celibates, religious scholars and thinkers.<br>
  Some dwell in homes, graveyards, cremation grounds and forests; but Maya still clings to them there. ||4||<br>
  When the Lord and Master releases one from his bonds,<br>
  the Name of the Lord, Har, Har, comes to dwell in his soul.<br>
  In the Saadh Sangat, the Company of the Holy, His humble servants are liberated; O Nanak, they are redeemed and enraptured by the Lord's Glance of Grace. ||5||2||18||<br>
  Maaroo, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Meditate in remembrance on the One Immaculate Lord.<br>
  No one is turned away from Him empty-handed.<br>
  He cherished and preserved you in your mother's womb;<br>
  He blessed you with body and soul, and embellished you.<br>
  Each and every instant, meditate on that Creator Lord.<br>
  Meditating in remembrance on Him, all faults and mistakes are covered.<br>
  Enshrine the Lord's lotus feet deep within the nucleus of your self.<br>
  Save your soul from the waters of corruption.<br>
  Your cries and shrieks shall be ended;<br>
  meditating on the Lord of the Universe, your doubts and fears shall be dispelled.<br>
  Rare is that being, who finds the Saadh Sangat, the Company of the Holy.<br>
  Nanak is a sacrifice, a sacrifice to Him. ||1||<br>
  The Lord's Name is the support of my mind and body.<br>
  Whoever meditates on Him is emancipated. ||1||Pause||<br>
  He believes that the false thing is true.<br>
  The ignorant fool falls in love with it.<br>
  He is intoxicated with the wine of sexual desire, anger and greed;<br>
  he loses this human life in exchance for a mere shell.<br>
  He abandons his own, and loves that of others.<br>
  His mind and body are permeated with the intoxication of Maya.<br>
  His thirsty desires are not quenched, although he indulges in pleasures.<br>
  His hopes are not fulfilled, and all his words are false.<br>
  He comes alone, and he goes alone.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 017</h2></center>
  False is all his talk of me and you.<br>
  The Lord Himself administers the poisonous potion, to mislead and delude.<br>
  O Nanak, the the karma of past actions cannot be erased. ||2||<br>
  Beasts, birds, demons and ghosts<br>
  - in these many ways, the false wander in reincarnation.<br>
  Wherever they go, they cannot remain there.<br>
  They have no place of rest; they rise up again and again and run around.<br>
  Their minds and bodies are filled with immense, expansive desires.<br>
  The poor wretches are cheated by egotism.<br>
  They are filled with countless sins, and are severely punished.<br>
  The extent of this cannot be estimated.<br>
  Forgetting God, they fall into hell.<br>
  There are no mothers there, no siblings, no friends and no spouses.<br>
  Those humble beings, unto whom the Lord and Master becomes Merciful,<br>
  O Nanak, cross over. ||3||<br>
  Rambling and roaming, wandering around, I came to seek the Sanctuary of God.<br>
  He is the Master of the meek, the father and mother of the world.<br>
  The Merciful Lord God is the Destroyer of sorrow and suffering.<br>
  He emancipates whoever He pleases.<br>
  He lifts them up and pulls him out of the deep dark pit.<br>
  Emancipation comes through loving devotional worship.<br>
  The Holy Saint is the very embodiment of the Lord's form.<br>
  He Himself saves us from the great fire.<br>
  By myself, I cannot practice meditation, austerities, penance and self-discipline.<br>
  In the beginning and in the end, God is inaccessible and unfathomable.<br>
  Please bless me with Your Name, Lord; Your slave begs only for this.<br>
  O Nanak, my Lord God is the Giver of the true state of life. ||4||3||19||<br>
  Maaroo, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Why do you try to deceive others, O people of the world? The Fascinating Lord is Merciful to the meek. ||1||<br>
  This is what I have come to know.<br>
  The brave and heroic Guru, the Generous Giver, gives Sanctuary and preserves our honor. ||1||Pause||<br>
  He submits to the Will of His devotees; He is forever and ever the Giver of peace. ||2||<br>
  Please bless me with Your Mercy, that I may meditate on Your Name alone. ||3||<br>
  Nanak, the meek and humble, begs for the Naam, the Name of the Lord; it eradicates duality and doubt. ||4||4||20||<br>
  Maaroo, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  My Lord and Master is utterly powerful.<br>
  I am just His poor servant. ||1||<br>
  My Enticing Beloved is very dear to my mind and my breath of life.<br>
  He blesses me with His gift. ||1||Pause||<br>
  I have seen and tested all.<br>
  There is none other than Him. ||2||<br>
  He sustains and nurtures all beings.<br>
  He was, and shall always be. ||3||<br>
  Please bless me with Your Mercy, O Divine Lord,<br>
  and link Nanak to Your service. ||4||5||21||<br>
  Maaroo, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  The Redeemer of sinners, who carries us across; I am a sacrifice, a sacrifice, a sacrifice, a sacrifice to Him.<br>
  If only I could meet with such a Saint, who would inspire me to meditate on the Lord, Har, Har, Har. ||1||<br>
  No one knows me; I am called Your slave.<br>
  This is my support and sustenance. ||1||Pause||<br>
  You support and cherish all; I am meek and humble - this is my only prayer.<br>
  You alone know Your Way; You are the water, and I am the fish. ||2||<br>
  O Perfect and Expansive Lord and Master, I follow You in love.<br>
  O God, You are pervading all the worlds, solar systems and galaxies. ||3||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 018</h2></center>
  You are eternal and unchanging, imperishable, invisible and infinite, O divine fascinating Lord.<br>
  Please bless Nanak with the gift of the Society of the Saints, and the dust of the feet of Your slaves. ||4||6||22||<br>
  Maaroo, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  The Saints are fulfilled and satisfied;<br>
  they know the Guru's Mantra and the Teachings.<br>
  They cannot even be described;<br>
  they are blessed with the glorious greatness of the Naam, the Name of the Lord. ||1||<br>
  My Beloved is a priceless jewel.<br>
  His Name is unattainable and immeasurable. ||1||Pause||<br>
  One whose mind is satisfied believing in the imperishable Lord God,<br>
  becomes Gurmukh and attains the essence of spiritual wisdom.<br>
  He sees all in his meditation.<br>
  He banishes egotistical pride from his mind. ||2||<br>
  Permanent is the place of those<br>
  who, through the Guru, realize the Mansion of the Lord's Presence.<br>
  Meeting the Guru, they remain awake and aware night and day;<br>
  they are committed to the Lord's service. ||3||<br>
  They are perfectly fulfilled and satisfied,<br>
  intuitively absorbed in Samaadhi.<br>
  The Lord's treasure comes into their hands;<br>
  O Nanak, through the Guru, they attain it. ||4||7||23||<br>
  Maaroo, Fifth Mehl, Sixth House, Du-Padas:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  Abandon all your clever tricks; meet with the Holy, and renounce your egotistical pride.<br>
  Everything else is false; with your tongue, chant the Name of the Lord, Raam, Raam. ||1||<br>
  O my mind, with your ears, listen to the Name of the Lord.<br>
  The sins of your many past lifetimes shall be washed away; then, what can the wretched Messenger of Death do to you? ||1||Pause||<br>
  Pain, poverty and fear shall not afflict you, and you shall find peace and pleasure.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, Nanak speaks; meditation on the Lord is the essence of spiritual wisdom. ||2||1||24||<br>
  Maaroo, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Those who have forgotten the Naam, the Name of the Lord - I have seen them reduced to dust.<br>
  The love of children and friends, and the pleasures of married life are torn apart. ||1||<br>
  O my mind, continually, continuously chant the Naam, the Name of the Lord.<br>
  You shall not burn in the ocean of fire, and your mind and body shall be blessed with peace. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Like the shade of a tree, these things shall pass away, like the clouds blown away by the wind.<br>
  Meeting with the Holy, devotional worship to the Lord is implanted within; O Nanak, only this shall work for you. ||2||2||25||<br>
  Maaroo, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  The perfect, primal Lord is the Giver of peace; He is always with you.<br>
  He does not die, and he does not come or go in reincarnation. He does not perish, and He is not affected by heat or cold. ||1||<br>
  O my mind, be in love with the Naam, the Name of the Lord.<br>
  Within the mind, think of the Lord, Har, Har, the treasure. This is the purest way of life. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Whoever meditates on the merciful compassionate Lord, the Lord of the Universe, is successful.<br>
  He is always new, fresh and young, clever and beautiful; Nanak's mind is pierced through with His Love. ||2||3||26||<br>
  Maaroo, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  While walking and sitting, sleeping and waking, contemplate within your heart the GurMantra.<br>
  Run to the Lord's lotus feet, and join the Saadh Sangat, the Company of the Holy. Cross over the terrifying world-ocean, and reach the other side. ||1||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 019</h2></center>
  O my mind, enshrine the Naam, the Name of the Lord, within your heart.<br>
  Love the Lord, and commit your mind and body to Him; forget everything else. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Soul, mind, body and breath of life belong to God; eliminate your self-conceit.<br>
  Meditate, vibrate on the Lord of the Universe, and all your desires shall be fulfilled; O Nanak, you shall never be defeated. ||2||4||27||<br>
  Maaroo, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Renounce your self-conceit, and the fever shall depart; become the dust of the feet of the Holy.<br>
  He alone receives Your Name, Lord, whom You bless with Your Mercy. ||1||<br>
  O my mind, drink in the Ambrosial Nectar of the Naam, the Name of the Lord.<br>
  Abandon other bland, insipid tastes; become immortal, and live throughout the ages. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Savor the essence of the One and only Naam; love the Naam, focus and attune yourself to the Naam.<br>
  Nanak has made the One Lord his only friend, companion and relative. ||2||5||28||<br>
  Maaroo, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  He nourishes and preserves mortals in the womb of the mother, so that the fiery heat does not hurt them.<br>
  That Lord and Master protects us here. Understand this in your mind. ||1||<br>
  O my mind, take the Support of the Naam, the Name of the Lord.<br>
  Understand the One who created you; the One God is the Cause of causes. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Remember the One Lord in your mind, renounce your clever tricks, and give up all your religious robes.<br>
  Meditating in remembrance forever on the Lord, Har, Har, O Nanak, countless beings have been saved. ||2||6||29||<br>
  Maaroo, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  His Name is the Purifier of sinners; He is the Master of the masterless.<br>
  In the vast and terrifying world-ocean, he is the raft for those who have such destiny inscribed on their foreheads. ||1||<br>
  Without the Naam, the Name of the Lord, huge numbers of companions have drowned.<br>
  Even if someone does not remember the Lord, the Cause of causes, still, the Lord reaches out with His hand, and saves him. ||1||Pause||<br>
  In the Saadh Sangat, the Company of the Holy, chant the Glorious Praises of the Lord, and take the Path of the Ambrosial Name of the Lord.<br>
  Shower me with Your Mercy, O Lord; listening to Your sermon, Nanak lives. ||2||7||30||<br>
  Maaroo, Anjulee ~ With Hands Cupped In Prayer, Fifth Mehl, Seventh House:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  Union and separation are ordained by the Primal Lord God.<br>
  The puppet is made from the five elements.<br>
  By the Command of the Dear Lord King, the soul came and entered into the body. ||1||<br>
  In that place, where the fire rages like an oven,<br>
  in that darkness where the body lies face down<br>
  - there, one remembers his Lord and Master with each and every breath, and then he is rescued. ||2||<br>
  Then, one comes out from within the womb,<br>
  and forgetting his Lord and Master, he attaches his consciousness to the world.<br>
  He comes and goes, and wanders in reincarnation; he cannot remain anywhere. ||3||<br>
  The Merciful Lord Himself emancipates.<br>
  He created and established all beings and creatures.<br>
  Those who depart after having been victorious in this priceless human life - O Nanak, their coming into the world is approved. ||4||1||31||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 020</h2></center>
  Maaroo, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  The One Lord alone is our help and support; neither physician nor friend, nor sister nor brother can be this. ||1||<br>
  His actions alone come to pass; He washes off the filth of sins. Meditate in remembrance on that Supreme Lord. ||2||<br>
  He abides in each and every heart, and dwells in all; His seat and place are eternal. ||3||<br>
  He does not come or go, and He is always with us. His actions are perfect. ||4||<br>
  He is the Savior and the Protector of His devotees.<br>
  The Saints live by meditating on God, the support of the breath of life.<br>
  The Almighty Lord and Master is the Cause of causes; Nanak is a sacrifice to Him. ||5||2||32||<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  Maaroo, Ninth Mehl:<br>
  The Name of the Lord is forever the Giver of peace.<br>
  Meditating in remembrance on it, Ajaamal was saved, and Ganika the prostitute was emancipated. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Dropadi the princess of Panchaala remembered the Lord's Name in the royal court.<br>
  The Lord, the embodiment of mercy, removed her suffering; thus His own glory was increased. ||1||<br>
  That man, who sings the Praise of the Lord, the treasure of mercy, has the help and support of the Lord.<br>
  Says Nanak, I have come to rely on this. I seek the Sanctuary of the Lord. ||2||1||<br>
  Maaroo, Ninth Mehl:<br>
  What should I do now, O mother?<br>
  I have wasted my whole life in sin and corruption; I never remembered the Lord. ||1||Pause||<br>
  When Death places the noose around my neck, then I lose all my senses.<br>
  Now, in this disaster, other than the Name of the Lord, who will be my help and support? ||1||<br>
  That wealth, which he believes to be his own, in an instant, belongs to another.<br>
  Says Nanak, this still really bothers my mind - I never sang the Praises of the Lord. ||2||2||<br>
  Maaroo, Ninth Mehl:<br>
  O my mother, I have not renounced the pride of my mind.<br>
  I have wasted my life intoxicated with Maya; I have not focused myself in meditation on the Lord. ||1||Pause||<br>
  When Death's club falls on my head, then I will be wakened from my sleep.<br>
  But what good will it do to repent at that time? I cannot escape by running away. ||1||<br>
  When this anxiety arises in the heart, then, one comes to love the Guru's feet.<br>
  My life becomes fruitful, O Nanak, only when I am absorbed in the Praises of God. ||2||3||<br>
  Maaroo, Ashtapadees, First Mehl, First House:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  Reciting and listening to the Vedas and the Puraanas, countless wise men have grown weary.<br>
  So many in their various religious robes have grown weary, wandering to the sixty-eight sacred shrines of pilgrimage.<br>
  The True Lord and Master is immaculate and pure. The mind is satisfied only by the One Lord. ||1||<br>
  You are eternal; You do not grow old. All others pass away.<br>
  One who lovingly focuses on the Naam, the source of nectar - his pains are taken away. ||1||Pause||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 021</h2></center>
  Study the Lord's Name, and understand the Lord's Name; follow the Guru's Teachings, and through the Naam, you shall be saved.<br>
  Perfect are the Teachings of the Perfect Guru; contemplate the Perfect Word of the Shabad.<br>
  The Lord's Name is the sixty-eight sacred shrines of pilgrimage, and the Eradicator of sins. ||2||<br>
  The blind ignorant mortal stirs the water and churns the water, wishing to obtain butter.<br>
  Following the Guru's Teachings, one churns the cream, and the treasure of the Ambrosial Naam is obtained.<br>
  The self-willed manmukh is a beast; he does not know the essence of reality that is contained within himself. ||3||<br>
  Dying in egotism and self-conceit, one dies, and dies again, only to be reincarnated over and over again.<br>
  But when he dies in the Word of the Guru's Shabad, then he does not die, ever again.<br>
  When he follows the Guru's Teachings, and enshrines the Lord, the Life of the World, within his mind, he redeems all his generations. ||4||<br>
  The Naam, the Name of the Lord, is the true object, the true commodity.<br>
  The Naam is the only true profit in this world. Follow the Guru's Teachings, and contemplate it.<br>
  To work in the love of duality, brings constant loss in this world. ||5||<br>
  True is one's association, true is one's place, and true is one's hearth and home, when one has the support of the Naam.<br>
  Contemplating the True Word of the Guru's Bani, and the True Word of the Shabad, one becomes content. ||6||<br>
  Enjoying princely pleasures, one shall be destroyed in pain and pleasure.<br>
  Adopting a name of greatness, one strings heavy sins around his neck.<br>
  Mankind cannot give gifts; You alone are the Giver of everything. ||7||<br>
  You are inaccessible and unfathomable; O Lord, You are imperishable and infinite.<br>
  Through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, seeking at the Lord's Door, one finds the treasure of liberation.<br>
  O Nanak, this union is not broken, if one deals in the merchandise of Truth. ||8||1||<br>
  Maaroo, First Mehl:<br>
  The boat is loaded with sin and corruption, and launched into the sea.<br>
  The shore cannot be seen on this side, nor on the shore beyond.<br>
  There are no oars, nor any boatmen, to cross over the terrifying world-ocean. ||1||<br>
  O Baba, the world is caught in the great noose.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, they are saved, contemplating the True Name. ||1||Pause||<br>
  The True Guru is the boat; the Word of the Shabad will carry them across.<br>
  There is neither wind nor fire, neither water nor form there.<br>
  The True Name of the True Lord is there; it carries them across the terrifying world-ocean. ||2||<br>
  The Gurmukhs reach the shore beyond, lovingly focusing on the True Lord.<br>
  Their comings and goings are ended, and their light merges into the Light.<br>
  Following the Guru's Teachings, intuitive peace wells up within them, and they remain merged in the True Lord. ||3||<br>
  The snake may be locked in a basket, but it is still poisonous, and the anger within its mind remains.<br>
  One obtains what is pre-ordained; why does he blame others?<br>
  If one, as Gurmukh, hears and believes in the Name, the charm against poison, his mind becomes content. ||4||<br>
  The crocodile is caught by the hook and line;<br>
  caught in the trap of evil-mindedness, he regrets and repents, again and again.<br>
  He does not understand birth and death; the inscription of one's past actions cannot be erased. ||5||<br>
  Injecting the poison of egotism, the world was created; with the Shabad enshrined within, the poison is eliminated.<br>
  Old age cannot torment one who remains lovingly absorbed in the True Lord.<br>
  He alone is called Jivan-Mikta, liberated while yet alive, from within whom egotism is eradicated. ||6||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 022</h2></center>
  The world is chasing after worldly affairs; caught and bound, it does not understand contemplative meditation.<br>
  The foolish, ignorant, self-willed manmukh has forgotten birth and death.<br>
  Those whom the Guru has protected are saved, contemplating the True Word of the Shabad. ||7||<br>
  In the cage of divine love, the parrot, speaks.<br>
  It pecks at the Truth, and drinks in the Ambrosial Nectar; it flies away, only once.<br>
  Meeting with the Guru, one recognizes his Lord and Master; says Nanak, he finds the gate of liberation. ||8||2||<br>
  Maaroo, First Mehl:<br>
  One who dies in the Word of the Shabad conquers death; otherwise, where can you run?<br>
  Through the Fear of God, fear runs away; His Name is Ambrosial Nectar.<br>
  You alone kill and protect; except for You, there is no place at all. ||1||<br>
  O Baba, I am filthy, shallow and totally without understanding.<br>
  Without the Naam, no one is anything; the Perfect Guru has made my intellect perfect. ||1||Pause||<br>
  I am full of faults, and I have no virtue at all. Without virtues, how can I go home?<br>
  Through the Word of the Shabad, intuitive peace wells up; without good destiny, the wealth is not obtained.<br>
  Those whose minds are not filled with the Naam are bound and gagged, and suffer in pain. ||2||<br>
  Those who have forgotten the Naam - why have they even come into the world?<br>
  Here and hereafter, they do not find any peace; they have loaded their carts with ashes.<br>
  Those who are separated, do not meet with the Lord; they suffer in terrible pain at Death's Door. ||3||<br>
  I do not know what will happen in the world hereafter; I am so confused - please teach me, Lord!<br>
  I am confused; I would fall at the feet of one who shows me the Way.<br>
  Without the Guru, there is no giver at all; His value cannot be described. ||4||<br>
  If I see my friend, then I will embrace Him; I have sent Him the letter of Truth.<br>
  His soul-bride stands waiting expectantly; as Gurmukh, I see Him with my eyes.<br>
  By the Pleasure of Your Will, You abide in my mind, and bless me with Your Glance of Grace. ||5||<br>
  One who is wandering hungry and thirsty - what can he give, and what can anyone ask from him?<br>
  I cannot conceive of any other, who can bless my mind and body with perfection.<br>
  The One who created me takes care of me; He Himself blesses me with glory. ||6||<br>
  In the body-village is my Lord and Master, whose body is ever-new, Innocent and child-like, incomparably playful.<br>
  He is neither a woman, nor a man, nor a bird; the True Lord is so wise and beautiful.<br>
  Whatever pleases Him, happens; You are the lamp, and You are the incense. ||7||<br>
  He hears the songs and tastes the flavors, but these flavors are useless and insipid, and bring only disease to the body.<br>
  One who loves the Truth and speaks the Truth, escapes from the sorrow of separation.<br>
  Nanak does not forget the Naam; whatever happens is by the Lord's Will. ||8||3||<br>
  Maaroo, First Mehl:<br>
  Practice Truth - other greed and attachments are useless.<br>
  The True Lord has fascinated this mind, and my tongue enjoys the taste of Truth.<br>
  Without the Name, there is no juice; the others depart, loaded with poison. ||1||<br>
  I am such a slave of Yours, O my Beloved Lord and Master.<br>
  I walk in harmony with Your Command, O my True, Sweet Beloved. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Night and day, the slave works for his overlord.<br>
  I have sold my mind for the Word of the Guru's Shabad; my mind is comforted and consoled by the Shabad.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 023</h2></center>
  The Perfect Guru is honored and celebrated; He has taken away the pains of my mind. ||2||<br>
  I am the servant and slave of my Master; what glorious greatness of His can I describe?<br>
  The Perfect Master, by the Pleasure of His Will, forgives, and then one practices Truth.<br>
  I am a sacrifice to my Guru, who re-unites the separated ones. ||3||<br>
  The intellect of His servant and slave is noble and true; it is made so by the Guru's intellect.<br>
  The intuition of those who are true is beautiful; the intellect of the self-willed manmukh is insipid.<br>
  My mind and body belong to You, God; from the very beginning, Truth has been my only support. ||4||<br>
  In Truth I sit and stand; I eat and speak the Truth.<br>
  With Truth in my consciousness, I gather the wealth of Truth, and drink in the sublime essence of Truth.<br>
  In the home of Truth, the True Lord protects me; I speak the Words of the Guru's Teachings with love. ||5||<br>
  The self-willed manmukh is very lazy; he is trapped in the wilderness.<br>
  He is drawn to the bait, and continually pecking at it, he is trapped; his link to the Lord is ruined.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, one is liberated, absorbed in the primal trance of Truth. ||6||<br>
  His slave remains continually pierced through with love and affection for God.<br>
  Without the True Lord, the soul of the false, corrupt person is burnt to ashes.<br>
  Abandoning all evil actions, he crosses over in the boat of Truth. ||7||<br>
  Those who have forgotten the Naam have no home, no place of rest.<br>
  The Lord's slave renounces greed and attachment, and obtains the Lord's Name.<br>
  If You forgive him, Lord, then He is united with You; Nanak is a sacrifice. ||8||4||<br>
  Maaroo, First Mehl:<br>
  The Lord's slave renounces his egotistical pride, through the Guru's Fear, intuitively and easily.<br>
  The slave realizes his Lord and Master; glorious is his greatness!<br>
  Meeting with his Lord and Master, he finds peace; His value cannot be desribed. ||1||<br>
  I am the slave and servant of my Lord and Master; all glory is to my Master.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, I am saved, in the Sanctuary of the Lord. ||1||Pause||<br>
  The slave has been given the most excellent task, by the Primal Command of the Master.<br>
  The slave realizes the Hukam of His Command, and submits to His Will forever.<br>
  The Lord King Himself grants forgiveness; how glorious is His greatness! ||2||<br>
  He Himself is True, and everything is True; this is revealed through the Word of the Guru's Shabad.<br>
  He alone serves You, whom You have enjoined to do so.<br>
  Without serving Him, no one finds Him; in duality and doubt, they are ruined. ||3||<br>
  How could we forget Him from our minds? The gifts which he bestows increase day by day.<br>
  Soul and body, all belong to Him; He infused the breath into us.<br>
  If he shows His Mercy, then we serve Him; serving Him, we merge in Truth. ||4||<br>
  He alone is the Lord's slave, who remains dead while yet alive, and eradicates egotism from within.<br>
  His bonds are broken, the fire of his desire is quenched, and he is liberated.<br>
  The treasure of the Naam, the Name of the Lord, is within all, but how rare are those who, as Gurmukh, obtain it. ||5||<br>
  Within the Lord's slave, there is no virtue at all; the Lord's slave is totally unworthy.<br>
  There is no Giver as great as You, Lord; You alone are the Forgiver.<br>
  Your slave obeys the Hukam of Your Command; this is the most excellent action. ||6||<br>
  The Guru is the pool of nectar in the world-ocean; whatever one desires, that fruit is obtained.<br>
  The treasure of the Naam brings immortality; enshrine it in your heart and mind.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 024</h2></center>
  Serving the Guru, eternal peace is obtained, by those whom the Lord inspires to obey the Hukam of His Command. ||7||<br>
  Gold and silver, and all metals, mix with dust in the end<br>
  Without the Name, nothing goes along with you; the True Guru has imparted this understanding.<br>
  O Nanak, those who are attuned to the Naam are immaculate and pure; they remain merged in the Truth. ||8||5||<br>
  Maaroo, First Mehl:<br>
