  The Order is issued, and he cannot remain; the permit to stay has been torn up.<br>
  This mind is tied to its faults; it suffers terrible pain in its body.<br>
  The Perfect Guru forgives all the mistakes of the beggar at His Door. ||1||<br>
  How can he stay here? He must get up and depart. Contemplate the Word of the Shabad, and understand this.<br>
  He alone is united, whom You, O Lord, unite. Such is the Primal Command of the Infinite Lord. ||1||Pause||<br>
  As You keep me, I remain; whatever You give me, I eat.<br>
  As You lead me, I follow, with the Ambrosial Name in my mouth.<br>
  All glorious greatness rests in the hands of my Lord and Master; my mind yearns to unite with You. ||2||<br>
  Why should anyone praise any other created being? That Lord acts and sees.<br>
  The One who created me, abides within my mind; there is no other at all.<br>
  So praise that True Lord, and you shall be blessed with true honor. ||3||<br>
  The Pandit, the religious scholar, reads, but does not reach the Lord; he is totally entangled in worldly affairs.<br>
  He keeps the company of both virtue and vice, tormented by hunger and the Messenger of Death.<br>
  One who is protected by the Perfect Lord, forgets separation and fear. ||4||<br>
  They alone are perfect, O Siblings of Destiny, whose honor is certified.<br>
  Perfect is the intellect of the Perfect Lord. True is His glorious greatness.<br>
  His gifts never run short, although those who receive may grow weary of receiving. ||5||<br>
  Searching the salty sea, one finds the pearl.<br>
  It looks beautiful for a few days, but in the end, it is eaten away by dust.<br>
  If one serves the Guru, the ocean of Truth, the gifts one receives never run short. ||6||<br>
  They alone are pure, who are pleasing to my God; all others are soiled with filth.<br>
  The filthy become pure, when they meet with the Guru, the Philosopher's Stone.<br>
  Who can estimate the value of the color of the true jewel? ||7||<br>
  Wearing religious robes, the Lord is not obtained, nor is He obtained by giving donations at sacred shrines of pilgrimage.<br>
  Go and ask the readers of the Vedas; without faith, the world is cheated.<br>
  O Nanak, he alone values the jewel, who is blessed with the spiritual wisdom of the Perfect Guru. ||8||6||<br>
  Maaroo, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  The self-willed manmukh, in a fit of passion, abandons his home, and is ruined; then, he spies on the homes of others.<br>
  He neglects his household duties, and does not meet with the True Guru; he is caught in the whirlpool of evil-mindedness.<br>
  Wandering in foreign lands and reading scriptures, he grows weary, and his thirsty desires only increase.<br>
  His perishable body does not remember the Word of the Shabad; like a beast, he fills his belly. ||1||<br>
  O Baba, this is the way of life of the Sannyaasi, the renunciate.<br>
  Through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, he is to enshrine love for the One Lord. Imbued with Your Name, Lord, he remains satisfied and fulfilled. ||1||Pause||<br>
  He dyes his robes with saffron dye, and wearing these robes, he goes out begging.<br>
  Tearing his robes, he makes a patched coat, and puts the money in his wallet.<br>
  From house to house he goes begging, and tries to teach the world; but his mind is blind, and so he loses his honor.<br>
  He is deluded by doubt, and does not remember the Word of the Shabad. He loses his life in the gamble. ||2||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 025</h2></center>
  Without the Guru, the fire within is not quenched; and outside, the fire still burns.<br>
  Without serving the Guru, there is no devotional worship. How can anyone, by himself, know the Lord?<br>
  Slandering others, one lives in hell; within him is hazy darkness.<br>
  Wandering to the eixty-eight sacred shrines of pilgrimage, he is ruined. How can the filth of sin be washed away? ||3||<br>
  He sifts through the dust, and applies ashes to his body, but he is searching for the path of Maya's wealth.<br>
  Inwardly and outwardly, he does not know the One Lord; if someone tells him the Truth, he grows angry.<br>
  He reads the scriptures, but tells lies; such is the intellect of one who has no guru.<br>
  Without chanting the Naam, how can he find peace? Without the Name, how can he look good? ||4||<br>
  Some shave their heads, some keep their hair in matted tangles; some keep it in braids, while some keep silent, filled with egotistical pride.<br>
  Their minds waver and wander in ten directions, without loving devotion and enlightenment of the soul.<br>
  They abandon the Ambrosial Nectar, and drink the deadly poison, driven mad by Maya.<br>
  Past actions cannot be erased; without understanding the Hukam of the Lord's Command, they become beasts. ||5||<br>
  With bowl in hand, wearing his patched coat, great desires well up in his mind.<br>
  Abandoning his own wife, he is engrossed in sexual desire; his thoughts are on the wives of others.<br>
  He teaches and preaches, but does not contemplate the Shabad; he is bought and sold on the street.<br>
  With poison within, he pretends to be free of doubt; he is ruined and humiliated by the Messenger of Death. ||6||<br>
  He alone is a Sannyaasi, who serves the True Guru, and removes his self-conceit from within.<br>
  He does not ask for clothes or food; without asking, he accepts whatever he receives.<br>
  He does not speak empty words; he gathers in the wealth of tolerance, and burns away his anger with the Naam.<br>
  Blessed is such a householder, Sannyaasi and Yogi, who focuses his consciousness on the Lord's feet. ||7||<br>
  Amidst hope, the Sannyaasi remains unmoved by hope; he remains lovingly focused on the One Lord.<br>
  He drinks in the sublime essence of the Lord, and so finds peace and tranquility; in the home of his own being, he remains absorbed in the deep trance of meditation.<br>
  His mind does not waver; as Gurmukh, he understands. He restrains it from wandering out.<br>
  Following the Guru's Teachings, he searches the home of his body, and obtains the wealth of the Naam. ||8||<br>
  Brahma, Vishnu and Shiva are exalted, imbued with contemplative meditation on the Naam.<br>
  The sources of creation, speech, the heavens and the underworld, all beings and creatures, are infused with Your Light.<br>
  All comforts and liberation are found in the Naam, and the vibrations of the Guru's Bani; I have enshrined the True Name within my heart.<br>
  Without the Naam, no one is saved; O Nanak, with the Truth, cross over to the other side. ||9||7||<br>
  Maaroo, First Mehl:<br>
  Through the union of mother and father, the fetus is formed. The egg and sperm join together to make the body.<br>
  Upside-down within the womb, it lovingly dwells on the Lord; God provides for it, and gives it nourishment there. ||1||<br>
  How can he cross over the terrifying world-ocean?<br>
  The Gurmukh obtains the Immaculate Naam, the Name of the Lord; the unbearable load of sins is removed. ||1||Pause||<br>
  I have forgotten Your Virtues, Lord; I am insane - what can I do now?<br>
  You are the Merciful Giver, above the heads of all. Day and night, You give gifts, and take care of all. ||2||<br>
  One is born to achieve the four great objectives of life. The spirit has taken up its home in the material world.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 026</h2></center>
  Driven by hunger, it sees the path of Maya's riches; this emotional attachment takes away the treasure of liberation. ||3||<br>
  Weeping and wailing, he does not receive them; he searches here and there, and grows weary.<br>
  Engrossed in sexual desire, anger and egotism, he falls in love with his false relatives. ||4||<br>
  He eats and enjoys, listens and watches, and dresses up to show off in this house of death.<br>
  Without the Word of the Guru's Shabad, he does not undersand himself. Without the Lord's Name, death cannot be avoided. ||5||<br>
  The more attachment and egotism delude and confuse him, the more he cries out, "Mine, mine!", and the more he loses out.<br>
  His body and wealth pass away, and he is torn by skepticism and cynicism; in the end, he regrets and repents, when the dust falls on his face. ||6||<br>
  He grows old, his body and youth waste away, and his throat is plugged with mucous; water flows from his eyes.<br>
  He feet fail him, and his hands shake and tremble; the faithless cynic does not enshrine the Lord in his heart. ||7||<br>
  His intellect fails him, his black hair turns white, and no one wants to keep him in their home.<br>
  Forgetting the Naam, these are the stigmas which stick to him; the Messenger of Death beats him, and drags him to hell. ||8||<br>
  The record of one's past actions cannot be erased; who else is to blame for one's birth and death?<br>
  Without the Guru, life and death are pointless; without the Word of the Guru's Shabad, life just burns away. ||9||<br>
  The pleasures enjoyed in happiness bring ruin; acting in corruption is useless indulgence.<br>
  Forgetting the Naam, and caught by greed, he betrays his own source; the club of the Righteous Judge of Dharma will strike him over the head. ||10||<br>
  The Gurmukhs sing the Glorious Praises of the Lord's Name; the Lord God blesses them with His Glance of Grace.<br>
  Those beings are pure, perfect unlimited and infinite; in this world, they are the embodiment of the Guru, the Lord of the Universe. ||11||<br>
  Meditate in remembrance on the Lord; meditate and contemplate the Guru's Word, and love to associate with the humble servants of the Lord.<br>
  The Lord's humble servants are the embodiment of the Guru; they are supreme and respected in the Court of the Lord. Nanak seeks the dust of the feet of those humble servants of the Lord. ||12||8||<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  Maaroo, Kaafee, First Mehl, Second House:<br>
  The double-minded person comes and goes, and has numerous friends.<br>
  The soul-bride is separated from her Lord, and she has no place of rest; how can she be comforted? ||1||<br>
  My mind is attuned to the Love of my Husband Lord.<br>
  I am devoted, dedicated, a sacrifice to the Lord; if only He would bless me with His Glance of Grace, even for an instant! ||1||Pause||<br>
  I am a rejected bride, abandoned in my parents' home; how can I go to my in-laws now?<br>
  I wear my faults around my neck; without my Husband Lord, I am grieving, and wasting away to death. ||2||<br>
  But if, in my parents' home, I remember my Husband Lord, then I will come to dwell in the home of my in-laws yet.<br>
  The happy soul-brides sleep in peace; they find their Husband Lord, the treasure of virtue. ||3||<br>
  Their blankets and mattresses are made of silk, and so are the clothes on their bodies.<br>
  The Lord rejects the impure soul-brides. Their life-night passes in misery. ||4||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 027</h2></center>
  I have tasted many flavors, and worn many robes,<br>
  but without my Husband Lord, my youth is slipping away uselessly; I am separated from Him, and I cry out in pain. ||5||<br>
  I have heard the True Lord's message, contemplating the Guru.<br>
  True is the home of the True Lord; by His Gracious Grace, I love Him. ||6||<br>
  The spiritual teacher applies the ointment of Truth to his eyes, and sees God, the Seer.<br>
  The Gurmukh comes to know and understand; ego and pride are subdued. ||7||<br>
  O Lord, You are pleased with those who are like Yourself; there are many more like me.<br>
  O Nanak, the Husband does not separate from those who are imbued with Truth. ||8||1||9||<br>
  Maaroo, First Mehl:<br>
  Neither the sisters, nor the sisters-in-law, nor the mothers-in-law, shall remain.<br>
  The true relationship with the Lord cannot be broken; it was established by the Lord, O sister soul-brides. ||1||<br>
  I am a sacrifice to my Guru; I am forever a sacrifice to Him.<br>
  Wandering so far without the Guru, I grew weary; now, the Guru has united me in Union with my Husband Lord. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Aunts, uncles, grandparents and sisters-in-law<br>
  - they all come and go; they cannot remain. They are like boatloads of passengers embarking. ||2||<br>
  Uncles, aunts, and cousins of all sorts, cannot remain.<br>
  The caravans are full, and great crowds of them are loading up at the riverbank. ||3||<br>
  O sister-friends, my Husband Lord is dyed in the color of Truth.<br>
  She who lovingly remembers her True Husband Lord is not separated from Him again. ||4||<br>
  All the seasons are good, in which the soul-bride falls in love with the True Lord.<br>
  That soul-bride, who knows her Husband Lord, sleeps in peace, night and day. ||5||<br>
  At the ferry, the ferryman announces, "O travellers, hurry up and cross over."<br>
  I have seen them crossing over there, on the boat of the True Guru. ||6||<br>
  Some are getting on board, and some have already set out; some are weighed down with their loads.<br>
  Those who deal in Truth, remain with their True Lord God. ||7||<br>
  I am not called good, and I see none who are bad.<br>
  O Nanak, one who conquers and subdues his ego, becomes just like the True Lord. ||8||2||10||<br>
  Maaroo, First Mehl:<br>
  I do not believe that anyone is foolish; I do not believe that anyone is clever.<br>
  Imbued forever with the Love of my Lord and Master, I chant His Name, night and day. ||1||<br>
  O Baba, I am so foolish, but I am a sacrifice to the Name.<br>
  You are the Creator, You are wise and all-seeing. Through Your Name, we are carried across. ||1||Pause||<br>
  The same person is foolish and wise; the same light within has two names.<br>
  The most foolish of the foolish are those who do not believe in the Name. ||2||<br>
  Through the Guru's Gate, the Gurdwara, the Name is obtained. Without the True Guru, it is not received.<br>
  Through the Pleasure of the True Guru's Will, the Name comes to dwell in the mind, and then, night and day, one remains lovingly absorbed in the Lord. ||3||<br>
  In power, pleasures, beauty, wealth and youth, one gambles his life away.<br>
  Bound by the Hukam of God's Command, the dice are thrown; he is just a piece in the game of chess. ||4||<br>
  The world is clever and wise, but it is deluded by doubt, and forgets the Name; the Pandit, the religious scholar, studies the scriptures, but he is still a fool.<br>
  Forgetting the Name, he dwells upon the Vedas; he writes, but he is confused by his poisonous corruption. ||5||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 028</h2></center>
  He is like the crop planted in the salty soil, or the tree growing on the river bank, or the white clothes sprinkled with dirt.<br>
  This world is the house of desire; whoever enters it, is burnt down by egotistical pride. ||6||<br>
  Where are all the kings and their subjects? Those who are immersed in duality are destroyed.<br>
  Says Nanak, these are the steps of the ladder, of the Teachings of the True Guru; only the Unseen Lord shall remain. ||7||3||11||<br>
  Maaroo, Third Mehl, Fifth House, Ashtapadees:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  One whose mind is filled with the Lord's Love,<br>
  is intuitively exalted by the True Word of the Shabad.<br>
  He alone knows the pain of this love; what does anyone else know about its cure? ||1||<br>
  He Himself unites in His Union.<br>
  He Himself inspires us with His Love.<br>
  He alone appreciates the value of Your Love, upon whom You shower Your Grace, O Lord. ||1||Pause||<br>
  One whose spiritual vision is awakened - his doubt is driven out.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, he obtains the supreme status.<br>
  He alone is a Yogi, who understands this way, and contemplates the Word of the Guru's Shabad. ||2||<br>
  By good destiny, the soul-bride is united with her Husband Lord.<br>
  Following the Guru's Teachings, she eradicates her evil-mindedness from within.<br>
  With love, she continually enjoys pleasure with Him; she becomes the beloved of her Husband Lord. ||3||<br>
  Other than the True Guru, there is no physician.<br>
  He Himself is the Immaculate Lord.<br>
  Meeting with the True Guru, evil is conquered, and spiritual wisdom is contemplated. ||4||<br>
  One who is committed to this most sublime Shabad<br>
  becomes Gurmukh, and is rid of thirst and hunger.<br>
  By one's own efforts, nothing can be accomplished; the Lord, in His Mercy, bestows power. ||5||<br>
  The True Guru has revealed the essence of the Shaastras and the Vedas.<br>
  In His Mercy, He has come into the home of my self.<br>
  In the midst of Maya, the Immaculate Lord is known, by those upon whom You bestow Your Grace. ||6||<br>
  One who becomes Gurmukh, obtains the essence of reality;<br>
  he eradictes his self-conceit from within.<br>
  Without the True Guru, all are entangled in worldly affairs; consider this in your mind, and see. ||7||<br>
  Some are deluded by doubt; they strut around egotistically.<br>
  Some, as Gurmukh, subdue their egotism.<br>
  Attuned to the True Word of the Shabad, they remain detached from the world. The other ignorant fools wander, confused and deluded by doubt. ||8||<br>
  Those who have not become Gurmukh, and who have not found the Naam, the Name of the Lord<br>
  - those self-willed manmukhs waste their lives uselessly.<br>
  In the world hereafter, nothing except the Name will be of any assistance; this is understood by contemplating the Guru. ||9||<br>
  The Ambrosial Naam is the Giver of peace forever.<br>
  Throughout the four ages, it is known through the Perfect Guru.<br>
  He alone receives it, unto whom You bestow it; this is the essence of reality which Nanak has realized. ||10||1||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 029</h2></center>
  Maaroo, Fifth Mehl, Third House, Ashtapadees:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  Wandering and roaming through 8.4 million incarnations, you have now been given this human life, so difficult to obtain. ||1||<br>
  You fool! You are attached and clinging to such trivial pleasures!<br>
  The Ambrosial Nectar abides with you, but you are engrossed in sin and corruption. ||1||Pause||<br>
  You have come to trade in gems and jewels, but you have loaded only barren soil. ||2||<br>
  That home within which you live - you have not kept that home in your thoughts. ||3||<br>
  He is immovable, indestructible, the Giver of peace to the soul; and yet you do not sing His Praises, even for an instant. ||4||<br>
  You have forgotten that place where you must go; you have not attached your mind to the Lord, even for an instant. ||5||<br>
  Gazing upon your children, spouse, household and paraphernalia, you are entangled in them. ||6||<br>
  As God links the mortals, so are they linked, and so are the deeds they do. ||7||<br>
  When He becomes Merciful, then the Saadh Sangat, the Company of the Holy, is found; servant Nanak meditates on God. ||8||1||<br>
  Maaroo, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Granting His Grace, He has protected me; I have found the Saadh Sangat, the Company of the Holy.<br>
  My tongue lovingly chants the Lord's Name; this love is so sweet and intense! ||1||<br>
  He is the place of rest for my mind,<br>
  my friend, companion, associate and relative; He is the Inner-knower, the Searcher of hearts. ||1||Pause||<br>
  He created the world-ocean; I seek the Sanctuary of that God.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, I worship and adore God; the Messenger of Death can't say anything to me. ||2||<br>
  Emancipation and liberation are at His Door; He is the treasure in the hearts of the Saints.<br>
  The all-knowing Lord and Master shows us the true way of life; He is our Savior and Protector forever. ||3||<br>
  Pain, suffering and troubles are eradicated, when the Lord abides in the mind.<br>
  Death, hell and the most horrible dwelling of sin and corruption cannot even touch such a person. ||4||<br>
  Wealth, miraculous spiritual powers and the nine treasures come from the Lord, as do the streams of Ambrosial Nectar.<br>
  In the beginning, in the middle, and in the end, He is perfect, lofty, unapproachable and unfathomable. ||5||<br>
  The Siddhas, seekers, angelic beings, silent sages, and the Vedas speak of Him.<br>
  Meditating in remembrance on the Lord and Master, celestial peace is enjoyed; He has no end or limitation. ||6||<br>
  Countless sins are erased in an instant, meditating on the Benevolent Lord within the heart.<br>
  Such a person becomes the purest of the pure, and is blessed with the merits of millions of donations to charity and cleansing baths. ||7||<br>
  God is power, intellect, understanding, the breath of life, wealth, and everything for the Saints.<br>
  May I never forget Him from my mind, even for an instant - this is Nanak's prayer. ||8||2||<br>
  Maaroo, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  The sharp tool cuts down the tree, but it does not feel anger in its mind.<br>
  It serves the purpose of the cutter, and does not blame him at all. ||1||<br>
  O my mind, continually, continuously, meditate on the Lord.<br>
  The Lord of the Universe is merciful, divine and compassionate. Listen - this is the way of the Saints. ||1||Pause||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 030</h2></center>
  He plants his feet in the boat, and then sits down in it; the fatigue of his body is relieved.<br>
  The great ocean does not even affect him; in an instant, he arrives on the other shore. ||2||<br>
  Sandalwood, aloe, and camphor-paste - the earth does not love them.<br>
  But it doesn't mind, if someone digs it up bit by bit, and applies manure and urine to it. ||3||<br>
  High and low, bad and good - the comforting canopy of the sky stretches evenly over all.<br>
  It knows nothing of friend and enemy; all beings are alike to it. ||4||<br>
  Blazing with its dazzling light, the sun rises, and dispels the darkness.<br>
  Touching both the pure and the impure, it harbors no hatred to any. ||5||<br>
  The cool and fragrant wind gently blows upon all places alike.<br>
  Wherever anything is, it touches it there, and does not hesitate a bit. ||6||<br>
  Good or bad, whoever comes close to the fire - his cold is taken away.<br>
  It knows nothing of its own or others'; it is constant in the same quality. ||7||<br>
  Whoever seeks the Sancuary of the feet of the Sublime Lord - his mind is attuned to the Love of the Beloved.<br>
  Constantly singing the Glorious Praises of the Lord of the World, O Nanak, God becomes merciful to us. ||8||3||<br>
  Maaroo, Fifth Mehl, Fourth House, Ashtapadees:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  Moonlight, moonlight - in the courtyard of the mind, let the moonlight of God shine down. ||1||<br>
  Meditation, meditation - sublime is meditation on the Name of the Lord, Har, Har. ||2||<br>
  Renunciation, renunciation - noble is the renunciation of sexual desire, anger and greed. ||3||<br>
  Begging, begging - it is noble to beg for the Lord's Praise from the Guru. ||4||<br>
  Vigils, vigils - sublime is the vigil spent singing the Kirtan of the Lord's Praises. ||5||<br>
  Attachment, attachment - sublime is the attachment of the mind to the Guru's Feet. ||6||<br>
  He alone is blessed with this way of life, upon whose forehead such destiny is recorded. ||7||<br>
  Says Nanak, everything is sublime and noble, for one who enters the Sanctuary of God. ||8||1||4||<br>
  Maaroo, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Please come, O please come into the home of my heart, that I may hear with my ears the Lord's Praises. ||1||Pause||<br>
  With your coming, my soul and body are rejuvenated, and I sing with you the Lord's Praises. ||1||<br>
  By the Grace of the Saint, the Lord dwells within the heart, and the love of duality is eradicated. ||2||<br>
  By the kindness of the devotee, the intellect is enlightened, and pain and evil-mindedness are eradicated. ||3||<br>
  Beholding the Blessed Vision of His Darshan, one is sanctified, and is no longer consigned to the womb of reincarnation. ||4||<br>
  The nine treasures, wealth and miraculous spiritual powers are obtained, by one who is pleasing to Your mind. ||5||<br>
  Without the Saint, I have no place of rest at all; I cannot think of any other place to go. ||6||<br>
  I am unworthy; no one gives me sanctuary. But in the Society of the Saints, I merge in God. ||7||<br>
  Says Nanak, the Guru has revealed this miracle; within my mind, I enjoy the Lord, Har, Har. ||8||2||5||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 031</h2></center>
  Maaroo, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Fruitful is the life, the life of one who hears about the Lord, and chants and meditates on Him; he lives forever. ||1||Pause||<br>
  The real drink is that which satisfies the mind; this drink is the sublime essence of the Ambrosial Naam. ||1||<br>
  The real food is that which will never leave you hungry again; it will leave you contented and satisfied forever. ||2||<br>
  The real clothes are those which protect your honor before the Transcendent Lord, and do not leave you naked ever again. ||3||<br>
  The real enjoyment within the mind is to be absorbed in the sublime essence of the Lord, in the Society of the Saints. ||4||<br>
  Sew devotional worship to the Lord into the mind, without any needle or thread. ||5||<br>
  Imbued and intoxicated with the sublime essence of the Lord, this experience will never wear off again. ||6||<br>
  One is blessed with all treasures, when God, in His Mercy, gives them. ||7||<br>
  O Nanak, service to the Saints beings peace; I drink in the wash water of the feet of the Saints. ||8||3||6||<br>
  Maaroo, Fifth Mehl, Eighth House, Anjulees ~ With Hands Cupped In Prayer:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  The household which is filled with abundance - that household suffers anxiety.<br>
  One whose household has little, wanders around searching for more.<br>
  He alone is happy and at peace, who is liberated from both conditions. ||1||<br>
  Householders and kings fall into hell, along with renunciates and angry men,<br>
  and all those who study and recite the Vedas in so many ways.<br>
  Perfect is the work of that humble servant, who remains unattached while in the body. ||2||<br>
  The mortal sleeps, even while he is awake; he is being plundered by doubt.<br>
  Without the Guru, liberation is not obtained, friend.<br>
  In the Saadh Sangat, the Company of the Holy, the bonds of egotism are released, and one comes to behold the One and only Lord. ||3||<br>
  Doing deeds, one is placed in bondage; but if he does not act, he is slandered.<br>
  Intoxicated with emotional attachment, the mind is afflicted with anxiety.<br>
  One who looks alike upon pleasure and pain, by Guru's Grace, sees the Lord in each and every heart. ||4||<br>
  Within the world, one is afflicted by skepticism;<br>
  he does not know the imperceptible Unspoken Speech of the Lord.<br>
  He alone understands, whom the Lord inspires to understand. The Lord cherishes him as His child. ||5||<br>
  He may try to abandon Maya, but he is not released.<br>
  If he collects things, then his mind is afraid of losing them.<br>
  I wave the fly-brush over that holy person, whose honor is protected in the midst of Maya. ||6||<br>
  He alone is a warrior hero, who remains dead to the world.<br>
  One who runs away will wander in reincarnation.<br>
  Whatever happens, accept that as good. Realize the Hukam of His Command, and your evil-mindedness will be burnt away. ||7||<br>
  Whatever He links us to, to that we are linked.<br>
  He acts, and does, and watches over His Creation.<br>
  You are the Giver of peace, the Perfect Lord of Nanak; as You grant Your blessings, I dwell upon Your Name. ||8||1||7||<br>
  Maaroo, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Beneath the tree, all beings have gathered.<br>
  Some are hot-headed, and some speak very sweetly.<br>
  Sunset has come, and they rise up and depart; their days have run their course and expired. ||1||<br>
  Those who committed sins are sure to be ruined.<br>
  Azraa-eel, the Angel of Death, seizes and tortures them.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 032</h2></center>
  They are consigned to hell by the Creator Lord, and the Accountant calls them to give their account. ||2||<br>
  No brothers or sisters can go with them.<br>
  Leaving behind their property, youth and wealth, they march off.<br>
  They do not know the kind and compassionate Lord; they shall be crushed like sesame seeds in the oil-press. ||3||<br>
  You happily, cheerfully steal the possessions of others,<br>
  but the Lord God is with you, watching and listening.<br>
  Through worldly greed, you have fallen into the pit; you know nothing of the future. ||4||<br>
  You shall be born and born again, and die and die again, only to be reincarnated again.<br>
  You shall suffer terrible punishment, on your way to the land beyond.<br>
  The mortal does not know the One who created him; he is blind, and so he shall suffer. ||5||<br>
  Forgetting the Creator Lord, he is ruined.<br>
  The drama of the world is bad; it brings sadness and then happiness.<br>
  One who does not meet the Saint does not have faith or contentment; he wanders just as he pleases. ||6||<br>
  The Lord Himself stages all this drama. Some, he lifts up, and some he throws into the waves.<br>
  As He makes them dance, so do they dance. Everyone lives their lives according to their past actions. ||7||<br>
  When the Lord and Master grants His Grace, then we meditate on Him.<br>
  In the Society of the Saints, one is not consigned to hell.<br>
  Please bless Nanak with the gift of the Ambrosial Naam, the Name of the Lord; he continually sings the songs of Your Glories. ||8||2||8||12||20||<br>
  Maaroo, Solahas, First Mehl:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  The True Lord is True; there is no other at all.<br>
  He who created, shall in the end destroy.<br>
  As it pleases You, so You keep me, and so I remain; what excuse could I offer to You? ||1||<br>
  You Yourself create, and You Yourself destroy.<br>
  You yourself link each and every person to their tasks.<br>
  You contemplate Yourself, You Yourself make us worthy; You Yourself place us on the Path. ||2||<br>
  You Yourself are all-wise, You Yourself are all-knowing.<br>
  You Yourself created the Universe, and You are pleased.<br>
  You Yourself are the air, water and fire; You Yourself unite in Union. ||3||<br>
  You Yourself are the moon, the sun, the most perfect of the perfect.<br>
  You Yourself are spiritual wisdom, meditation, and the Guru, the Warrior Hero.<br>
  The Messenger of Death, and his noose of death, cannot touch one, who is lovingly focused on You, O True Lord. ||4||<br>
  You Yourself are the male, and You Yourself are the female.<br>
  You Yourself are the chess-board, and You Yourself are the chessman.<br>
  You Yourself staged the drama in the arena of the world, and You Yourself evaluate the players. ||5||<br>
  You Yourself are the bumble bee, the flower, the fruit and the tree.<br>
  You Yourself are the water, the desert, the ocean and the pool.<br>
  You Yourself are the great fish, the tortoise, the Cause of causes; Your form cannot be known. ||6||<br>
  You Yourself are the day, and You Yourself are the night.<br>
  You Yourself are pleased by the Word of the Guru's Bani.<br>
  From the very beginning, and throughout the ages, the unstruck sound current resounds, night and day; in each and every heart, the Word of the Shabad, echoes Your Will. ||7||<br>
  You Yourself are the jewel, incomparably beautiful and priceless.<br>
  You Yourself are the Assessor, the Perfect Weigher.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 033</h2></center>
  You Yourself test and forgive. You Yourself give and take, O Siblings of Destiny. ||8||<br>
  He Himself is the bow, and He Himself is the archer.<br>
  He Himself is all-wise, beautiful and all-knowing.<br>
  He is the speaker, the orator and the listener. He Himself made what is made. ||9||<br>
  Air is the Guru, and water is known to be the father.<br>
  The womb of the great mother earth gives birth to all.<br>
  Night and day are the two nurses, male and female; the world plays in this play. ||10||<br>
  You Yourself are the fish, and You Yourself are the net.<br>
  You Yourself are the cows, and You yourself are their keeper.<br>
  Your Light fills all the beings of the world; they walk according to Your Command, O God. ||11||<br>
  You Yourself are the Yogi, and You Yourself are the enjoyer.<br>
  You Yourself are the reveller; You form the supreme Union.<br>
  You Yourself are speechless, formless and fearless, absorbed in the primal ecstasy of deep meditation. ||12||<br>
  The sources of creation and speech are contained within You, Lord.<br>
  All that is seen, is coming and going.<br>
  They are the true bankers and traders, whom the True Guru has inspired to understand. ||13||<br>
  The Word of the Shabad is understood through the Perfect True Guru.<br>
  The True Lord is overflowing with all powers.<br>
  You are beyond our grasp, and forever independent. You do not have even an iota of greed. ||14||<br>
  Birth and death are meaningless, for those<br>
  who enjoy the sublime celestial essence of the Shabad within their minds.<br>
  He Himself is the Giver of liberation, satisfaction and blessings, to those devotees who love Him in their minds. ||15||<br>
  He Himself is immaculate; by contact with the Guru, spiritual wisdom is obtained.<br>
  Whatever is seen, shall merge into You.<br>
  Nanak, the lowly, begs for charity at Your Door; please, bless him with the glorious greatness of Your Name. ||16||1||<br>
  Maaroo, First Mehl:<br>
  He Himself is the earth, the mythical bull which supports it and the Akaashic ethers.<br>
  The True Lord Himself reveals His Glorious Virtues.<br>
  He Himself is celibate, chaste and contented; He Himself is the Doer of deeds. ||1||<br>
  He who created the creation, beholds what He has created.<br>
  No one can erase the Inscription of the True Lord.<br>
  He Himself is the Doer, the Cause of causes; He Himself is the One who bestows glorious greatness. ||2||<br>
  The five thieves cause the fickle consciousness to waver.<br>
  It looks into the homes of others, but does not search its own home.<br>
  The body-village crumbles into dust; without the Word of the Shabad, one's honor is lost. ||3||<br>
  One who realizes the Lord through the Guru, comprehends the three worlds.<br>
  He subdues his desires, and struggles with his mind.<br>
  Those who serve You, become just like You; O Fearless Lord, You are their best friend from infancy. ||4||<br>
  You Yourself are the heavenly realms, this world and the nether regions of the underworld.<br>
  You Yourself are the embodiment of light, forever young.<br>
  With matted hair, and a horrible, dreadful form, still, You have no form or feature. ||5||<br>
  The Vedas and the Bible do not know the mystery of God.<br>
  He has no mother, father, child or brother.<br>
  He created all the mountains, and levels them again; the Unseen Lord cannot be seen. ||6||<br>
  I have grown weary of making so many friends.<br>
  No one can rid me of my sins and mistakes.<br>
  God is the Supreme Lord and Master of all the angels and mortal beings; blessed with His Love, their fear is dispelled. ||7||<br>
  He puts back on the Path those who have wandered and strayed.<br>
  You Yourself make them stray, and You teach them again.<br>
  I cannot see anything except the Name. Through the Name comes salvation and merit. ||8||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 034</h2></center>
  The Ganges, the Jamunaa where Krishna played, Kaydar Naat'h,<br>
  Benares, Kanchivaram, Puri, Dwaarkaa,<br>
  Ganga Saagar where the Ganges empties into the ocean, Trivaynee where the three rivers come together, and the sixty-eight sacred shrines of pilgrimage, are all merged in the Lord's Being. ||9||<br>
  He Himself is the Siddha, the seeker, in meditative contemplation.<br>
  He Himself is the King and the Council.<br>
  God Himself, the wise Judge, sits on the throne; He takes away doubt, duality and fear. ||10||<br>
  He Himself is the Qazi; He Himself is the Mullah.<br>
  He Himself is infallible; He never makes mistakes.<br>
  He Himself is the Giver of Grace, compassion and honor; He is no one's enemy. ||11||<br>
  Whoever He forgives, He blesses with glorious greatness.<br>
  He is the Giver of all; He does not have even an iota of greed.<br>
  The Immaculate Lord is all pervading, permeating everywhere, both hidden and manifest. ||12||<br>
  How can I praise the inaccessible, infinite Lord?<br>
  The True Creator Lord is the Enemy of ego.<br>
  He unites those whom He blesses with His Grace; uniting them in His Union, they are united. ||13||<br>
  Brahma, Vishnu and Shiva stand at His Door;<br>
  they serve the unseen, infinite Lord.<br>
  Millions of others can be seen crying at His door; I cannot even estimate their numbers. ||14||<br>
  True is the Kirtan of His Praise, and True is the Word of His Bani.<br>
  I can see no other in the Vedas and the Puraanas.<br>
  Truth is my capital; I sing the Glorious Praises of the True Lord. I have no other support at all. ||15||<br>
  In each and every age, the True Lord is, and shall always be.<br>
  Who has not died? Who shall not die?<br>
  Nanak the lowly offers this prayer; see Him within your own self, and lovingly focus on the Lord. ||16||2||<br>
  Maaroo, First Mehl:<br>
  In duality and evil-mindedness, the soul-bride is blind and deaf.<br>
  She wears the dress of sexual desire and anger.<br>
  Her Husband Lord is within the home of her own heart, but she does not know Him; without her Husband Lord, she cannot go to sleep. ||1||<br>
  The great fire of desire blazes within her.<br>
  The self-willed manmukh looks around in the four directions.<br>
  Without serving the True Guru, how can she find peace? Glorious greatness rests in the hands of the True Lord. ||2||<br>
  Eradicating sexual desire, anger and egotism,<br>
  she destroys the five thieves through the Word of the Shabad.<br>
  Taking up the sword of spiritual wisdom, she struggles with her mind, and hope and desire are smoothed over in her mind. ||3||<br>
  From the union of the mother's egg and the father's sperm,<br>
  the form of infinite beauty has been created.<br>
  The blessings of light all come from You; You are the Creator Lord, pervading everywhere. ||4||<br>
  You have created birth and death.<br>
  Why should anyone fear, if they come to understand through the Guru?<br>
  When You, O Merciful Lord, look with Your kindness, then pain and suffering leave the body. ||5||<br>
  One who sits in the home of his own self, eats his own fears.<br>
  He quiets and holds his wandering mind still.<br>
  His heart-lotus blossoms forth in the overflowing green pool, and the Lord of his soul becomes his companion and helper. ||6||<br>
  With their death already ordained, mortals come into this world.<br>
  How can they remain here? They have to go to the world beyond.<br>
  True is the Lord's Command; the true ones dwell in the eternal city. The True Lord blesses them with glorious greatness. ||7||<br>
  He Himself created the whole world.<br>
  The One who made it, assigns the tasks to it.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 035</h2></center>
  I cannot see any other above the True Lord. The True Lord does the appraisal. ||8||<br>
  In this green pasture, the mortal stays only a few days.<br>
  He plays and frolics in utter darkness.<br>
  The jugglers have staged their show, and left, like people mumbling in a dream. ||9||<br>
  They alone are blessed with glorious greatness at the Lord's throne,<br>
  who enshrine the fearless Lord in their minds, and lovingly center themselves on Him.<br>
  In the galaxies and solar systems, nether regions, celestial realms and the three worlds, the Lord is in the primal void of deep absorption. ||10||<br>
  True is the village, and true is the throne,<br>
  of those Gurmukhs who meet with the True Lord, and find peace.<br>
  In Truth, seated upon the true throne, they are blessed with glorious greatness; their egotism is eradicated, along with the calculation of their account. ||11||<br>
  Calculating its account, the soul becomes anxious.<br>
  How can one find peace, through duality and the three gunas - the three qualities?<br>
  The One Lord is immaculate and formless, the Great Giver; through the Perfect Guru, honor is obtained. ||12||<br>
  In each and every age, very rare are those who, as Gurmukh, realize the Lord.<br>
  Their minds are imbued with the True, all-pervading Lord.<br>
  Seeking His Shelter, they find peace, and their minds and bodies are not stained with filth. ||13||<br>
  Their tongues are imbued with the True Lord, the source of nectar;<br>
  abiding with the Lord God, they have no fear or doubt.<br>
  Hearing the Word of the Guru's Bani, their ears are satisfied, and their light merges into the Light. ||14||<br>
  Carefully, carefully, I place my feet upon the ground.<br>
  Wherever I go, I behold Your Sanctuary.<br>
  Whether You grant me pain or pleasure, You are pleasing to my mind. I am in harmony with You. ||15||<br>
  No one is anyone's companion or helper at the very last moment;<br>
  as Gurmukh, I realize You and praise You.<br>
  O Nanak, imbued with the Naam, I am detached; in the home of my own self deep within, I am absorbed in the primal void of deep meditation. ||16||3||<br>
  Maaroo, First Mehl:<br>
  From the very beginning of time, and throughout the ages, You are infinite and incomparable.<br>
  You are my primal, immaculate Lord and Master.<br>
  I contemplate the Way of Yoga, the Way of Union with the True Lord. I am truly absorbed in the primal void of deep meditation. ||1||<br>
  For so many ages, there was only pitch darkness;<br>
  the Creator Lord was absorbed in the primal void.<br>
  There was the True Name, the glorious greatness of the Truth, and the glory of His true throne. ||2||<br>
  In the Golden Age of Truth, Truth and contentment filled the bodies.<br>
  Truth was pervasive, Truth, deep, profound and unfathomable.<br>
  The True Lord appraises the mortals on the Touchstone of Truth, and issues His True Command. ||3||<br>
  The Perfect True Guru is true and contented.<br>
  He alone is a spiritual hero, who believes in the Word of the Guru's Shabad.<br>
  He alone obtains a true seat in the True Court of the Lord, who surrenders to the Command of the Commander. ||4||<br>
  In the Golden Age of Truth, everyone spoke the Truth.<br>
  Truth was pervasive - the Lord was Truth.<br>
  With Truth in their minds and mouths, mortals were rid of doubt and fear. Truth was the friend of the Gurmukhs. ||5||<br>
  In the Silver Age of Traytaa Yoga, one power of Dharma was lost.<br>
  Three feet remained; through duality, one was cut off.<br>
  Those who were Gurmukh spoke the Truth, while the self-willed manmukhs wasted away in vain. ||6||<br>
  The manmukh never succeeds in the Court of the Lord.<br>
  Without the Word of the Shabad, how can one be pleased within?<br>
  In bondage they come, and in bondage they go; they understand and comprehend nothing. ||7||<br>
  In the Brass Age of Dwaapur Yuga, compassion was cut in half.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 036</h2></center>
  Only a few, as Gurmukh, remembered the Lord.<br>
  Dharmic faith, which upholds and supports the earth, had only two feet; Truth was revealed to the Gurmukhs. ||8||<br>
  The kings acted righteously only out of self-interest.<br>
  Tied to hopes of reward, they gave to charities.<br>
  Without the Lord's Name, liberation did not come, although they grew weary of performing rituals. ||9||<br>
  Practicing religious rituals, they sought liberation,<br>
  but the treasure of liberation comes only by praising the Shabad.<br>
  Without the Word of the Guru's Shabad, liberation is not obtained; practicing hypocrisy, they wander around confused. ||10||<br>
  Love and attachment to Maya cannot be abandoned.<br>
  They alone find release, who practice deeds of Truth.<br>
  Day and night, the devotees remain imbued with contemplative meditation; they become just like their Lord and Master. ||11||<br>
  Some chant and practice intensive meditation, and take cleansing baths at sacred shrines of pilgrimage.<br>
  They walk as You will them to walk.<br>
  By stubborn rituals of self-suppression, the Lord is not pleased. No one has ever obtained honor, without the Lord, without the Guru. ||12||<br>
  In the Iron Age, the Dark Age of Kali Yuga, only one power remains.<br>
  Without the Perfect Guru, no one has even described it.<br>
  The self-willed manmukhs have staged the show of falsehood. Without the True Guru, doubt does not depart. ||13||<br>
  The True Guru is the Creator Lord, independent and carefree.<br>
  He does not fear death, and He is not dependent on mortal men.<br>
  Whoever serves Him becomes immortal and imperishable, and will not be tortured by death. ||14||<br>
  The Creator Lord has enshrined Himself within the Guru.<br>
  The Gurmukh saves countless millions.<br>
  The Life of the World is the Great Giver of all beings. The Fearless Lord has no filth at all. ||15||<br>
  Everyone begs from the Guru, God's Treasurer.<br>
  He Himself is the immaculate, unknowable, infinite Lord.<br>
  Nanak speaks the Truth; he begs from God. Please bless me with the Truth, by Your Will. ||16||4||<br>
  Maaroo, First Mehl:<br>
  The True Lord unites with those who are united with the Word of the Shabad.<br>
  When it pleases Him, we intuitively merge with Him.<br>
  The Light of the Transcendent Lord pervades the three worlds; there is no other at all, O Siblings of Destiny. ||1||<br>
  I am His servant; I serve Him.<br>
  He is unknowable and mysterious; He is pleased by the Shabad.<br>
  The Creator is the Benefactor of His devotees. He forgives them - such is His greatness. ||2||<br>
  The True Lord gives and gives; His blessings never run short.<br>
  The false ones receive, and then deny having received.<br>
  They do not understand their origins, they are not pleased with the Truth, and so they wander in duality and doubt. ||3||<br>
  The Gurmukhs remain awake and aware, day and night.<br>
  Following the Guru's Teachings, they know the Love of the True Lord.<br>
  The self-willed manmukhs remain asleep, and are plundered. The Gurmukhs remain safe and sound, O Siblings of Destiny. ||4||<br>
  The false come, and the false go;<br>
  imbued with falsehood, they practice only falsehood.<br>
  Those who are imbued with the Shabad are robed in honor in the Court of the Lord; the Gurmukhs focus their consciousness on Him. ||5||<br>
  The false are cheated, and robbed by the robbers.<br>
  The garden is laid waste, like the rough wilderness.<br>
  Without the Naam, the Name of the Lord, nothing tastes sweet; forgetting the Lord, they suffer in sorrow. ||6||<br>
  Receiving the food of Truth, one is satisfied.<br>
  True is the glorious greatness of the jewel of the Name.<br>
  One who understands his own self, realizes the Lord. His light merges into the Light. ||7||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 037</h2></center>
  Wandering from the Name, he endures beatings.<br>
  Even great cleverness does not dispel doubt.<br>
  The unconscious fool does not remain conscious of the Lord; he putrifies and rots away to death, carrying his heavy load of sin. ||8||<br>
  No one is free of conflict and strife.<br>
  Show me anyone who is, and I will praise him.<br>
  Dedicating mind and body to God, one meets the Lord, the Life of the World, and becomes just like Him. ||9||<br>
  No one knows the state and extent of God.<br>
  Whoever calls himself great, will be eaten by his greatness.<br>
  There is no lack of gifts of our True Lord and Master. He created all. ||10||<br>
  Great is the glorious greatness of the independent Lord.<br>
  He Himself created, and gives sustanance to all.<br>
  The Merciful Lord is not far away; the Great Giver spontaneously unites with Himself, by His Will. ||11||<br>
  Some are sad, and some are afflicted with disease.<br>
  Whatever God does, He does by Himself.<br>
  Through loving devotion, and the Perfect Teachings of the Guru, the unstruck sound current of the Shabad is realized. ||12||<br>
  Some wander and roam around, hungry and naked.<br>
  Some act in stubbornness and die, but do not know the value of God.<br>
  They do not know the difference between good and bad; this is understood only through the practice of the Word of the Shabad. ||13||<br>
  Some bathe at sacred shrines and refuse to eat.<br>
  Some torment their bodies in burning fire.<br>
  Without the Lord's Name, liberation is not obtained; how can anyone cross over? ||14||<br>
  Abandoning the Guru's Teachings, some wander in the wilderness.<br>
  The self-willed manmukhs are destitute; they do not meditate on the Lord.<br>
  They are ruined, destroyed and drowned from practicing falsehood; death is the enemy of the false. ||15||<br>
  By the Hukam of the Lord's Command, they come, and by the Hukam of His Command, they go.<br>
  One who realizes His Hukam, merges in the True Lord.<br>
  O Nanak, he merges in the True Lord, and his mind is pleased with the Lord. The Gurmukhs do His work. ||16||5||<br>
  Maaroo, First Mehl:<br>
  He Himself is the Creator Lord, the Architect of Destiny.<br>
  He evaluates those whom He Himself has created.<br>
  He Himself is the True Guru, and He Himself is the servant; He Himself created the Universe. ||1||<br>
  He is near at hand, not far away.<br>
  The Gurmukhs understand Him; perfect are those humble beings.<br>
  Associating with them night and day is profitable. This is the glorious greatness of associating with the Guru. ||2||<br>
  Throughout the ages, Your Saints are holy and sublime, O God.<br>
  They sing the Glorious Praises of the Lord, savoring it with their tongues.<br>
  They chant His Praises, and their pain and poverty are taken away; they are not afraid of anyone else. ||3||<br>
  They remain awake and aware, and do not appear to sleep.<br>
  They serve up Truth, and so save their companions and relatives.<br>
  They are not stained with the filth of sins; they are immaculate and pure, and remain absorbed in loving devotional worship. ||4||<br>
  O humble servants of the Lord, understand the Word of the Guru's Bani.<br>
  This youth, breath and body shall pass away.<br>
  O mortal, you shall die today or tomorrow; chant, and meditate on the Lord within your heart. ||5||<br>
  O mortal, abandon falsehood and your worthless ways.<br>
  Death viciously kills the false beings.<br>
  The faithless cynic is ruined through falsehood and his egotistical mind.On the path of duality, he rots away and decomposes. ||6||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 038</h2></center>
  Abandon slander and envy of others.<br>
  Reading and studying, they burn, and do not find tranquility.<br>
  Joining the Sat Sangat, the True Congregation, praise the Naam, the Name of the Lord. The Lord, the Supreme Soul, shall be your helper and companion. ||7||<br>
  Abandon sexual desire, anger and wickedness.<br>
  Abandon your involvement in egotistical affairs and conflicts.<br>
  If you seek the Sanctuary of the True Guru, then you shall be saved. In this way you shall cross over the terrifying world-ocean, O Siblings of Destiny. ||8||<br>
  In the hereafter, you shall have to cross over the fiery river of poisonous flames.<br>
  No one else will be there; your soul shall be all alone.<br>
  The ocean of fire spits out waves of searing flames; the self-willed manmukhs fall into it, and are roasted there. ||9||<br>
  Liberation comes from the Guru; He grants this blessing by the Pleasure of His Will.<br>
  He alone knows the way, who obtains it.<br>
  So ask one who has obtained it, O Siblings of Destiny. Serve the True Guru, and find peace. ||10||<br>
  Without the Guru, he dies entangled in sin and corruption.<br>
  The Messenger of Death smashes his head and humiliates him.<br>
  The slanderous person is not freed of his bonds; he is drowned, slandering others. ||11||<br>
  So speak the Truth, and realize the Lord deep within.<br>
  He is not far away; look, and see Him.<br>
  No obstacles shall block your way; become Gurmukh, and cross over to the other side. This is the way to cross over the terrifying world-ocean. ||12||<br>
  The Naam, the Name of the Lord, abides deep within the body.<br>
  The Creator Lord is eternal and imperishable.<br>
  The soul does not die, and it cannot be killed; God creates and watches over all. Through the Word of the Shabad, His Will is manifest. ||13||<br>
  He is immaculate, and has no darkness.<br>
  The True Lord Himself sits upon His throne.<br>
  The faithless cynics are bound and gagged, and forced to wander in reincarnation. They die, and are reborn, and continue coming and going. ||14||<br>
  The Guru's servants are the Beloveds of the True Guru.<br>
  Contemplating the Shabad, they sit upon His throne.<br>
  They realize the essence of reality, and know the state of their inner being. This is the true glorious greatness of those who join the Sat Sangat. ||15||<br>
  He Himself saves His humble servant, and saves his ancestors as well.<br>
  His companions are liberated; He carries them across.<br>
  Nanak is the servant and slave of that Gurmukh who lovingly focuses his consciousness on the Lord. ||16||6||<br>
  Maaroo, First Mehl:<br>
  For many ages, only darkness prevailed;<br>
  the infinite, endless Lord was absorbed in the primal void.<br>
  He sat alone and unaffected in absolute darkness; the world of conflict did not exist. ||1||<br>
  Thirty-six ages passed like this.<br>
  He causes all to happen by the Pleasure of His Will.<br>
  No rival of His can be seen. He Himself is infinite and endless. ||2||<br>
  God is hidden throughout the four ages - understand this well.<br>
  He pervades each and every heart, and is contained within the belly.<br>
  The One and Only Lord prevails throughout the ages. How rare are those who contemplate the Guru, and understand this. ||3||<br>
  From the union of the sperm and the egg, the body was formed.<br>
  From the union of air, water and fire, the living being is made.<br>
  He Himself plays joyfully in the mansion of the body; all the rest is just attachment to Maya's expanse. ||4||<br>
  Within the mother's womb, upside-down, the mortal meditated on God.<br>
  The Inner-knower, the Searcher of hearts, knows everything.<br>
  With each and every breath, he contemplated the True Name, deep within himself, within the womb. ||5||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 039</h2></center>
  He came into the world to obtain the four great blessings.<br>
  He came to dwell in the home of the Shiva and Shakti, energy and matter.<br>
  But he forgot the One Lord, and he has lost the game. The blind person forgets the Naam, the Name of the Lord. ||6||<br>
  The child dies in his childish games.<br>
  They cry and mourn, saying that he was such a playful child.<br>
  The Lord who owns him has taken him back. Those who weep and mourn are mistaken. ||7||<br>
  What can they do, if he dies in his youth?<br>
  They cry out, "His is mine, he is mine!"<br>
  They cry for the sake of Maya, and are ruined; their lives in this world are cursed. ||8||<br>
  Their black hair eventually turns grey.<br>
  Without the Name, they lose their wealth, and then leave.<br>
  They are evil-minded and blind - they are totally ruined; they are plundered, and cry out in pain. ||9||<br>
  One who understands himself, does not cry.<br>
  When he meets the True Guru, then he understands.<br>
  Without the Guru, the heavy, hard doors are not opened. Obtaining the Word of the Shabad, one is emancipated. ||10||<br>
  The body grows old, and is beaten out of shape.<br>
  But he does not meditate on the Lord, His only friend, even at the end.<br>
  Forgetting the Naam, the Name of the Lord, he departs with his face blackened. The false are humiliated in the Court of the Lord. ||11||<br>
  Forgetting the Naam, the false ones depart.<br>
  Coming and going, dust falls on their heads.<br>
  The soul-bride finds no home in her in-laws' home, the world hereafter; she suffers in agony in this world of her parents' home. ||12||<br>
  She eats, dresses and plays joyfully,<br>
  but without loving devotional worship of the Lord, she dies uselessly.<br>
  One who does not distinguish between good and evil, is beaten by the Messenger of Death; how can anyone escape this? ||13||<br>
  One who realizes what he has to possess, and what he has to abandon,<br>
  associating with the Guru, comes to know the Word of the Shabad, within the home of his own self.<br>
  Do not call anyone else bad; follow this way of life. Those who are true are judged to be genuine by the True Lord. ||14||<br>
  Without Truth, no one succeeds in the Court of the Lord.<br>
  Through the True Shabad, one is robed in honor.<br>
  He forgives those with whom He is pleased; they silence their egotism and pride. ||15||<br>
  One who realizes the Hukam of God's Command, by the Grace of the Guru,<br>
  comes to know the lifestyle of the ages.<br>
  O Nanak, chant the Naam, and cross over to the other side. The True Lord will carry you across. ||16||1||7||<br>
  Maaroo, First Mehl:<br>
  I have no other friend like the Lord.<br>
  He gave me body and mind, and infused consciousness into my being.<br>
  He cherishes and cares for all beings; He is deep within, the wise, all-knowing Lord. ||1||<br>
  The Guru is the sacred pool, and I am His beloved swan.<br>
  In the ocean, there are so many jewels and rubies.<br>
  The Lord's Praises are pearls, gems and diamonds. Singing His Praises, my mind and body are drenched with His Love. ||2||<br>
  The Lord is inaccessible, inscrutable, unfathomable and unattached.<br>
  The Lord's limits cannot be found; the Guru is the Lord of the World.<br>
  Through the Teachings of the True Guru, the Lord carries us across to the other side. He unites in His Union those who are colored by His Love. ||3||<br>
  Without the True Guru, how can anyone be liberated?<br>
  He has been the Friend of the Lord, from the very beginning of time, and all throughout the ages.<br>
  By His Grace, He grants liberation in His Court; He forgives them for their sins. ||4||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 040</h2></center>
  The True Guru, the Giver, grants liberation;<br>
  all diseases are eradicated, and one is blessed with the Ambrosial Nectar.<br>
  Death, the tax collector, does not impose any tax on one whose inner fire has been put out, whose heart is cool and tranquil. ||5||<br>
  The body has developed a great love for the soul-swan.<br>
  He is a Yogi, and she is a beautiful woman.<br>
  Day and night, he enjoys her with delight, and then he arises and departs without consulting her. ||6||<br>
  Creating the Universe, God remains diffused throughout it.<br>
  In the wind, water and fire, He vibrates and resounds.<br>
  The mind wavers, keeping company with evil passions; one obtains the rewards of his own actions. ||7||<br>
  Forgetting the Naam, one suffers the misery of his evil ways.<br>
  When the order to depart is issued, how can he remain here?<br>
  He falls into the pit of hell, and suffers like a fish out of water. ||8||<br>
  The faithless cynic has to endure 8.4 million hellish incarnations.<br>
  As he acts, so does he suffer.<br>
  Without the True Guru, there is no liberation. Bound and gagged by his own actions, he is helpless. ||9||<br>
  This path is very narrow, like the sharp edge of a sword.<br>
  When his account is read, he shall be crushed like the sesame seed in the mill.<br>
  Mother, father, spouse and child - none is anyone's friend in the end. Without the Lord's Love, no one is liberated. ||10||<br>
  You may have many friends and companions in the world,<br>
  but without the Guru, the Transcendent Lord Incarnate, there is no one at all.<br>
  Service to the Guru is the way to liberation. Night and day, sing the Kirtan of the Lord's Praises. ||11||<br>
  Abandon falsehood, and pursue the Truth,<br>
  and you shall obtain the fruits of your desires.<br>
  Very few are those who trade in the merchandise of Truth. Those who deal in it, obtain the true profit. ||12||<br>
  Depart with the merchandise of the Name of the Lord, Har, Har,<br>
  and you shall intuitively obtain the Blessed Vision of His Darshan, in the Mansion of His Presence.<br>
  The Gurmukhs search for Him and find Him; they are the perfect humble beings. In this way, they see Him, who looks upon all alike. ||13||<br>
  God is endless; following the Guru's Teachings, some find Him.<br>
  Through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, they instruct their minds.<br>
  Accept as True, Perfectly True, the Word of the True Guru's Bani. In this way, you shall merge in the Lord, the Supreme Soul. ||14||<br>
  Naarad and Saraswati are Your servants.<br>
  Your servants are the greatest of the great, throughout the three worlds.<br>
  Your creative power permeates all; You are the Great Giver of all. You created the whole creation. ||15||<br>
  Some serve at Your Door, and their sufferings are dispelled.<br>
  They are robed with honor in the Court of the Lord, and emancipated by the True Guru.<br>
  The True Guru breaks the bonds of egotism, and restrains the fickle consciousness. ||16||<br>
  Meet the True Guru, and search for the way,<br>
  by which you may find God, and not have to answer for your account.<br>
  Subdue your egotism, and serve the Guru; O servant Nanak, you shall be drenched with the Lord's Love. ||17||2||8||<br>
  Maaroo, First Mehl:<br>
  My Lord is the Destroyer of demons.<br>
  My Beloved Lord is pervading each and every heart.<br>
  The unseen Lord is always with us, but He is not seen at all. The Gurmukh contemplates the record. ||1||<br>
  The Holy Gurmukh seeks Your Sanctuary.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 041</h2></center>
  God grants His Grace, and carries him across to the other side.<br>
  The ocean is very deep, filled with fiery water; the Guru, the True Guru, carries us across to the other side. ||2||<br>
  The blind, self-willed manmukh does not understand.<br>
  He comes and goes in reincarnation, dying, and dying again.<br>
  The primal inscription of destiny cannot be erased. The spiritually blind suffer terribly at Death's door. ||3||<br>
  Some come and go, and do not find a home in their own heart.<br>
  Bound by their past actions, they commit sins.<br>
  The blind ones have no understanding, no wisdom; they are trapped and ruined by greed and egotism. ||4||<br>
  Without her Husband Lord, what good are the soul-bride's decorations?<br>
  She has forgotten her Lord and Master, and is infatuated with another's husband.<br>
  Just as no one knows who is the father of the prostitute's son, such are the worthless, useless deeds that are done. ||5||<br>
  The ghost, in the body-cage, suffers all sorts of afflictions.<br>
  Those who are blind to spiritual wisdom, putrefy in hell.<br>
  The Righteous Judge of Dharma collects the balance due on the account, of those who forget the Name of the Lord. ||6||<br>
  The scorching sun blazes with flames of poison.<br>
  The self-willed manmukh is dishonored, a beast, a demon.<br>
  Trapped by hope and desire, he practices falsehood, and is afflicted by the terrible disease of corruption. ||7||<br>
  He carries the heavy load of sins on his forehead and head.<br>
  How can he cross the terrifying world-ocean?<br>
  From the very beginning of time, and throughout the ages, the True Guru has been the boat; through the Lord's Name, He carries us across. ||8||<br>
  The love of one's children and spouse is so sweet in this world.<br>
  The expansive expanse of the Universe is attachment to Maya.<br>
  The True Guru snaps the noose of Death, for that Gurmukh who contemplates the essence of reality. ||9||<br>
  Cheated by falsehood, the self-willed manmukh walks along many paths;<br>
  he may be highly educated, but he burns in the fire.<br>
  The Guru is the Great Giver of the Ambrosial Naam, the Name of the Lord. Chanting the Naam, sublime peace is obtained. ||10||<br>
  The True Guru, in His Mercy, implants Truth within.<br>
  All suffering is eradicated, and one is placed on the Path.<br>
  Not even a thorn ever pierces the foot of one who has the True Guru as his Protector. ||11||<br>
  Dust mixes with dust, when the body wastes away.<br>
  The self-willed manmukh is like a stone slab, which is impervious to water.<br>
  He cries out and weeps and wails; he is reincarnated into heaven and then hell. ||12||<br>
  They live with the poisonous snake of Maya.<br>
  This duality has ruined so many homes.<br>
  Without the True Guru, love does not well up. Imbued with devotional worship, the soul is satisfied. ||13||<br>
  The faithless cynics chase after Maya.<br>
  Forgetting the Naam, how can they find peace?<br>
  In the three qualities, they are destroyed; they cannot cross over to the other side. ||14||<br>
  The false are called pigs and dogs.<br>
  They bark themselves to death; they bark and bark and howl in fear.<br>
  False in mind and body, they practice falsehood; through their evil-mindedness, they lose out in the Court of the Lord. ||15||<br>
  Meeting the True Guru, the mind is stabilized.<br>
  One who seeks His Sanctuary is blessed with the Lord's Name.<br>
  They are given the priceless wealth of the Lord's Name; singing His Praises, they are His beloveds in His court. ||16||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 042</h2></center>
  In the Sanctuary of the Holy, chant the Lord's Name.<br>
  Through the True Guru's Teachings, one comes to know His state and extent.<br>
  Nanak: chant the Name of the Lord, Har, Har, O my mind; the Lord, the Uniter, shall unite you with Himself. ||17||3||9||<br>
  Maaroo, First Mehl:<br>
  Remain in your own home, O my foolish and ignorant mind.<br>
  Meditate on the Lord - concentrate deep within your being and meditate on Him.<br>
  Renounce your greed, and merge with the infinite Lord. In this way, you shall find the door of liberation. ||1||<br>
  If you forget Him, the Messenger of Death will catch sight of you.<br>
  All peace will be gone, and you will suffer in pain in the world hereafter.<br>
  Chant the Name of the Lord as Gurmukh, O my soul; this is the supreme essence of contemplation. ||2||<br>
  Chant the Name of the Lord, Har, Har, the sweetest essence.<br>
  As Gurmukh, see the essence of the Lord deep within.<br>
  Day and night, remain imbued with the Lord's Love. This is the essence of all chanting, deep meditation and self-discipline. ||3||<br>
  Speak the Guru's Word, and the Name of the Lord.<br>
  In the Society of the Saints, search for this essence.<br>
  Follow the Guru's Teachings - seek and find the home of your own self, and you shall never be consigned to the womb of reincarnation again. ||4||<br>
  Bathe at the sacred shrine of Truth, and sing the Glorious Praises of the Lord.<br>
  Reflect upon the essence of reality, and lovingly focus your consciousness on the Lord.<br>
  At the very last moment, the Messenger of Death will not be able to touch you, if you chant the Name of the Beloved Lord. ||5||<br>
  The True Guru, the Primal Being, the Great Giver, is all-knowing.<br>
  Whoever has Truth within himself, merges in the Word of the Shabad.<br>
  One whom the True Guru unites in Union, is rid of the overpowering fear of death. ||6||<br>
  The body is formed from the union of the five elements.<br>
  Know that the Lord's jewel is within it.<br>
  The soul is the Lord, and the Lord is the soul; contemplating the Shabad, the Lord is found. ||7||<br>
  Abide in truth and contentment, O humble Siblings of Destiny.<br>
  Hold tight to compassion and the Sanctuary of the True Guru.<br>
  Know your soul, and know the Supreme Soul; associating with the Guru, you shall be emancipated. ||8||<br>
  The faithless cynics are stuck in falsehood and deceit.<br>
  Day and night, they slander many others.<br>
  Without meditative remembrance, they come and then go, and are cast into the hellish womb of reincarnation. ||9||<br>
  The faithless cynic is not rid of his fear of death.<br>
  The Messenger of Death's club is never taken away.<br>
  He has to answer to the Righteous Judge of Dharma for the account of his actions; the egotistical being carries the unbearable load. ||10||<br>
  Tell me: without the Guru, what faithless cynic has been saved?<br>
  Acting egotistically, he falls into the terrifying world-ocean.<br>
  Without the Guru, no one is saved; meditating on the Lord, they are carried across to the other side. ||11||<br>
  No one can erase the Guru's blessings.<br>
  The Lord carries across those whom He forgives.<br>
  The pains of birth and death do not even approach those whose minds are filled with God, the infinite and endless. ||12||<br>
  Those who forget the Guru come and go in reincarnation.<br>
  They are born, only to die again, and continue committing sins.<br>
  The unconscious, foolish, faithless cynic does not remember the Lord; but when he is stricken with pain, then he cries out for the Lord. ||13||<br>
  Pleasure and pain are the consequences of the actions of past lives.<br>
  The Giver, who blesses us with these - He alone knows.<br>
  So who can you blame, O mortal being? The hardships you suffer are from your own actions. ||14||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 043</h2></center>
  Practicing egotism and possessiveness, you have come into the world.<br>
  Hope and desire bind you and lead you on.<br>
  Indulging in egotism and self-conceit, what will you be able to carry with you, except the load of ashes from poison and corruption? ||15||<br>
  Worship the Lord in devotion, O humble Siblings of Destiny.<br>
  Speak the Unspoken Speech, and the mind will merge back into the Mind.<br>
  Restrain your restless mind within its own home, and the Lord, the Destroyer, shall destroy your pain. ||16||<br>
  I seek the support of the Perfect Guru, the Lord.<br>
  The Gurmukh loves the Lord; the Gurmukh realizes the Lord.<br>
  O Nanak, through the Lord's Name, the intellect is exalted; granting His forgiveness, the Lord carries him across to the other side. ||17||4||10||<br>
  Maaroo, First Mehl:<br>
  O Divine Guru, I have entered Your Sanctuary.<br>
  You are the Almighty Lord, the Merciful Lord.<br>
  No one knows Your wondrous plays; You are the perfect Architect of Destiny. ||1||<br>
  From the very beginning of time, and throughout the ages, You cherish and sustain Your beings.<br>
  You are in each and every heart, O Merciful Lord of incomparable beauty.<br>
  As You will, You cause all to walk; everyone acts according to Your Command. ||2||<br>
  Deep within the nucleus of all, is the Light of the Life of the World.<br>
  The Lord enjoys the hearts of all, and drinks in their essence.<br>
  He Himself gives, and He himself takes; He is the generous father of the beings of the three worlds. ||3||<br>
  Creating the world, He has set His play into motion.<br>
  He placed the soul in the body of air, water and fire.<br>
  The body-village has nine gates; the Tenth Gate remains hidden. ||4||<br>
  There are four horrible rivers of fire.<br>
  How rare is that Gurmukh who understands this, and through the Word of the Shabad, remains unattached.<br>
  The faithless cynics are drowned and burnt through their evil-mindedness. The Guru saves those who are imbued with the Love of the Lord. ||5||<br>
  Water, fire, air, earth and ether<br>
  - in that house of the five elements, they dwell.<br>
  Those who remain imbued with the Word of the True Guru's Shabad, renounce Maya, egotism and doubt. ||6||<br>
  This mind is drenched with the Shabad, and satisfied.<br>
  Without the Name, what support can anyone have?<br>
  The temple of the body is being plundered by the thieves within, but this faithless cynic does not even recognize these demons. ||7||<br>
  They are argumentative demons, terrifying goblins.<br>
  These demons stir up conflict and strife.<br>
  Without awareness of the Shabad, one comes and goes in reincarnation; he loses his honor in this coming and going. ||8||<br>
  The body of the false person is just a pile of barren dirt.<br>
  Without the Name, what honor can you have?<br>
  Bound and gagged throughout the four ages, there is no liberation; the Messenger of Death keeps such a person under his gaze. ||9||<br>
  At Death's door, he is tied up and punished;<br>
  such a sinner does not obtain salvation.<br>
  He cries out in pain, like the fish pierced by the hook. ||10||<br>
  The faithless cynic is caught in the noose all alone.<br>
  The miserable spiritually blind person is caught in the power of Death.<br>
  Without the Lord's Name, liberation is not known. He shall waste away, today or tomorrow. ||11||<br>
  Other than the True Guru, no one is your friend.<br>
  Here and hereafter, God is the Savior.<br>
  He grants His Grace, and bestows the Lord's Name. He merges with Him, like water with water. ||12||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 044</h2></center>
  The Guru instructs His wandering Sikhs;<br>
  if they go astray, He sets them on the right path.<br>
  So serve the Guru, forever, day and night; He is the Destroyer of pain - He is with you as your companion. ||13||<br>
  O mortal being, what devotional worship have you performed to the Guru?<br>
  Even Brahma, Indra and Shiva do not know it.<br>
  Tell me, how can the unknowable True Guru be known? He alone attains this realization, whom the Lord forgives. ||14||<br>
  One who has love within, obtains the Blessed Vision of His Darshan.<br>
  One who enshrines love for the Word of the Guru's Bani, meets with Him.<br>
  Day and night, the Gurmukh sees the immaculate Divine Light everywhere; this lamp illuminates his heart. ||15||<br>
  The food of spiritual wisdom is the supremely sweet essence.<br>
  Whoever tastes it, sees the Blessed Vision of the Lord's Darshan.<br>
  Beholding His Darshan, the unattached one meets the Lord; subduing the mind's desires, he merges into the Lord. ||16||<br>
  Those who serve the True Guru are supreme and famous.<br>
  Deep within each and every heart, they recognize God.<br>
  Please bless Nanak with the Lord's Praises, and the Sangat, the Congregation of the Lord's humble servants; through the True Guru, they know their Lord God. ||17||5||11||<br>
  Maaroo, First Mehl:<br>
  The True Lord is the Creator of the Universe.<br>
  He established and contemplates the worldly sphere.<br>
  He Himself created the creation, and beholds it; He is True and independent. ||1||<br>
  He created the beings of different kinds.<br>
  The two travellers have set out in two directions.<br>
  Without the Perfect Guru, no one is liberated. Chanting the True Name, one profits. ||2||<br>
  The self-willed manmukhs read and study, but they do not know the way.<br>
  They do not understand the Naam, the Name of the Lord; they wander, deluded by doubt.<br>
  They take bribes, and give false testimony; the noose of evil-mindedness is around their necks. ||3||<br>
  They read the Simritees, the Shaastras and the Puraanas;<br>
  they argue and debate, but do not know the essence of reality.<br>
  Without the Perfect Guru, the essence of reality is not obtained. The true and pure beings walk the Path of Truth. ||4||<br>
  All praise God and listen, and listen and speak.<br>
  He Himself is wise, and He Himself judges the Truth.<br>
  Those whom God blesses with His Glance of Grace become Gurmukh, and praise the Word of the Shabad. ||5||<br>
  Many listen and listen, and speak the Guru's Bani.<br>
  Listening and speaking, no one knows His limits.<br>
  He alone is wise, unto whom the unseen Lord reveals Himself; he speaks the Unspoken Speech. ||6||<br>
  At birth, the congratulations pour in;<br>
  the ignorant sing songs of joy.<br>
  Whoever is born, is sure to die, according to the destiny of past deeds inscribed upon his head by the Sovereign Lord King. ||7||<br>
  Union and separation were created by my God.<br>
  Creating the Universe, He gave it pain and pleasure.<br>
  The Gurmukhs remain unaffected by pain and pleasure; they wear the armor of humility. ||8||<br>
  The noble people are traders in Truth.<br>
  They purchase the true merchandise, contemplating the Guru.<br>
  One who has the wealth of the true commodity in his lap, is blessed with the rapture of the True Shabad. ||9||<br>
  The false dealings lead only to loss.<br>
  The trades of the Gurmukh are pleasing to God.<br>
  His stock is safe, and his capital is safe and sound. The noose of Death is cut away from around his neck. ||10||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 045</h2></center>
  Everyone speaks as they please.<br>
  The self-willed manmukh, in duality, does not know how to speak.<br>
  The blind person has a blind and deaf intellect; coming and going in reincarnation, he suffers in pain. ||11||<br>
  In pain he is born, and in pain he dies.<br>
  His pain is not relieved, without seeking the Sanctuary of the Guru.<br>
  In pain he is created, and in pain he perishes. What has he brought with himself? And what will he take away? ||12||<br>
  True are the actions of those who are under the Guru's influence.<br>
  They do not come and go in reincarnation, and they are not subject to the laws of Death.<br>
  Whoever abandons the branches, and clings to the true root, enjoys true ecstasy within his mind. ||13||<br>
  Death cannot strike down the people of the Lord.<br>
  They do not see pain on the most difficult path.<br>
  Deep within the nucleus of their hearts, they worship and adore the Lord's Name; there is nothing else at all for them. ||14||<br>
  There is no end to the Lord's sermon and Praise.<br>
  As it pleases You, I remain under Your Will.<br>
  I am embellished with robes of honor in the Court of the Lord, by the Order of the True King. ||15||<br>
  How can I chant Your uncounted glories?<br>
  Even the greatest of the great do not know Your limits.<br>
  Please bless Nanak with the Truth, and preserve his honor; You are the supreme emperor above the heads of kings. ||16||6||12||<br>
  Maaroo, First Mehl, Dakhanee:<br>
  Deep within the body-village is the fortress.<br>
  The dwelling of the True Lord is within the city of the Tenth Gate.<br>
  This place is permanent and forever immaculate. He Himself created it. ||1||<br>
  Within the fortress are balconies and bazaars.<br>
  He Himself takes care of His merchandise.<br>
  The hard and heavy doors of the Tenth Gate are closed and locked. Through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, they are thrown open. ||2||<br>
  Within the fortress is the cave, the home of the self.<br>
  He established the nine gates of this house, by His Command and His Will.<br>
  In the Tenth Gate, the Primal Lord, the unknowable and infinite dwells; the unseen Lord reveals Himself. ||3||<br>
  Within the body of air, water and fire, the One Lord dwells.<br>
  He Himself stages His wondrous dramas and plays.<br>
  By His Grace, water puts out the burning fire; He Himself stores it up in the watery ocean. ||4||<br>
  Creating the earth, He established it as the home of Dharma.<br>
  Creating and destroying, He remains unattached.<br>
  He stages the play of the breath everywhere. Withdrawing His power, He lets the beings crumble. ||5||<br>
  Your gardener is the vast vegetation of nature.<br>
  The wind blowing around is the chauree, the fly-brush, waving over You.<br>
