  The Lord placed the two lamps, the sun and the moon; the sun merges in the house of the moon. ||6||<br>
  The five birds do not fly wild.<br>
  The tree of life is fruitful, bearing the fruit of Ambrosial Nectar.<br>
  The Gurmukh intuitively sings the Glorious Praises of the Lord; he eats the food of the Lord's sublime essence. ||7||<br>
  The dazzling light glitters, although neither the moon nor the stars are shining;<br>
  neither the sun's rays nor the lightning flashes across the sky.<br>
  I describe the indescribable state, which has no sign, where the all-pervading Lord is still pleasing to the mind. ||8||<br>
  The rays of Divine Light have spread out their brilliant radiance.<br>
  Having created the creation, the Merciful Lord Himself gazes upon it.<br>
  The sweet, melodious, unstruck sound current vibrates continuously in the home of the fearless Lord. ||9||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 046</h2></center>
  When the unstruck sound current resounds, doubt and fear run away.<br>
  God is all-pervading, giving shade to all.<br>
  All belong to You; to the Gurmukhs, You are known. Singing Your Praises, they look beautiful in Your Court. ||10||<br>
  He is the Primal Lord, immaculate and pure.<br>
  I know of no other at all.<br>
  The One Universal Creator Lord dwells within, and is pleasing to the mind of those who banishe egotism and pride. ||11||<br>
  I drink in the Ambrosial Nectar, given by the True Guru.<br>
  I do not know any other second or third.<br>
  He is the One, Unique, Infinite and Endless Lord; He evaluates all beings and places some in His treasury. ||12||<br>
  Spiritual wisdom and meditation on the True Lord are deep and profound.<br>
  No one knows Your expanse.<br>
  All that are, beg from You; You are attained only by Your Grace. ||13||<br>
  You hold karma and Dharma in Your hands, O True Lord.<br>
  O Independent Lord, Your treasures are inexhaustible.<br>
  You are forever kind and compassionate, God. You unite in Your Union. ||14||<br>
  You Yourself see, and cause Yourself to be seen.<br>
  You Yourself establish, and You Yourself disestablish.<br>
  The Creator Himself unites and separates; He Himself kills and rejuvenates. ||15||<br>
  As much as there is, is contained within You.<br>
  You gaze upon Your creation, sitting within Your royal palace.<br>
  Nanak offers this true prayer; gazing upon the Blessed Vision of the Lord's Darshan, I have found peace. ||16||1||13||<br>
  Maaroo, First Mehl:<br>
  If I am pleasing to You, Lord, then I obtain the Blessed Vision of Your Darshan.<br>
  In loving devotional worship, O True Lord, I sing Your Glorious Praises.<br>
  By Your Will, O Creator Lord, You have become pleasing to me, and so sweet to my tongue. ||1||<br>
  The devotees look beautiful in the Darbaar, the Court of God.<br>
  Your slaves, Lord, are liberated.<br>
  Eradicating self-conceit, they are attuned to Your Love; night and day, they meditate on the Naam, the Name of the Lord. ||2||<br>
  Shiva, Brahma, gods and goddesses,<br>
  Indra, ascetics and silent sages serve You.<br>
  Celibates, givers of charity and the many forest-dwellers have not found the Lord's limits. ||3||<br>
  No one knows You, unless You let them know You.<br>
  Whatever is done, is by Your Will.<br>
  You created the 8.4 million species of beings; by Your Will, they draw their breath. ||4||<br>
  Whatever is pleasing to Your Will, undoubtedly comes to pass.<br>
  The self-willed manmukh shows off, and comes to grief.<br>
  Forgetting the Name, he finds no place of rest; coming and going in reincarnation, he suffers in pain. ||5||<br>
  Pure is the body, and immaculate is the swan-soul;<br>
  within it is the immaculate essence of the Naam.<br>
  Such a being drinks in all his pains like Ambrosial Nectar; he never suffers sorrow again. ||6||<br>
  For his excessive indulgences, he receives only pain;<br>
  from his enjoyments, he contracts diseases, and in the end, he wastes away.<br>
  His pleasure can never erase his pain; without accepting the Lord's Will, he wanders lost and confused. ||7||<br>
  Without spiritual wisdom, they all just wander around.<br>
  The True Lord is pervading and permeating everywhere, lovingly engaged.<br>
  The Fearless Lord is known through the Shabad, the Word of the True Guru; one's light merges into the Light. ||8||<br>
  He is the eternal, unchanging, immeasurable Lord.<br>
  In an instant, He destroys, ang then reconstructs.<br>
  He has no form or shape, no limit or value. Pierced by the Shabad, one is satisfied. ||9||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 047</h2></center>
  I am the slave of Your slaves, O my Beloved.<br>
  The seekers of Truth and goodness contemplate You.<br>
  Whoever believes in the Name, wins; He Himself implants Truth within. ||10||<br>
  The Truest of the True has the Truth is His lap.<br>
  The True Lord is pleased with those who love the Shabad.<br>
  Exerting His power, the Lord has established Truth throughout the three worlds; with Truth He is pleased. ||11||<br>
  Everyone calls Him the greatest of the great.<br>
  Without the Guru, no one understands Him.<br>
  The True Lord is pleased with those who merge in Truth; they are not separated again, and they do not suffer. ||12||<br>
  Separated from the Primal Lord, they loudly weep and wail.<br>
  They die and die, only to be reborn, when their time has passed.<br>
  He blesses those whom He forgives with glorious greatness; united with Him, they do not regret or repent. ||13 |<br>
  | He Himself is the Creator, and He Himself is the Enjoyer.<br>
  He Himself is satisfied, and He Himself is liberated.<br>
  The Lord of liberation Himself grants liberation; He eradicates possessiveness and attachment. ||14||<br>
  I consider Your gifts to be the most wonderful gifts.<br>
  You are the Cause of causes, Almighty Infinite Lord.<br>
  Creating the creation, You gaze upon what You have created; You cause all to do their deeds. ||15||<br>
  They alone sing Your Glorious Praises, who are pleasing to You, O True Lord.<br>
  They issue forth from You, and merge again into You.<br>
  Nanak offers this true prayer; meeting with the True Lord, peace is obtained. ||16||2||14||<br>
  Maaroo, First Mehl:<br>
  For endless eons, there was only utter darkness.<br>
  There was no earth or sky; there was only the infinite Command of His Hukam.<br>
  There was no day or night, no moon or sun; God sat in primal, profound Samaadhi. ||1||<br>
  There were no sources of creation or powers of speech, no air or water.<br>
  There was no creation or destruction, no coming or going.<br>
  There were no continents, nether regions, seven seas, rivers or flowing water. ||2||<br>
  There were no heavenly realms, earth or nether regions of the underworld.<br>
  There was no heaven or hell, no death or time.<br>
  There was no hell or heaven, no birth or death, no coming or going in reincarnation. ||3||<br>
  There was no Brahma, Vishnu or Shiva.<br>
  No one was seen, except the One Lord.<br>
  There was no female or male, no social class or caste of birth; no one experienced pain or pleasure. ||4||<br>
  There were no people of celibacy or charity; no one lived in the forests.<br>
  There were no Siddhas or seekers, no one living in peace.<br>
  There were no Yogis, no wandering pilgrims, no religious robes; no one called himself the master. ||5||<br>
  There was no chanting or meditation, no self-discipline, fasting or worship.<br>
  No one spoke or talked in duality.<br>
  He created Himself, and rejoiced; He evaluates Himself. ||6||<br>
  There was no purification, no self-restraint, no malas of basil seeds.<br>
  There were no Gopis, no Krishna, no cows or cowherds.<br>
  There were no tantras, no mantras and no hypocrisy; no one played the flute. ||7||<br>
  There was no karma, no Dharma, no buzzing fly of Maya.<br>
  Social class and birth were not seen with any eyes.<br>
  There was no noose of attachment, no death inscribed upon the forehead; no one meditated on anything. ||8||<br>
  There was no slander, no seed, no soul and no life.<br>
  There was no Gorakh and no Maachhindra.<br>
  There was no spiritual wisdom or meditation, no ancestry or creation, no reckoning of accounts. ||9||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 048</h2></center>
  There were no castes or social classes, no religious robes, no Brahmin or Kh'shaatriya.<br>
  There were no demi-gods or temples, no cows or Gaayatri prayer.<br>
  There were no burnt offerings, no ceremonial feasts, no cleansing rituals at sacred shrines of pilgrimage; no one worshipped in adoration. ||10||<br>
  There was no Mullah, there was no Qazi.<br>
  There was no Shaykh, or pilgrims to Mecca.<br>
  There was no king or subjects, and no worldly egotism; no one spoke of himself. ||11||<br>
  There was no love or devotion, no Shiva or Shakti - no energy or matter.<br>
  There were no friends or companions, no semen or blood.<br>
  He Himself is the banker, and He Himself is the merchant. Such is the Pleasure of the Will of the True Lord. ||12||<br>
  There were no Vedas, Korans or Bibles, no Simritees or Shaastras.<br>
  There was no recitation of the Puraanas, no sunrise or sunset.<br>
  The Unfathomable Lord Himself was the speaker and the preacher; the unseen Lord Himself saw everything. ||13||<br>
  When He so willed, He created the world.<br>
  Without any supporting power, He sustained the universe.<br>
  He created Brahma, Vishnu and Shiva; He fostered enticement and attachment to Maya. ||14||<br>
  How rare is that person who listens to the Word of the Guru's Shabad.<br>
  He created the creation, and watches over it; the Hukam of His Command is over all.<br>
  He formed the planets, solar systems and nether regions, and brought what was hidden to manifestation. ||15||<br>
  No one knows His limits.<br>
  This understanding comes from the Perfect Guru.<br>
  O Nanak, those who are attuned to the Truth are wonderstruck; singing His Glorious Praises, they are filled with wonder. ||16||3||15||<br>
  Maaroo, First Mehl:<br>
  He Himself created the creation, remaining unattached.<br>
  The Merciful Lord has established His True Home.<br>
  Binding together air, water and fire, He created the fortress of the body. ||1||<br>
  The Creator established the nine gates.<br>
  In the Tenth Gate, is the dwelling of the infinite, unseen Lord.<br>
  The seven seas are overflowing with the Ambrosial Water; the Gurmukhs are not stained with filth. ||2||<br>
  The lamps of the sun and the moon fill all with light.<br>
  Creating them, He beholds His own glorious greatness.<br>
  The Giver of peace is forever the embodiment of Light; from the True Lord, glory is obtained. ||3||<br>
  Within the fortress are the stores and markets; the business is transacted there.<br>
  The Supreme Merchant weighs with the perfect weights.<br>
  He Himself buys the jewel, and He Himself appraises its value. ||4||<br>
  The Appraiser appraises its value.<br>
  The Independent Lord is overflowing with His treasures.<br>
  He holds all powers, He is all-pervading; how few are those who, as Gurmukh, understand this. ||5||<br>
  When He bestows His Glance of Grace, one meets the Perfect Guru.<br>
  The tyrannical Messenger of Death cannot strike him then.<br>
  He blossoms forth like the lotus flower in the water; he blossoms forth in joyful meditation. ||6||<br>
  He Himself rains down the Ambrosial Stream of jewels, diamonds, and rubies of priceless value.<br>
  When they meet the True Guru, then they find the Perfect Lord; they obtain the treasure of Love. ||7||<br>
  Whoever receives the priceless treasure of Love<br>
  - his weight never decreases; he has perfect weight.<br>
  The trader of Truth becomes true, and obtains the merchandise. ||8||<br>
  How rare are those who obtain the true merchandise.<br>
  Meeting the Perfect True Guru, one meets with the Lord.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 049</h2></center>
  One who becomes Gurmukh realizes the Hukam of His command; surrendering to His Command, one merges in the Lord. ||9||<br>
  By His Command we come, and by His command we merge into Him again.<br>
  By His Command, the world was formed.<br>
  By His Command, the heavens, this world and the nether regions were created; by His Command, His Power supports them. ||10||<br>
  The Hukam of His Command is the mythical bull which supports the burden of the earth on its head.<br>
  By His Hukam, air, water and fire came into being.<br>
  By His Hukam, one dwells in the house of matter and energy - Shiva and Shakti. By His Hukam, He plays His plays. ||11||<br>
  By the Hukam of His command, the sky is spread above.<br>
  By His Hukam, His creatures dwell in the water, on the land and throughout the three worlds.<br>
  By His Hukam, we draw our breath and receive our food; by His Hukam, He watches over us, and inspires us to see. ||12||<br>
  By His Hukam, He created His ten incarnations,<br>
  and the uncounted and infinite gods and devils.<br>
  Whoever obeys the Hukam of His Command, is robed with honor in the Court of the Lord; united with the Truth, He merges in the Lord. ||13||<br>
  By the Hukam of His Command, the thirty-six ages passed.<br>
  By His Hukam, the Siddhas and seekers contemplate Him.<br>
  The Lord Himself has brought all under His control. Whoever He forgives, is liberated. ||14||<br>
  In the strong fortress of the body with its beautiful doors, is the king, with his special assistants and ministers.<br>
  Those gripped by falsehood and greed do not dwell in the celestial home; engrossed in greed and sin, they come to regret and repent. ||15||<br>
  Truth and contentment govern this body-village.<br>
  Chastity, truth and self-control are in the Sanctuary of the Lord.<br>
  O Nanak, one intuitively meets the Lord, the Life of the World; the Word of the Guru's Shabad brings honor. ||16||4||16||<br>
  Maaroo, First Mehl:<br>
  In the Primal Void, the Infinite Lord assumed His Power.<br>
  He Himself is unattached, infinite and incomparable.<br>
  He Himself exercised His Creative Power, and He gazes upon His creation; from the Primal Void, He formed the Void. ||1||<br>
  From this Primal Void, He fashioned air and water.<br>
  He created the universe, and the king in the fortress of the body.<br>
  Your Light pervades fire, water and souls; Your Power rests in the Primal Void. ||2||<br>
  From this Primal Void, Brahma, Vishnu and Shiva issued forth.<br>
  This Primal Void is pervasive throughout all the ages.<br>
  That humble being who contemplates this state is perfect; meeting with him, doubt is dispelled. ||3||<br>
  From this Primal Void, the seven seas were established.<br>
  The One who created them, Himself contemplates them.<br>
  That human being who becomes Gurmukh, who bathes in the pool of Truth, is not cast into the womb of reincarnation again. ||4||<br>
  From this Primal Void, came the moon, the sun and the earth.<br>
  His Light pervades all the three worlds.<br>
  The Lord of this Primal Void is unseen, infinite and immaculate; He is absorbed in the Primal Trance of Deep Meditation. ||5||<br>
  From this Primal Void, the earth and the Akaashic Ethers were created.<br>
  He supports them without any visible support, by exercising His True Power.<br>
  He fashioned the three worlds, and the rope of Maya; He Himself creates and destroys. ||6||<br>
  From this Primal Void, came the four sources of creation, and the power of speech.<br>
  They were created from the Void, and they will merge into the Void.<br>
  The Supreme Creator created the play of Nature; through the Word of His Shabad, He stages His Wondrous Show. ||7||<br>
  From this Primal Void, He made both night and day;<br>
  creation and destruction, pleasure and pain.<br>
  The Gurmukh is immortal, untouched by pleasure and pain. He obtains the home of his own inner being. ||8||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 050</h2></center>
  The Saam Veda, the Rig Veda, the Jujar Veda and the At'harva Veda<br>
  form the mouth of Brahma; they speak of the three gunas, the three qualities of Maya.<br>
  None of them can describe His worth. We speak as He inspires us to speak. ||9||<br>
  From the Primal Void, He created the seven nether regions.<br>
  From the Primal Void, He established this world to lovingly dwell upon Him.<br>
  The Infinite Lord Himself created the creation. Everyone acts as You make them act, Lord. ||10||<br>
  Your Power is diffused through the three gunas: raajas, taamas and satva.<br>
  Through egotism, they suffer the pains of birth and death.<br>
  Those blessed by His Grace become Gurmukh; they attain the fourth state, and are liberated. ||11||<br>
  From the Primal Void, the ten incarnations welled up.<br>
  Creating the Universe, He made the expanse.<br>
  He fashioned the demi-gods and demons, the heavenly heralds and celestial musicians; everyone acts according to their past karma. ||12||<br>
  The Gurmukh understands, and does not suffer the disease.<br>
  How rare are those who understand this ladder of the Guru.<br>
  Throughout the ages, they are dedicated to liberation, and so they become liberated; thus they are honored. ||13||<br>
  From the Primal Void, the five elements became manifest.<br>
  They joined to form the body, which engages in actions.<br>
  Both bad and good are written on the forehead, the seeds of vice and virtue. ||14||<br>
  The True Guru, the Primal Being, is sublime and detached.<br>
  Attuned to the Word of the Shabad, He is intoxicated with the sublime essence of the Lord.<br>
  Riches, intellect, miraculous spiritual powers and spiritual wisdom are obtained from the Guru; through perfect destiny, they are received. ||15||<br>
  This mind is so in love with Maya.<br>
  Only a few are spiritually wise enough to understand and know this.<br>
  In hope and desire, egotism and skepticism, the greedy man acts falsely. ||16||<br>
  From the True Guru, contemplative meditation is obtained.<br>
  And then, one dwells with the True Lord in His celestial home, the Primal State of Absorption in Deepest Samaadhi.<br>
  O Nanak, the immaculate sound current of the Naad, and the Music of the Shabad resound; one merges into the True Name of the Lord. ||17||5||17||<br>
  Maaroo, First Mehl:<br>
  Wherever I look, I see the Lord, merciful to the meek.<br>
  God is compassionate; He does not come or go in reincarnation.<br>
  He pervades all beings in His mysterious way; the Sovereign Lord remains detached. ||1||<br>
  The world is a reflection of Him; He has no father or mother.<br>
  He has not acquired any sister or brother.<br>
  There is no creation or destruction for Him; He has no ancestry or social status. The Ageless Lord is pleasing to my mind. ||2||<br>
  You are the Deathless Primal Being. Death does not hover over Your head.<br>
  You are the unseen inaccessible and detached Primal Lord.<br>
  You are true and content; the Word of Your Shabad is cool and soothing. Through it, we are lovingly, intuitively attuned to You. ||3||<br>
  The three qualities are pervasive; the Lord dwells in His home, the fourth state.<br>
  He has made death and birth into a bite of food.<br>
  The immaculate Light is the Life of the whole world. The Guru reveals the unstruck melody of the Shabad. ||4||<br>
  Sublime and good are those humble Saints, the Beloveds of the Lord.<br>
  They are intoxicated with the sublime essence of the Lord, and are carried across to the other side.<br>
  Nanak is the dust of the Society of the Saints; by Guru's Grace, he finds the Lord. ||5||<br>
  You are the Inner-knower, the Searcher of hearts. All beings belong to You.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 051</h2></center>
  You are the Great Giver; I am Your slave.<br>
  Please be merciful and bless me with Your Ambrosial Naam, and the jewel, the lamp of the Guru's spiritual wisdom. ||6||<br>
  From the union of the five elements, this body was made.<br>
  Finding the Lord, the Supreme Soul, peace is established.<br>
  The good karma of past actions brings fruitful rewards, and man is blessed with the jewel of the Lord's Name. ||7||<br>
  His mind does not feel any hunger or thirst.<br>
  He knows the Immaculate Lord to be everywhere, in each and every heart.<br>
  Imbued with the Lord's Ambrosial essence, he becomes a pure, detached renunciate; he is lovingly absorbed in the Guru's Teachings. ||8||<br>
  Whoever does the deeds of the soul, day and night,<br>
  sees the immaculate Divine Light deep within.<br>
  Enraptured with the delightful essence of the Shabad, the source of nectar, my tongue plays the sweet music of the flute. ||9||<br>
  He alone plays the sweet music of this flute,<br>
  who knows the three worlds.<br>
  O Nanak, know this, through the Guru's Teachings, and lovingly focus yourself on the Lord's Name. ||10||<br>
  Rare are those beings in this world,<br>
  who contemplate the Word of the Guru's Shabad, and remain detached.<br>
  They save themselves, and save all their associates and ancestors; fruitful is their birth and coming into this world. ||11||<br>
  He alone knows the home of his own heart, and the door to the temple,<br>
  who obtains perfect understanding from the Guru.<br>
  In the body-fortress is the palace; God is the True Master of this Palace. The True Lord established His True Throne there. ||12||<br>
  The fourteen realms and the two lamps are the witnesses.<br>
  The Lord's servants, the self-elect, do not taste the poison of corruption.<br>
  Deep within, is the priceless, incomparable commodity; meeting with the Guru, the wealth of the Lord is obtained. ||13||<br>
  He alone sits on the throne, who is worthy of the throne.<br>
  Following the Guru's Teachings, he subdues the five demons, and becomes the Lord's foot soldier.<br>
  He has existed from the very beginning of time and throughout the ages; He exists here and now, and will always exist. Meditating on Him, skepticism and doubt are dispelled. ||14||<br>
  The Lord of the Throne is greeted and worshipped day and night.<br>
  This true glorious greatness comes to those who love the Guru's Teachings.<br>
  O Nanak, meditate on the Lord, and swim across the river; they find the Lord, their best friend, in the end. ||15||1||18||<br>
  Maaroo, First Mehl:<br>
  Gather in the wealth of the Lord, O humble Siblings of Destiny.<br>
  Serve the True Guru, and remain in His Sanctuary.<br>
  This wealth cannot be stolen; the celestial melody of the Shabad wells up and keeps us awake and aware. ||1||<br>
  You are the One Universal Creator, the Immaculate King.<br>
  You Yourself arrange and resolve the affairs of Your humble servant.<br>
  You are immortal, immovable, infinite and priceless; O Lord, Your place is beautiful and eternal. ||2||<br>
  In the body-village, the most sublime place,<br>
  the supremely noble people dwell.<br>
  Above them is the Immaculate Lord, the One Universal Creator; they are lovingly absorbed in the profound, primal state of Samaadhi. ||3||<br>
  There are nine gates to the body-village;<br>
  the Creator Lord fashioned them for each and every person.<br>
  Within the Tenth Gate, dwells the Primal Lord, detached and unequalled. The unknowable reveals Himself. ||4||<br>
  The Primal Lord cannot be held to account; True is His Celestial Court.<br>
  The Hukam of His Command is in effect; True is His Insignia.<br>
  O Nanak, search and examine your own home, and you shall find the Supreme Soul, and the Name of the Lord. ||5||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 052</h2></center>
  The Primal Lord is everywhere, immaculate and all-knowing.<br>
  He administers justice, and is absorbed in the spiritual wisdom of the Guru.<br>
  He seizes sexual desire and anger by their necks, and kills them; He eradicates egotism and greed. ||6||<br>
  In the True Place, the Formless Lord abides.<br>
  Whoever understands his own self, contemplates the Word of the Shabad.<br>
  He comes to abide deep within the True Mansion of His Presence, and his comings and goings are ended. ||7||<br>
  His mind does not waver, and he is not buffeted by the winds of desire.<br>
  Such a Yogi vibrates the unstruck sound current of the Shabad.<br>
  God Himself plays the pure music of the Panch Shabad, the five primal sounds to hear. ||8||<br>
  In the Fear of God, in detachment, one intuitively merges into the Lord.<br>
  Renouncing egotism, he is imbued with the unstruck sound current.<br>
  With the ointment of enlightenment, the Immaculate Lord is known; the Immaculate Lord King is pervading everywhere. ||9||<br>
  God is eternal and imperishable; He is the Destroyer of pain and fear.<br>
  He cures the disease, and cuts away the noose of death.<br>
  O Nanak, the Lord God is the Destroyer of fear; meeting the Guru, the Lord God is found. ||10||<br>
  One who knows the Immaculate Lord chews up death.<br>
  One who understands karma, realizes the Word of the Shabad.<br>
  He Himself knows, and He Himself realizes. This whole world is all His play. ||11||<br>
  He Himself is the Banker, and He Himself is the Merchant.<br>
  The Appraiser Himself appraises.<br>
  He Himself tests upon His Touchstone, and He Himself estimates the value. ||12||<br>
  God Himself, the Merciful Lord, grants His Grace.<br>
  The Gardener pervades and permeates each and every heart.<br>
  The pure, primal, detached Lord abides within all. The Guru, the Lord Incarnate, leads us to meet the Lord God. ||13||<br>
  God is wise and all-knowing; He purges men of their pride.<br>
  Eradicating duality, the One Lord reveals Himself.<br>
  Such a being remains unattached amidst hope, singing the Praise of the Immaculate Lord, who has no ancestry. ||14||<br>
  Eradicating egotism, he obtains the peace of the Shabad.<br>
  He alone is spiritually wise, who contemplates his own self.<br>
  O Nanak, singing the Glorious Praises of the Lord, the true profit is obtained; in the Sat Sangat, the True Congregation, the fruit of Truth is obtained. ||15||2||19||<br>
  Maaroo, First Mehl:<br>
  Speak the Truth, and remain in the home of Truth.<br>
  Remain dead while yet alive, and cross over the terrifying world-ocean.<br>
  The Guru is the boat, the ship, the raft; meditating on the Lord in your mind, you shall be carried across to the other side. ||1||<br>
  Eliminating egotism, possessiveness and greed,<br>
  one is liberated from the nine gates, and obtains a place in the Tenth Gate.<br>
  Lofty and high, the farthest of the far and infinite, He created Himself. ||2||<br>
  Receiving the Guru's Teachings, and lovingly attuned to the Lord, one crosses over.<br>
  Singing the Praises of the absolute Lord, why should anyone be afraid of death?<br>
  Wherever I look, I see only You; I do not sing of any other at all. ||3||<br>
  True is the Lord's Name, and True is His Sanctuary.<br>
  True is the Word of the Guru's Shabad, grasping it, one is carries across.<br>
  Speaking the Unspoken, one sees the Infinite Lord, and then, he does not have to enter the womb of reincarnation again. ||4||<br>
  Without the Truth, no one finds sincerity or contentment.<br>
  Without the Guru, no one is liberated; coming and going in reincarnation continue.<br>
  Chanting the Mool Mantra, and the Name of the Lord, the source of nectar, says Nanak, I have found the Perfect Lord. ||5||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 053</h2></center>
  Without the Truth, the terrifying world-ocean cannot be crossed.<br>
  This ocean is vast and unfathomable; it is overflowing with the worst poison.<br>
  One who receives the Guru's Teachings, and remains aloof and detached, obtains a place in the home of the Fearless Lord. ||6||<br>
  False is the cleverness of loving attachment to the world.<br>
  In no time at all, it comes and goes.<br>
  Forgetting the Naam, the Name of the Lord, the proud egotistical people depart; in creation and destruction they are wasted away. ||7||<br>
  In creation and destruction, they are bound in bondage.<br>
  The noose of egotism and Maya is around their necks.<br>
  Whoever does not accept the Guru's Teachings, and does not dwell upon the Lord's Name, is bound and bagged, and dragged into the City of Death. ||8||<br>
  Without the Guru, how can anyone be emancipated or liberated?<br>
  Without the Guru, how can anyone meditate on the Lord's Name?<br>
  Accepting the Guru's Teachings, cross over the arduous, terrifying world-ocean; you shall be emancipated, and find peace. ||9||<br>
  Through the Guru's Teachings, Krishna lifted up the mountain of Govardhan.<br>
  Through the Guru's Teachings, Rama floated stones across the ocean.<br>
  Accepting the Guru's Teachings, the supreme status is obtained; O Nanak, the Guru eradicates doubt. ||10||<br>
  Accepting the Guru's Teachings, cross over to the other side through Truth.<br>
  O soul, remember the Lord within your heart.<br>
  The noose of death is cut away, meditating on the Lord; you shall obtain the Immaculate Lord, who has no ancestry. ||11||<br>
  Through the Guru's Teachings, the Holy become one's friends and Siblings of Destiny.<br>
  Through the Guru's Teachings, the inner fire is subdued and extinguished.<br>
  Chant the Naam with your mind and mouth; know the unknowable Lord, the Life of the World, deep within the nucleus of your heart. ||12||<br>
  The Gurmukh understands, and is pleased with the Word of the Shabad.<br>
  Who does he praise or slander?<br>
  Know yourself, and meditate on the Lord of the Universe; let your mind be pleased with the Lord, the Master of the Universe. ||13||<br>
  Know the One who pervades all the realms of the universe.<br>
  As Gurmukh, understand and realize the Shabad.<br>
  The Enjoyer enjoys each and every heart, and yet He remains detached from all. ||14||<br>
  Through the Guru's Teachings, chant the Pure Praises of the Lord.<br>
  Through the Guru's Teachings, behold the lofty Lord with your eyes.<br>
  Whoever listens to the Lord's Name, and the Word of His Bani, O Nanak, is imbued with the color of the Lord's Love. ||15||3||20||<br>
  Maaroo, First Mehl:<br>
  Leave behind sexual desire, anger and the slander of others.<br>
  Renounce greed and possessiveness, and become carefree.<br>
  Break the chains of doubt, and remain unattached; you shall find the Lord, and the Lord's sublime essence, deep within yourself. ||1||<br>
  As one sees the flash of lightning in the night,<br>
  see the Divine Light deep within your nucleus, day and night.<br>
  The Lord, the embodiment of bliss, incomparably beautiful, reveals the Perfect Guru. ||2||<br>
  So meet with the True Guru, and God Himself will save you.<br>
  He placed the lamps of the sun and the moon in the home of the sky.<br>
  See the invisible Lord, and remain absorbed in loving devotion. God is all throughout the three worlds. ||3||<br>
  Obtaining the sublime ambrosial essence, desire and fear are dispelled.<br>
  The state of inspired illumination is obtained, and self-conceit is eradicated.<br>
  The lofty and exalted state, the highest of the high is obtained, practicing the immaculate Word of the Shabad. ||4||<br>
  The Naam, the Name of the invisible and unfathomable Lord, is infinite.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 054</h2></center>
  The sublime essence of the Beloved Naam is utterly sweet.<br>
  O Lord, please bless Nanak with Your Praise in each and every age; meditating on the Lord, I cannot find His limits. ||5||<br>
  With the Naam deep within the nucleus of the self, the jewel is obtained.<br>
  Meditating on the Lord, the mind is comforted and consoled by the mind itself.<br>
  On that most difficult path, the Destroyer of fear is found, and one does not have to enter the womb of reincarnation again. ||6||<br>
  Through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, inspiration for loving devotional worship wells up.<br>
  I beg for the treasure of the Naam, and the Lord's Praise.<br>
  When it pleases the Lord, He unites me in Union with the Guru; the Lord saves the whole world. ||7||<br>
  One who chants the Lord's Chant, attains the Wisdom of the True Guru.<br>
  The tyrant, the Messenger of Death, becomes a servant at his feet.<br>
  In the noble congregation of the Sangat, one's state and way of life become noble as well, and one crosses over the terrifying world-ocean. ||8||<br>
  Through the Shabad, one crosses over this terrifying world-ocean.<br>
  The duality within is burnt away from within.<br>
  Taking up the five arrows of virtue, Death is killed, drawing the Bow of the Tenth Gate in the Mind's Sky. ||9||<br>
  How can the faithless cynics attain enlightened awareness of the Shabad?<br>
  Without awareness of the Shabad, they come and go in reincarnation.<br>
  O Nanak, the Gurmukh obtains the support of liberation; by perfect destiny, he meets the Lord. ||10||<br>
  The Fearless True Guru is our Savior and Protector.<br>
  Devotional worship is obtained through the Guru, the Lord of the world.<br>
  The blissful music of the unstruck sound current vibrates and resounds; through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, the Immaculate Lord is obtained. ||11||<br>
  He alone is fearless, who has no destiny written on His head.<br>
  God Himself is unseen; He reveals Himself through His wondrous creative power.<br>
  He Himself is unattached, unborn and self-existent. O Nanak, through the Guru's Teachings, He is found. ||12||<br>
  The True Guru knows the state of one's inner being.<br>
  He alone is fearless, who realizes the Word of the Guru's Shabad.<br>
  He looks within his own inner being, and realizes the Lord within all; his mind does not waver at all. ||13||<br>
  He alone is fearless, within whose being the Lord abides.<br>
  Day and night, he is delighted with the Immaculate Naam, the Name of the Lord.<br>
  O Nanak, in the Sangat, the Holy Congregation, the Lord's Praise is obtained, and one easily, intuitively meets the Lord. ||14||<br>
  One who knows God, within the self and beyond,<br>
  remains detached, and brings his wandering mind back to its home.<br>
  The True Primal Lord is over all the three worlds; O Nanak, His Ambrosial Nectar is obtained. ||15||4||21||<br>
  Maaroo, First Mehl:<br>
  The Creator Lord is infinite; His creative power is wondrous.<br>
  Created beings have no power over Him.<br>
  He formed the living beings, and He Himself sustains them; the Hukam of His Command controls each and every one. ||1||<br>
  The all-pervading Lord orchestrates all through His Hukam.<br>
  Who is near, and who is far away?<br>
  Behold the Lord, both hidden and manifest, in each and every heart; the unique Lord is permeating all. ||2||<br>
  One whom the Lord unites with Himself, merges in conscious awareness.<br>
  Through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, meditate on the Lord's Name.<br>
  God is the embodiment of bliss, incomparably beautiful and unfathomable; meeting with the Guru, doubt is dispelled. ||3||<br>
  The Naam, the Name of the Lord, is more dear to me than my mind, body and wealth.<br>
  In the end, when I must depart, it shall be my only help and support.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 055</h2></center>
  In this world of love and attachment, no one is anyone else's friend or companion; without the Lord, without the Guru, who has ever found peace? ||4||<br>
  He, unto whom the Perfect Guru grants His Grace,<br>
  is merged in the Word of the Shabad, through the Teachings of the brave, heroic Guru.<br>
  O Nanak, dwell upon, and serve at the Guru's feet; He places those who wander back on the Path. ||5||<br>
  The wealth of the Lord's Praise is very dear to the humble Saints.<br>
  Through the Guru's Teachings, I have obtained Your Name, Lord.<br>
  The beggar serves at the Lord's door, and in the Court of the Lord, sings His Praises. ||6||<br>
  When one meets the True Guru, he is called into the Mansion of the Lord's Presence.<br>
  In the True Court, he is blessed with salvation and honor.<br>
  The faithless cynic has no place of rest in the Lord's palace; he suffers the pains of birth and death. ||7||<br>
  So serve the True Guru, the unfathomable ocean,<br>
  and you shall obtain the profit, the wealth, the jewel of the Naam.<br>
  The filth of corruption is washed away, by bathing in the pool of Ambrosial Nectar. In the Guru's pool, contentment is obtained. ||8||<br>
  So serve the Guru without hesitation.<br>
  And in the midst of hope, remain unmoved by hope.<br>
  Serve the Eradicator of cynicism and suffering, and you shall never again be afflicted by the disease. ||9||<br>
  One who is pleasing to the True Lord is blessed with glorious greatness.<br>
  Who else can teach him anything?<br>
  The Lord and the Guru are pervading in one form. O Nanak, the Lord loves the Guru. ||10||<br>
  Some read scriptures, the Vedas and the Puraanas.<br>
  Some sit and listen, and read to others.<br>
  Tell me, how can the heavy, rigid doors be opened? Without the True Guru, the essence of reality is not realized. ||11||<br>
  Some collect dust, and smear their bodies with ashes;<br>
  but deep within them are the outcasts of anger and egotism.<br>
  Practicing hypocrisy, Yoga is not obtained; without the True Guru, the unseen Lord is not found. ||12||<br>
  Some make vows to visit sacred shrines of pilgrimage, keep fasts and live in the forest.<br>
  Some practice chastity, charity and self-discipline, and speak of spiritual wisdom.<br>
  But without the Lord's Name, how can anyone find peace? Without the True Guru, doubt is not dispelled. ||13||<br>
  Inner cleansing techniques, channeling the energy to raise the Kundalini to the Tenth Gate,<br>
  inhaling, exhaling and holding the breath by the force of the mind -<br>
  by empty hypocritical practices, Dharmic love for the Lord is not produced. Only through the Word of the Guru's Shabad is the sublime, supreme essence obtained. ||14||<br>
  Seeing the Lord's creative power, my mind remains satisfied.<br>
  Through the Guru's Shabad, I have realized that all is God.<br>
  O Nanak, the Lord, the Supreme Soul, is in all. The Guru, the True Guru, has inspired me to see the unseen Lord. ||15||5||22||<br>
  Maaroo, Solhay, Third Mehl:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  By the Hukam of His Command, He effortlessly created the Universe.<br>
  Creating the creation, He gazes upon His own greatness.<br>
  He Himself acts, and inspires all to act; in His Will, He pervades and permeates all. ||1||<br>
  The world is in the darkness of love and attachment to Maya.<br>
  How rare is that Gurmukh who contemplates, and understands.<br>
  He alone attains the Lord, unto whom He grants His Grace. He Himself unites in His Union. ||2||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 056</h2></center>
  Uniting with Himself, He bestows glorious greatness.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, one comes to know the Lord's worth.<br>
  The self-willed manmukh wanders everywhere, weeping and wailing; he is utterly ruined by the love of duality. ||3||<br>
  Egotism was instilled into the illusion of Maya.<br>
  The self-willed manmukh is deluded, and loses his honor.<br>
  But one who becomes Gurmukh is absorbed in the Name; he remains immersed in the True Lord. ||4||<br>
  Spiritual wisdom is obtained from the Guru, along with the jewel of the Naam, the Name of the Lord.<br>
  Desires are subdued, and one remains immersed in the mind.<br>
  The Creator Himself stages all His plays; He Himself bestows understanding. ||5||<br>
  One who serves the True Guru eradicates self-conceit.<br>
  Meeting with his Beloved, he finds peace through the Word of the Shabad.<br>
  Deep within his inner being, he is imbued with loving devotion; intuitively, he becomes one with the Lord. ||6||<br>
  The Destroyer of pain is known through the Guru.<br>
  The Great Giver, the Life of the world, Himself has met me.<br>
  He alone understands, whom the Lord joins with Himself. Fear and doubt are taken away from his body. ||7||<br>
  He Himself is the Gurmukh, and He Himself bestows His blessings.<br>
  Through the True Word of the Shabad, serve the True Guru.<br>
  Old age and death cannot even touch one who is in harmony with the True Lord. ||8||<br>
  The world is burning up in the fire of desire.<br>
  It burns and burns, and is destroyed in all its corruption.<br>
  The self-willed manmukh finds no place of rest anywhere. The True Guru has imparted this understanding. ||9||<br>
  Those who serve the True Guru are very fortunate.<br>
  They remain lovingly focused on the True Name forever.<br>
  The Immaculate Naam, the Name of the Lord, permeates the nucleus of their inner being; through the Shabad, their desires are quenched. ||10||<br>
  True is the Word of the Shabad, and True is the Bani of His Word.<br>
  How rare is that Gurmukh who realizes this.<br>
  Those who are imbued with the True Shabad are detached. Their comings and goings in reincarnation are ended. ||11||<br>
  One who realizes the Shabad is cleansed of impurities.<br>
  The Immaculate Naam abides within his mind.<br>
  He serves his True Guru forever, and egotism is eradicated from within. ||12||<br>
  If one comes to understand, through the Guru, then he comes to know the Lord's Door.<br>
  But without the Naam, one babbles and argues in vain.<br>
  The glory of serving the True Guru is that it eradicates hunger and thirst. ||13||<br>
  When the Lord unites them with Himself, then they come to understand.<br>
  Without spiritual wisdom, they understand nothing at all.<br>
  One whose mind is filled with the Guru's gift forever - his inner being resounds with the Shabad, and the Word of the Guru's Bani. ||14||<br>
  He acts according to his pre-ordained destiny.<br>
  No one can erase the Command of the Primal Lord.<br>
  They alone dwell in the Sat Sangat, the True Congregation, who have such pre-ordained destiny. ||15||<br>
  He alone finds the Lord, unto whom He grants His Grace.<br>
  He links his consciousness to the deep meditative state of the True Shabad.<br>
  Nanak, Your slave, offers this humble prayer; I stand at Your Door, begging for Your Name. ||16||1||<br>
  Maaroo, Third Mehl:<br>
  The One and only Lord is pervading and permeating everywhere.<br>
  How rare is that person, who as Gurmukh, understands this.<br>
  The One Lord is permeating and pervading, deep within the nucleus of all. Without Him, there is no other at all. ||1||<br>
  He created the 8.4 millions species of beings.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 057</h2></center>
  The spiritual teachers and meditators proclaim this.<br>
  He Himself nourishes all; no one else can estimate His value. ||2||<br>
  Love and attachment to Maya are utter darkness.<br>
  Egotism and possessiveness have spread throughout the expanse of the universe.<br>
  Night and day, they burn, day and night; without the Guru, there is no peace or tranquility. ||3||<br>
  He Himself unites, and He Himself separates.<br>
  He Himself establishes, and He Himself disestablishes.<br>
  True is the Hukam of His Command, and True is the expanse of His universe. No one else can issue any Command. ||4||<br>
  He alone is attached to the Lord, whom the Lord attaches to Himself.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, the fear of death runs away.<br>
  The Shabad, the Giver of peace, dwells forever deep within the nucleus of the self. One who is Gurmukh understands. ||5||<br>
  God Himself unites those united in His Union.<br>
  Whatever is pre-ordained by destiny, cannot be erased.<br>
  Night and day, His devotees worship Him, day and night; one who becomes Gurmukh serves Him. ||6||<br>
  Serving the True Guru, lasting peace is experienced.<br>
  He Himself, the Giver of all, has come and met me.<br>
  Subduing egotism, the fire of thirst has been extinguished; contemplating the Word of the Shabad, peace is found. ||7||<br>
  One who is attached to his body and family, does not understand.<br>
  But one who becomes Gurmukh, sees the Lord with his eyes.<br>
  Night and day, he chants the Naam, day and night; meeting with his Beloved, he finds peace. ||8||<br>
  The self-willed manmukh wanders distracted, attached to duality.<br>
  That unfortunate wretch - why didn't he just die as soon as he was born?<br>
  Coming and going, he wastes away his life in vain. Without the Guru, liberation is not obtained. ||9||<br>
  That body which is stained with the filth of egotism is false and impure.<br>
  It may be washed a hundred times, but its filth is still not removed.<br>
  But if it is washed with the Word of the Shabad, then it is truly cleansed, and it shall never be soiled again. ||10||<br>
  The five demons destroy the body.<br>
  He dies and dies again, only to be reincarnated; he does not contemplate the Shabad.<br>
  The darkness of emotional attachment to Maya is within his inner being; as if in a dream, he does not understand. ||11||<br>
  Some conquer the five demons, by being attached to the Shabad.<br>
  They are blessed and very fortunate; the True Guru comes to meet them.<br>
  Within the nucleus of their inner being, they dwell upon the Truth; attuned to the Lord's Love, they intuitively merge in Him. ||12||<br>
  The Guru's Way is known through the Guru.<br>
  His perfect servant attains realization through the Shabad.<br>
  Deep within his heart, he dwells forever upon the Shabad; he tastes the sublime essence of the True Lord with his tongue. ||13||<br>
  Egotism is conquered and subdued by the Shabad.<br>
  I have enshrined the Name of the Lord within my heart.<br>
  Other than the One Lord, I know nothing at all. Whatever will be, will automatically be. ||14||<br>
  Without the True Guru, no one obtains intuitive wisdom.<br>
  The Gurmukh understands, and is immersed in the True Lord.<br>
  He serves the True Lord, and is attuned to the True Shabad. The Shabad banishes egotism. ||15||<br>
  He Himself is the Giver of virtue, the Contemplative Lord.<br>
  The Gurmukh is given the winning dice.<br>
  O Nanak, immersed in the Naam, the Name of the Lord, one becomes true; from the True Lord, honor is obtained. ||16||2||<br>
  Maaroo, Third Mehl:<br>
  One One True Lord is the Life of the World, the Great Giver.<br>
  Serving the Guru, through the Word of the Shabad, He is realized.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 058</h2></center>
  There is only One Command, and there is only One Supreme King. In each and every age, He links each to their tasks. ||1||<br>
  That humble being is immaculate, who knows his own self.<br>
  The Lord, the Giver of peace, Himself comes and meets him.<br>
  His tongue is imbued with the Shabad, and he sings the Glorious Praises of the Lord; he is honored in the Court of the True Lord. ||2||<br>
  The Gurmukh is blessed with the glorious greatness of the Naam.<br>
  The self-willed manmukh, the slanderer, loses his honor.<br>
  Attuned to the Naam, the supreme soul-swans remain detached; in the home of the self, they remain absorbed in deep meditative trance. ||3||<br>
  That humble being who dies in the Shabad is perfect.<br>
  The brave, heroic True Guru chants and proclaims this.<br>
  Deep within the body is the true pool of Ambrosial Nectar; the mind drinks it in with loving devotion. ||4||<br>
  The Pandit, the religious scholar, reads and instructs others,<br>
  but he does not realize that his own home is on fire.<br>
  Without serving the True Guru, the Naam is not obtained. You can read until you are exhausted, but you shall not find peace and tranquility. ||5||<br>
  Some smear their bodies with ashes, and wander around in religious disguises.<br>
  Without the Word of the Shabad, who has ever subdued egotism?<br>
  Night and day, they continue burning, day and night; they are deluded and confused by their doubt and religious costumes. ||6||<br>
  Some, in the midst of their household and family, remain always unattached.<br>
  They die in the Shabad, and dwell in the Lord's Name.<br>
  Night and day, they remain forever attuned to His Love; they focus their consciousness on loving devotion and the Fear of God. ||7||<br>
  The self-willed manmukh indulges in slander, and is ruined.<br>
  The dog of greed barks within him.<br>
  The Messenger of Death never leaves him, and in the end, he leaves, regretting and repenting. ||8||<br>
  Through the True Word of the Shabad, true honor is obtained.<br>
  Without the Name, no one attains liberation.<br>
  Without the True Guru, no one finds the Name. Such is the making which God has made. ||9||<br>
  Some are Siddhas and seekers, and great contemplators.<br>
  Some remain imbued with the Naam, the Name of the Formless Lord, day and night.<br>
  He alone understands, whom the Lord unites with Himself; through loving devotional worship, fear is dispelled. ||10||<br>
  Some take cleansing baths and give donations to charities, but they do not understand.<br>
  Some struggle with their minds, and conquer and subdue their minds.<br>
  Some are imbued with love for the True Word of the Shabad; they merge with the True Shabad. ||11||<br>
  He Himself creates and bestows glorious greatness.<br>
  By the Pleasure of His Will, He bestows union.<br>
  Bestowing His Grace, He comes to dwell in the mind; such is the Command ordained by my God. ||12||<br>
  Those humble beings who serve the True Guru are true.<br>
  The false, self-willed manmukhs do not know how to serve the Guru.<br>
  The Creator Himself creates the creation and watches over it; he attaches all according to the Pleasure of His Will. ||13||<br>
  In each and every age, the True Lord is the one and only Giver.<br>
  Through perfect destiny, one realizes the Word of the Guru's Shabad.<br>
  Those who are immersed in the Shabad are not separated again. By His Grace, they are intuitively immersed in the Lord. ||14||<br>
  Acting in egotism, they are stained with the filth of Maya.<br>
  They die and die again, only to be reborn in the love of duality.<br>
  Without serving the True Guru, no one finds liberation. O mind, tune into this, and see. ||15||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 059</h2></center>
  He does whatever He pleases.<br>
  No one has done, or can do anything by himself.<br>
  O Nanak, through the Name, one is blessed with glorious greatness, and obtains honor in the Court of the True Lord. ||16||3||<br>
  Maaroo, Third Mehl:<br>
  All who come shall have to depart.<br>
  In the love of duality, they are caught by the noose of the Messenger of Death.<br>
  Those humble beings who are protected by the True Guru, are saved. They merge into the Truest of the True. ||1||<br>
  The Creator Himself creates the creation, and watches over it.<br>
  Thay alone are acceptable, upon whom He bestows His Glance of Grace.<br>
  The Gurmukh attains spiritual wisdom, and understands everything. The ignorant ones act blindly. ||2||<br>
  The self-willed manmukh is cynical; he doesn't understand.<br>
  He dies and dies again, only to be reborn, and loses his life uselessly again.<br>
  The Gurmukh is imbued with the Naam, the Name of the Lord; he find peace, and is intuitively immersed in the True Lord. ||3||<br>
  Chasing after worldly affairs, the mind has become corroded and rusty.<br>
  But meeting with the Perfect Guru, it is transmuted into gold once again.<br>
  When the Lord Himself grants forgiveness, then peace is obtained; through the Perfect Word of the Shabad, one is united with Him. ||4||<br>
  The false and evil-minded are the most wicked of the wicked.<br>
  They are the most unworthy of the unworthy.<br>
  With false intellect, and insipid words of mouth, evil-minded, they do not obtain the Naam. ||5||<br>
  The unworthy soul-bride is not pleasing to her Husband Lord.<br>
  False-minded, her actions are false.<br>
  The foolish person does not know the excellence of her Husband Lord. Without the Guru, she does not understand at all. ||6||<br>
  The evil-minded, wicked soul-bride practices wickedness.<br>
  She decorates herself, but her Husband Lord is not pleased.<br>
  The virtuous soul-bride enjoys and ravishes her Husband Lord forever; the True Guru unites her in His Union. ||7||<br>
  God Himself issues the Hukam of His Command, and beholds all.<br>
  Some are forgiven, according to their pre-ordained destiny.<br>
  Night and day, they are imbued with the Naam, and they find the True Lord. He Himself unites them in His Union. ||8||<br>
  Egotism attaches them to the juice of emotional attachment, and makes them run around.<br>
  The Gurmukh is intuitively immersed in the True Love of the Lord.<br>
  He Himself unites, He Himself acts, and beholds. Without the True Guru, understanding is not obtained. ||9||<br>
  Some contemplate the Word of the Shabad; these humble beings remain always awake and aware.<br>
  Some are attached to the love of Maya; these unfortunate ones remain asleep.<br>
  He Himself acts, and inspires all to act; no one else can do anything. ||10||<br>
  Through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, death is conquered and killed.<br>
  Keep the Name of the Lord enshrined within your heart.<br>
  Serving the True Guru, peace is obtained, and one merges in the Name of the Lord. ||11||<br>
  In the love of duality, the world wanders around insane.<br>
  Immersed in love and attachment to Maya, it suffers in pain.<br>
  Wearing all sorts of religious robes, He is not obtained. Without the True Guru, peace is not found. ||12||<br>
  Who is to blame, when He Himself does everything?<br>
  As He wills, so is the path we take.<br>
  He Himself is the Merciful Giver of peace; as He wills, so do we follow. ||13||<br>
  He Himself is the Creator, and He Himself is the Enjoyer.<br>
  He Himself is detached, and He Himself is attached.<br>
  He Himself is immaculate, compassionate, the lover of nectar; the Hukam of His Command cannot be erased. ||14||<br>
  Those who know the One Lord are very fortunate.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 060</h2></center>
  He dwells in each and every heart, the Great Giver, the Life of the world.<br>
  At the same time, He is both hidden and revealed. For the Gurmukh, doubt and fear are dispelled. ||15||<br>
  The Gurmukh knows the One, the Dear Lord.<br>
  Deep within the nucleus of his inner being, is the Naam, the Name of the Lord; he realizes the Word of the Shabad.<br>
  He alone receives it, unto whom You give it. O Nanak, the Naam is glorious greatness. ||16||4||<br>
  Maaroo, Third Mehl:<br>
  I praise the true, profound and unfathomable Lord.<br>
  All the world is in His power.<br>
  He enjoys all hearts forever, day and night; He Himself dwells in peace. ||1||<br>
  True is the Lord and Master, and True is His Name.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, I enshrine Him in my mind.<br>
  He Himself has come to dwell deep within the nucleus of my heart; the noose of death has been snapped. ||2||<br>
  Whom should I serve, and whom should I praise?<br>
  I serve the True Guru, and praise the Word of the Shabad.<br>
  Through the True Shabad, the intellect is exalted and ennobled forever, and the lotus deep within blossoms forth. ||3||<br>
  The body is frail and perishable, like paper.<br>
  When the drop of water falls upon it, it crumbles and dissolves instantaneously.<br>
  But the body of the Gurmukh, who understands, is like gold; the Naam, the Name of the Lord, dwells deep within. ||4||<br>
  Pure is that kitchen, which is enclosed by spiritual awareness.<br>
  The Lord's Name is my food, and Truth is my support.<br>
  Forever satisfied, sanctified and pure is that person, within whose heart the Lord's Name abides. ||5||<br>
  I am a sacrifice to those who are attached to the Truth.<br>
  They sing the Glorious Praises of the Lord, and remain awake and aware night and day.<br>
  True peace fills them forever, and their tongues savor the sublime essence of the Lord. ||6||<br>
  I remember the Lord's Name, and no other at all.<br>
  I serve the One Lord, and no other at all.<br>
  The Perfect Guru has revealed the whole Truth to me; I dwell in the True Name. ||7||<br>
  Wandering, wandering in reincarnation, again and again, he comes into the world.<br>
  He is deluded and confused, when the Lord and Master confuses him.<br>
  He meets with the Dear Lord, when, as Gurmukh, he understands; he remembers the Shabad, the Word of the immortal, eternal Lord God. ||8||<br>
  I am a sinner, overflowing with sexual desire and anger.<br>
  With what mouth should I speak? I have no virtue, and I have rendered no service.<br>
  I am a sinking stone; please, Lord, unite me with Yourself. Your Name is eternal and imperishable. ||9||<br>
  No one does anything; no one is able to do anything.<br>
  That alone happens, which the Lord Himself does, and causes to be done.<br>
  Those whom He Himself forgives, find peace; they dwell forever in the Naam, the Name of the Lord. ||10||<br>
  This body is the earth, and the infinite Shabad is the seed.<br>
  Deal and trade with the True Name alone.<br>
  The True wealth increases; it is never exhausted, when the Naam dwells deep within. ||11||<br>
  O Dear Lord, please bless me, the worthless sinner, with virtue.<br>
  Forgive me, and bless me with Your Name.<br>
  One who becomes Gurmukh, is honored; he dwells in the Name of the One Lord alone. ||12||<br>
  The wealth of the Lord is deep within one's inner being, but he does not realize it.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, one comes to understand.<br>
  One who becomes Gurmukh is blessed with this wealth; he lives forever in the Naam. ||13||<br>
  Fire and wind lead him into delusions of doubt.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 061</h2></center>
  In love and attachment to Maya, he has no understanding at all.<br>
  The blind, self-willed manmukh sees nothing; through the Guru's Teachings, the Naam is gloriously revealed. ||14||<br>
  The manmukhs are asleep in egotism and Maya.<br>
  They do not watch over their own homes, and are ruined in the end.<br>
  They slander others, and burn in great anxiety; they dwell in pain and suffering. ||15||<br>
  The Creator Himself has created the creation.<br>
  He blesses the Gurmukh with understanding.<br>
  O Nanak, those who are attuned to the Naam - their minds become immaculate; they dwell in the Naam, and only the Naam. ||16||5||<br>
  Maaroo, Third Mehl:<br>
  I serve the One Lord, who is eternal, stable and True.<br>
  Attached to duality, the whole world is false.<br>
  Following the Guru's Teachings, I praise the True Lord forever, pleased with the Truest of the True. ||1||<br>
  Your Glorious Virtues are so many, Lord; I do not know even one.<br>
  The Life of the world, the Great Giver, attaches us to himself.<br>
  He Himself forgives, and bestows glorious greatness. Following the Guru's Teachings, this mind is delighted. ||2||<br>
  The Word of the Shabad has subdued the waves of Maya.<br>
  Egotism has been conquered, and this mind has become immaculate.<br>
  I intuitively sing His Glorious Praises, imbued with the Lord's Love. My tongue chants and savors the Lord's Name. ||3||<br>
  Crying out, "Mine, mine!" he spends his life.<br>
  The self-willed manmukh does not understand; he wanders around in ignorance.<br>
  The Messenger of Death watches over him every moment, every instant; night and day, his life is wasting away. ||4||<br>
  He practices greed within, and does not understand.<br>
  He does not see the Messenger of Death hovering over his head.<br>
  Whatever one does in this world, will come to face him in the hereafter; what can he do at that very last moment? ||5||<br>
  Those who are attached to the Truth are true.<br>
  The self-willed manmukhs, attached to duality, weep and wail.<br>
  He is the Lord and Master of both worlds; He Himself delights in virtue. ||6||<br>
  Through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, His humble servant is exalted forever.<br>
  This mind is enticed by the Naam, the source of nectar.<br>
  It is not stained at all by the dirt of attachment to Maya; through the Guru's Teachings, it is pleased and saturated with the Lord's Name. ||7||<br>
  The One Lord is contained within all.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, He is revealed.<br>
  One who subdues his ego, finds lasting peace; he drinks in the Ambrosial Nectar of the True Name. ||8||<br>
  God is the Destroyer of sin and pain.<br>
  The Gurmukh serves Him, and contemplates the Word of the Shabad.<br>
  He Himself is pervading everything. The Gurmukh's body and mind are saturated and pleased. ||9||<br>
  The world is burning in the fire of Maya.<br>
  The Gurmukh extinguishes this fire, by contemplating the Shabad.<br>
  Deep within are peace and tranquility, and lasting peace is obtained. Following the Guru's Teachings, one is blessed with the Naam, the Name of the Lord. ||10||<br>
  Even Indra, seated upon his throne, is caught in the fear of death.<br>
  The Messenger of Death will not spare them, even though they try all sorts of things.<br>
  When one meets with the True Guru, one is liberated, drinking in and savoring the sublime essence of the Lord, Har, Har. ||11||<br>
  There is no devotion within the self-willed manmukh.<br>
  Through devotional worship, the Gurmukh obtains peace and tranquility.<br>
  Forever pure and sanctified is the Word of the Guru's Bani; following the Guru's Teachings, one's inner being is drenched in it. ||12||<br>
  I have considered Brahma, Vishnu and Shiva.<br>
  They are bound by the three qualities - the three gunas; they are far away from liberation.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 062</h2></center>
  The Gurmukh knows the spiritual wisdom of the One Lord. Night and day, he chants the Naam, the Name of the Lord. ||13||<br>
  He may read the Vedas, but he does not realize the Lord's Name.<br>
  For the sake of Maya, he reads and recites and argues.<br>
  The ignorant and blind person is filled with filth within. How can he cross over the impassable world-ocean? ||14||<br>
  He voices all the controversies of the Vedas,<br>
  but his inner being is not saturated or satisfied, and he does not realize the Word of the Shabad.<br>
  The Vedas tell all about virtue and vice, but only the Gurmukh drinks in the Ambrosial Nectar. ||15||<br>
  The One True Lord is all by Himself.<br>
  There is no one else except Him.<br>
  O Nanak, true is the mind of one who is attuned to the Naam; he speaks Truth, and nothing but Truth. ||16||6||<br>
  Maaroo, Third Mehl:<br>
  The True Lord has established the Throne of Truth.<br>
  He dwells in His own home deep within the self, where there is no emotional attachment to Maya.<br>
  The True Lord dwells deep within the nucleus of the Gurmukh's heart forever; his actions are excellent. ||1||<br>
  True is his merchandise, and true is his trade.<br>
  There is no doubt within him, and no expanse of duality.<br>
  He has earned the true wealth, which is never exhausted. How few are those who contemplate this, and understand. ||2||<br>
  They alone are attached to the True Name, whom the Lord Himself attaches.<br>
  The Word of the Shabad is deep within the nucleus of the self; good fortune is recorded upon their foreheads.<br>
  Through the True Word of the Shabad, they sing the True Praises of the Lord; they are attuned to contemplative meditation on the Shabad. ||3||<br>
  I praise the True Lord, the Truest of the True.<br>
  I see the One Lord, and no other.<br>
  The Guru's Teachings are the ladder to reach the highest of the high. the jewel of spiritual wisdom conquers egotism. ||4||<br>
  Emotional attachment to Maya is burnt away by the Word of the Shabad.<br>
  The True One comes to dwell in the mind, when it pleases You, O Lord.<br>
  True are all the actions of the truthful; the thirst of egotism is subdued. ||5||<br>
  All by Himself, God created emotional attachment to Maya.<br>
  How rare are those who, as Gurmukh, realize the Lord.<br>
  One who becomes Gurmukh practices Truth; true and excellent are his actions. ||6||<br>
  He does those deeds which are pleasing to my God;<br>
  through the Shabad, he burns away egotism and the thirst of desire.<br>
  Following the Guru's Teachings, he remains forever cool and calm deep within; he conquers and subdues his ego. ||7||<br>
  Those who are attached to the Truth are pleased with everything.<br>
  They are embellished with the True Word of the Shabad.<br>
  Those who are true in this world, are true in the Court of the Lord. The Merciful Lord adorns them with His Mercy. ||8||<br>
  Those who are attached to duality, and not the Truth,<br>
  are trapped in emotional attachment to Maya; they totally suffer in pain.<br>
  Without the Guru, they do not understand pain and pleasure; attached to Maya, they suffer in terrible pain. ||9||<br>
  Those whose minds are pleased with the True Word of the Shabad<br>
  act according to pre-ordained destiny.<br>
  They serve the True Lord, and meditate on the True Lord; they are imbued with contemplative meditation on the True Lord. ||10||<br>
  Service to the Guru seems sweet to them.<br>
  Night and day, they are intuitively immersed in celestial peace.<br>
  Chanting the Name of the Lord, Har, Har, their minds become immaculate; they love to serve the Guru. ||11||<br>
  Those humble beings are at peace, whom the True Guru attaches to the Truth.<br>
  He Himself, in His Will, merges them into Himself.<br>
  Those humble beings, whom the True Guru protects, are saved. The rest are ruined through emotional attachment to Maya. ||12||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 063</h2></center>
  The Gurmukh realizes the True Word of the Shabad.<br>
  He has no family, and he has no mother.<br>
  The One and Only Lord is pervading and permeating deep within the nucleus of all. He is the Support of all beings. ||13||<br>
  Egotism, possessiveness, and the love of duality<br>
  - none of these shall go along with you; such is the pre-ordained will of our Lord and Master.<br>
  Through the True Guru, practice Truth, and the True Lord shall take away your pains. ||14||<br>
  If You so bless me, then I shall find lasting peace.<br>
  Through the True Word of the Shabad, I live the Truth.<br>
  The True Lord is within me, and my mind and body have become True. I am blessed with the overflowing treasure of devotional worship. ||15||<br>
  He Himself watches, and issues His Command.<br>
  He Himself inspires us to obey His Will.<br>
  O Nanak, only those who are attuned to the Naam are detached; their minds, bodies and tongues are embellished with the Naam. ||16||7||<br>
  Maaroo, Third Mehl:<br>
  He Himself created Himself, and came into being.<br>
  The One Lord is pervading in all, remaining hidden.<br>
  The Lord, the Life of the world, takes care of all. Whoever knows his own self, realizes God. ||1||<br>
  He who created Brahma, Vishnu and Shiva,<br>
  links each and every being to its tasks.<br>
  He merges into Himself, whoever is pleasing to His Will. The Gurmukh knows the One Lord. ||2||<br>
  The world is coming and going in reincarnation.<br>
  Attached to Maya, it dwells on its many sins.<br>
  One who realizes the Word of the Guru's Shabad, praises forever the eternal, unchanging True Lord. ||3||<br>
  Some are attached to the root - they find peace.<br>
  But those who are attached to the branches, waste their lives away uselessly.<br>
  Those humble beings, who chant the Name of the Ambrosial Lord, produce the ambrosial fruit. ||4||<br>
  I have no virtues; what words should I speak?<br>
  You see all, and weigh them on Your scale.<br>
  By Your will, You preserve me, and so do I remain. The Gurmukh knows the One Lord. ||5||<br>
  According to Your Will, You link me to my true tasks.<br>
  Renouncing vice, I am immersed in virtue.<br>
  The One Immaculate True Lord abides in virtue; through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, He is realized. ||6||<br>
  Wherever I look, there I see Him.<br>
  Duality and evil-mindedness are destroyed through the Shabad.<br>
  The One Lord God is immersed in His Oneness. He is attuned forever to His own delight. ||7||<br>
  The body-lotus is withering away,<br>
  but the ignorant, self-willed manmukh does not understand the Shabad.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, he searches his body, and finds the Great Giver, the Life of the world. ||8||<br>
  The Lord frees up the body-fortress, which was seized by sins,<br>
  when one keeps the Dear Lord enshrined forever in the heart.<br>
  The fruits of his desires are obtained, and he is dyed in the permanent color of the Lord's Love. ||9||<br>
  The self-willed manmukh speaks of spiritual wisdom, but does not understand.<br>
  Again and again, he comes into the world, but he finds no place of rest.<br>
  The Gurmukh is spiritually wise, and praises the Lord forever. Throughout each and every age, the Gurmukh knows the One Lord. ||10||<br>
  All the deeds which the manmukh does bring pain - nothing but pain.<br>
  The Word of the Shabad is not within him; how can he go to the Court of the Lord?<br>
  The True Shabad dwells deep within the mind of the Gurmukh; he serves the Giver of peace forever. ||11||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 064</h2></center>
  Wherever I look, I see You, everywhere.<br>
  Through the Perfect Guru, all this is known.<br>
  I meditate forever and ever on the Naam; this mind is imbued with the Naam. ||12||<br>
  Imbued with the Naam, the body is sanctified.<br>
  Without the Naam, they are drowned and die without water.<br>
  They come and go, but do not understand the Naam. Some, as Gurmukh, realize the Word of the Shabad. ||13||<br>
  The Perfect True Guru has imparted this understanding.<br>
  Without the Name, no one attains liberation.<br>
  Through the Naam, the Name of the Lord, one is blessed with glorious greatness; he remains intuitively attuned to the Lord's Love. ||14||<br>
  The body-village crumbles and collapses into a pile of dust.<br>
  Without the Shabad, the cycle of reincarnation is not brought to an end.<br>
  One who knows the One Lord, through the True Guru, praises the True Lord, and remains immersed in the True Lord. ||15||<br>
  The True Word of the Shabad comes to dwell in the mind, when the Lord bestows His Glance of Grace.<br>
  O Nanak, those who are attuned to the Naam, the Name of the Formless Lord, realize the True Lord in His True Court. ||16||8||<br>
  Maaroo, Solhay, Third Mehl:<br>
  O Creator, it is You Yourself who does all.<br>
  All beings and creatures are under Your Protection.<br>
  You are hidden, and yet permeating within all; through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, You are realized. ||1||<br>
  Devotion to the Lord is a treasure overflowing.<br>
  He Himself blesses us with contemplative meditation on the Shabad.<br>
  You do whatever You please; my mind is attuned to the True Lord. ||2||<br>
  You Yourself are the priceless diamond and jewel.<br>
  In Your Mercy, You weigh with Your scale.<br>
  All beings and creatures are under Your protection. One who is blessed by Your Grace realizes his own self. ||3||<br>
  One who receives Your Mercy, O Primal Lord,<br>
  does not die, and is not reborn; he is released from the cycle of reincarnation.<br>
  He sings the Glorious Praises of the True Lord, day and night, and, throughout the ages, he knows the One Lord. ||4||<br>
  Emotional attachment to Maya wells up throughout the whole world,<br>
  from Brahma, Vishnu and all the demi-gods.<br>
  Those who are pleasing to Your Will, are attached to the Naam; through spiritual wisdom and understanding, You are recognized. ||5||<br>
  The world is engrossed in vice and virtue.<br>
  Happiness and misery are totally loaded with pain.<br>
  One who becomes Gurmukh finds peace; such a Gurmukh recognizes the Naam. ||6||<br>
  No one can erase the record of one's actions.<br>
  Through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, one finds the door of salvation.<br>
  One who conquers self-conceit and recognizes the Lord, obtains the fruits of his pre-destined rewards. ||7||<br>
  Emotionally attached to Maya, one's consciousness is not attached to the Lord.<br>
  In the love of duality, he will suffer terrible agony in the world hereafter.<br>
  The hypocritical, self-willed manmukhs are deluded by doubt; at the very last moment, they regret and repent. ||8||<br>
  In accordance with the Lord's Will, he sings the Glorious Praises of the Lord.<br>
  He is rid of all sins, and all suffering.<br>
  The Lord is immaculate, and immaculate is the Word of His Bani. My mind is imbued with the Lord. ||9||<br>
  One who is blessed with the Lord's Glance of Grace, obtains the Lord, the treasure of virtue.<br>
  Egotism and possessiveness are brought to an end.<br>
  The One Lord is the only Giver of virtue and vice, merits and demerits; how rare are those who, as Gurmukh, understand this. ||10||<br>
  My God is immaculate, and utterly infinite.<br>
  God unites with Himself, through contemplation of the Word of the Guru's Shabad.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 065</h2></center>
  He Himself forgives, and implants the Truth. The mind and body are then attuned to the True Lord. ||11||<br>
  Within the polluted mind and body is the Light of the Infinite Lord.<br>
  One who understands the Guru's Teachings, contemplates this.<br>
  Conquering egotism, the mind becomes immaculate forever; with his tongue, he serves the Lord, the Giver of peace. ||12||<br>
  In the fortress of the body there are many shops and bazaars;<br>
  within them is the Naam, the Name of the utterly infinite Lord.<br>
  In His Court, one is embellished forever with the Word of the Guru's Shabad; he conquers egotism and realizes the Lord. ||13||<br>
  The jewel is priceless, inaccessible and infinite.<br>
  How can the poor wretch estimate its worth?<br>
  Through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, it is weighed, and so the Shabad is realized deep within. ||14||<br>
  The great volumes of the Simritees and the Shaastras only extend the extension of attachment to Maya.<br>
  The fools read them, but do not understand the Word of the Shabad. How rare are those who, as Gurmukh, understand. ||15||<br>
  The Creator Himself acts, and causes all to act.<br>
  Through the True Word of His Bani, Truth is implanted deep within.<br>
  O Nanak, through the Naam, one is blessed with glorious greatness, and throughout the ages, the One Lord is known. ||16||9||<br>
  Maaroo, Third Mehl:<br>
  Serve the True Creator Lord.<br>
  The Word of the Shabad is the Destroyer of pain.<br>
  He is inaccessible and unfathomable; He cannot be evaluated. He Himself is inaccessible and immeasurable. ||1||<br>
  The True Lord Himself makes Truth pervasive.<br>
  He attaches some humble beings to the Truth.<br>
  They serve the True Lord and practice Truth; through the Name, they are absorbed in the True Lord. ||2||<br>
  The Primal Lord unites His devotees in His Union.<br>
  He attaches them to true devotional worship.<br>
  One who sings forever the Glorious Praises of the Lord, through the True Word of His Bani, earns the profit of this life. ||3||<br>
  The Gurmukh trades, and understands his own self.<br>
  He knows no other than the One Lord.<br>
  True is the banker, and True are His traders, who buy the merchandise of the Naam. ||4||<br>
  He Himself fashions and creates the Universe.<br>
  He inspires a few to realize the Word of the Guru's Shabad.<br>
  Those humble beings who serve the True Guru are true. He snaps the noose of death from around their necks. ||5||<br>
  He destroys, creates, embellishes and fashions all beings,<br>
  and attaches them to duality, attachment and Maya.<br>
  The self-willed manmukhs wander around forever, acting blindly. Death has strung his noose around their necks. ||6||<br>
  He Himself forgives, and enjoins us to serve the Guru.<br>
  Through the Guru's Teachings, the Naam comes to dwell within the mind.<br>
  Night and day, meditate on the Naam, the Name of the True Lord, and earn the profit of the Naam in this world. ||7||<br>
  He Himself is True, and True is His Name.<br>
  The Gurmukh bestows it, and enshrines it within the mind.<br>
  Noble and exalted are those, within whose mind the Lord abides. Their heads are free of strife. ||8||<br>
  He is inaccessible and unfathomable; His value cannot be appraised.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, He dwells within the mind.<br>
  No one calls that person to account, who praises the Word of the Shabad, the Giver of virtue. ||9||<br>
  Brahma, Vishnu and Shiva serve Him.<br>
  Even they cannot find the limits of the unseen, unknowable Lord.<br>
  Those who are blessed by Your Glance of Grace, become Gurmukh, and comprehend the incomprehensible. ||10||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 066</h2></center>
  The Perfect True Guru has imparted this understanding.<br>
  I have enshrined the Naam, the One Name, within my mind.<br>
  I chant the Naam, and meditate on the Naam. Singing His Glorious Praises, I enter the Mansion of the Lord's Presence. ||11||<br>
  The servant serves, and obeys the Command of the Infinite Lord.<br>
  The self-willed manmukhs do not know the value of the Lord's Command.<br>
  By the Hukam of the Lord's Command, one is exalted; by His Hukam, one is glorified; by His Hukam, one becomes carefree. ||12||<br>
  By Guru's Grace, one recognizes the Lord's Hukam.<br>
  The wandering mind is restrained, and brought back to the home of the One Lord.<br>
  Imbued with the Naam, one remains forever detached; the jewel of the Naam rests within the mind. ||13||<br>
  The One Lord is pervasive throughout all the world.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, He is revealed.<br>
  Those humble beings who praise the Shabad are immaculate; they dwell within the home of their own inner self. ||14||<br>
  The devotees abide forever in Your Sanctuary, Lord.<br>
  You are inaccessible and unfathomable; Your value cannot be estimated.<br>
  As it pleases Your Will, You keep us; the Gurmukh meditates on the Naam. ||15||<br>
  Forever and ever, I sing Your Glorious Praises.<br>
  O my True Lord and Master, may I become pleasing to Your Mind.<br>
  Nanak offers this true prayer: O Lord, please bless me with Truth, that I may merge in the Truth. ||16||1||10||<br>
  Maaroo, Third Mehl:<br>
  Those who serve the True Guru are very fortunate.<br>
  Night and day, they remain lovingly attuned to the True Name.<br>
  The Lord, the Giver of peace, abides forever deep within their hearts; they delight in the True Word of the Shabad. ||1||<br>
  When the Lord grants His Grace, one meets with the Guru.<br>
  The Name of the Lord is enshrined within the mind.<br>
  The Lord, the Giver of peace, abides forever within the mind; the mind is delighted with the Word of the Shabad. ||2||<br>
  When the Lord bestows His Mercy, He unites in His Union.<br>
  Egotism and attachment are burned away by the Shabad.<br>
  In the Love of the One Lord, one remains liberated forever; he is not in conflict with anyone. ||3||<br>
  Without serving the True Guru, there is only pitch-black darkness.<br>
  Without the Shabad, no one crosses over to the other side.<br>
  Those who are imbued with the Shabad, are very detached. They earn the profit of the True Word of the Shabad. ||4||<br>
  Pain and pleasure are pre-ordained by the Creator.<br>
  He Himself has caused the love of duality to be pervasive.<br>
  One who becomes Gurmukh remains detached; how can anyone trust the self-willed manmukh? ||5||<br>
  Those who do not recognize the Shabad are manmukhs.<br>
  They do not know the essence of the Fear of the Guru.<br>
  Without this Fear, how can anyone find the Fearless True Lord? The Messenger of Death will pull the breath out. ||6||<br>
  The invulnerable Messenger of Death cannot be killed.<br>
