  The Word of the Guru's Shabad prevents him from approaching.<br>
  When he hears the Word of the Shabad, he runs far away. He is afraid that the self-sufficient Dear Lord will kill him. ||7||<br>
  The Dear Lord is the Ruler above all.<br>
  What can this wretched Messenger of Death do?<br>
  As slave to the Hukam of the Lord's Command, the mortal acts according to His Hukam. According to His Hukam, he is deprived of his breath. ||8||<br>
  The Gurmukh realizes that the True Lord created the creation.<br>
  The Gurmukh knows that the Lord has expanded the entire expanse.<br>
  One who becomes Gurmukh, understands the True Lord. Through the True Word of the Shabad, he finds peace. ||9||<br>
  The Gurmukh knows that the Lord is the Architect of karma.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 067</h2></center>
  Throughout the four ages, he recognizes the Word of the Guru's Shabad.<br>
  The Gurmukh does not die, the Gurmukh is not reborn; the Gurmukh is immersed in the Shabad. ||10||<br>
  The Gurmukh praises the Naam, and the Shabad.<br>
  God is inaccessible, unfathomable and self-sufficient.<br>
  The Naam, the Name of the One Lord, saves and redeems throughout the four ages. Through the Shabad, one trades in the Naam. ||11||<br>
  The Gurmukh obtains eternal peace and tranqulity.<br>
  The Gurmukh enshrines the Naam within his heart.<br>
  One who becomes Gurmukh recognizes the Naam, and the noose of evil-mindedness is snapped. ||12||<br>
  The Gurmukh wells up from, and then merges back into Truth.<br>
  He does not die and take birth, and is not consigned to reincarnation.<br>
  The Gurmukh remains forever imbued with the color of the Lord's Love. Night and day, he earns a profit. ||13||<br>
  The Gurmukhs, the devotees, are exalted and beautified in the Court of the Lord.<br>
  They are embellished with the True Word of His Bani, and the Word of the Shabad.<br>
  Night and day, they sing the Glorious Praises of the Lord, day and night, and they intuitively go to their own home. ||14||<br>
  The Perfect True Guru proclaims the Shabad;<br>
  night and day, remain lovingly attuned to devotional worship.<br>
  One who sings forever the Glorious Praises of the Lord, becomes immaculate; Immaculate are the Glorious Praises of the Sovereign Lord . ||15||<br>
  The True Lord is the Giver of virtue.<br>
  How rare are those who, as Gurmukh, understand this.<br>
  Servant Nanak praises the Naam; he blossoms forth in the ecstasy of the Name of the self-sufficient Lord. ||16||2||11||<br>
  Maaroo, Third Mehl:<br>
  Serve the Dear Lord, the inaccessible and infinite.<br>
  He has no end or limitation.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, one who dwells upon the Lord deep within his heart - his heart is filled with infinite wisdom. ||1||<br>
  The One Lord is pervading and permeating amidst all.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, He is revealed.<br>
  The Life of the world nurtures and cherishes all, giving sustenance to all. ||2||<br>
  The Perfect True Guru has imparted this understanding.<br>
  By the Hukam of His Command, He created the entire Universe.<br>
  Whoever submits to His Command, finds peace; His Command is above the heads of kings and emperors. ||3||<br>
  True is the True Guru. Infinite is the Word of His Shabad.<br>
  Through His Shabad, the world is saved.<br>
  The Creator Himself created the creation; He gazes upon it, and blesses it with breath and nourishment. ||4||<br>
  Out of millions, only a few understand.<br>
  Imbued with the Word of the Guru's Shabad, they are colored in His Love.<br>
  They praise the Lord, the Giver of peace forever; the Lord forgives His devotees, and blesses them with His Praise. ||5||<br>
  Those humble beings who serve the True Guru are true.<br>
  The falsest of the false die, only to be reborn.<br>
  The inaccessible, unfathomable, self-sufficient, incomprehensible Lord is the Lover of His devotees. ||6||<br>
  The Perfect True Guru implants Truth within.<br>
  Through the True Word of the Shabad, they sing His Glorious Praises forever.<br>
  The Giver of virtue is pervading deep within the nucleus of all beings; He inscribes the time of destiny upon each and every person's head. ||7||<br>
  The Gurmukh knows that God is always ever-present.<br>
  That humble being who serves the Shabad, is comforted and fulfilled.<br>
  Night and day, he serves the True Word of the Guru's Bani; he delights in the True Word of the Shabad. ||8||<br>
  The ignorant and blind cling to all sorts of rituals.<br>
  They stubborn-mindedly perform these rituals, and are consigned to reincarnation.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 068</h2></center>
  For the sake of poison, they act in greed and possessiveness, and evil-minded duality. ||9||<br>
  The Perfect True Guru implants devotional worship within.<br>
  Through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, he lovingly centers his consciousness on the Lord's Name.<br>
  The Lord pervades his mind, body and heart; deep within, his mind is drenched with devotional worship and praise of the Lord. ||10||<br>
  My True Lord God is the Destroyer of demons.<br>
  Through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, His devotees are saved.<br>
  My True Lord God is forever True. He is the Emperor over the heads of kings. ||11||<br>
  True are those devotees, who are pleasing to Your Mind.<br>
  They sing the Kirtan of His Praises at His Door; they are embellished and exalted by the Word of the Guru's Shabad.<br>
  Night and day, they sing the True Word of His Bani. The Naam is the wealth of the poor. ||12||<br>
  Those whom You unite, Lord, are never separated again.<br>
  Through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, they praise You forever.<br>
  You are the One Lord and Master over all. Through the Shabad, the Naam is praised. ||13||<br>
  Without the Shabad, no one knows You.<br>
  You Yourself speak the Unspoken Speech.<br>
  You Yourself are the Shabad forever, the Guru, the Great Giver; chanting the Lord's Name, You bestow Your treasure. ||14||<br>
  You Yourself are the Creator of the Universe.<br>
  No one can erase what You have written.<br>
  You Yourself bless the Gurmukh with the Naam, who is no longer skeptical, and is not held to account. ||15||<br>
  Your true devotees stand at the Door of Your Court.<br>
  They serve the Shabad with love and affection.<br>
  O Nanak, those who are attuned to the Naam remain detached; through the Naam, their affairs are resolved. ||16||3||12||<br>
  Maaroo, Third Mehl:<br>
  My True Lord God has staged a play.<br>
  He has created no one like anyone else.<br>
  He made them different, and he gazes upon them with pleasure; he placed all the flavors in the body. ||1||<br>
  You Yourself vibrate the beat of the breath.<br>
  Shiva and Shakti, energy and matter - You have placed them into the body.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, one turns away from the world, and attains the jewel of spiritual wisdom, and the Word of the Shabad. ||2||<br>
  He Himself created darkness and light.<br>
  He alone is pervasive; there is no other at all.<br>
  One who realizes his own self - by Guru's Grace, the lotus of his mind blossoms forth. ||3||<br>
  Only He Himself knows His depth and extent.<br>
  Other people can only listen and hear what is spoken and said.<br>
  One who is spiritually wise, understands himself as Gurmukh; he praises the True Lord. ||4||<br>
  Deep within the body is the priceless object.<br>
  He Himself opens the doors.<br>
  The Gurmukh intuitively drings in the Ambrosial Nectar, and the fire of desire is quenched. ||5||<br>
  He placed all the flavors within the body.<br>
  How rare are those who understand, through the Word of the Guru's Shabad.<br>
  So search within yourself, and praise the Shabad. Why run around outside your self? ||6||<br>
  Without tasting, no one enjoys the flavor.<br>
  Through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, one drinks in the Ambrosial Nectar.<br>
  The Ambrosial Nectar is drunk, and the immoral status is obtained, when one obtains the sublime essence of the Guru's Shabad. ||7||<br>
  One who realizes himself, knows all virtues.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 069</h2></center>
  Through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, he chants the Name of the Lord.<br>

  Maaroo, Third Mehl:<br>
  The One Lord is eternal and unchanging, forever True.<br>
  Through the Perfect Guru, this understanding is obtained.<br>
  Those who are drenched with the sublime essence of the Lord, meditate forever on Him; following the Guru's Teachings, they obtain the armor of humility. ||1||<br>
  Deep within, they love the True Lord forever.<br>
  Through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, they love the Lord's Name.<br>
  The Naam, the embodiment of the nine treasures, abides within their hearts; they renounce the profit of Maya. ||2||<br>
  Both the king and his subjects are involved in evil-mindedness and duality.<br>
  Without serving the True Guru, they do not become one with the Lord.<br>
  Those who meditate on the One Lord find eternal peace. Their power is eternal and unfailing. ||3||<br>
  No one can save them from coming and going.<br>
  Birth and death come from Him.<br>
  The Gurmukh meditates forever on the True Lord. Emancipation and liberation are obtained from Him. ||4||<br>
  Truth and self-control are found through the Door of the True Guru.<br>
  Egotism and anger are silenced through the Shabad.<br>
  Serving the True Guru, lasting peace is found; humility and contentment all come from Him. ||5||<br>
  Out of egotism and attachment, the Universe welled up.<br>
  Forgetting the Naam, the Name of the Lord, all the world perishes.<br>
  Without serving the True Guru, the Naam is not obtained. The Naam is the True profit in this world. ||6||<br>
  True is His Will, beauteous and pleasing through the Word of the Shabad.<br>
  The Panch Shabad, the five primal sounds, vibrate and resonate.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 070</h2></center>
  Through the True Name, one's actions are forever embellished. Without the Shabad, what can anyone do? ||7||<br>
  One instant, he laughs, and the next instant, he cries.<br>
  Because of duality and evil-mindedness, his affairs are not resolved.<br>
  Union and separation are pre-ordained by the Creator. Actions already committed cannot be taken back. ||8||<br>
  One who lives the Word of the Guru's Shabad becomes Jivan Mukta - liberated while yet alive.<br>
  He remains forever immersed in the Lord.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, one is blessed with glorious greatness; he is not afflicted by the disease of egotism. ||9||<br>
  Eating tasty delicacies, he fattens up his body<br>

  God is within his own heart, but he does not recognize the Word of the Shabad.<br>

  Those who forsake the object within their own hearts, wander outside.<br>
  The blind, self-willed manmukhs do not taste the flavor of God.<br>

  The self-willed manmukh has doubt as his spouse.<br>
  He dies of evil-mindedness, and suffers forever.<br>
  His mind is attached to sexual desire, anger and duality, and he does not find peace, even in dreams. ||13||<br>

  Maaroo, Third Mehl:<br>
  The Gurmukh contemplates the sound current of the Naad instead of the Vedas.<br>

 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 071</h2></center>
  One who becomes Gurmukh understands.<br>
  He rids himself of egotism, Maya and doubt.<br>

  They act in harmony with the Mind of the True Lord. ||9||<br>

  Wearing all sorts of religious robes, they do not please the Lord.<br>
  Tinged by corruption, they earn only pain; they are immersed in pain. ||11||<br>

  He comes to understand death and birth.<br>
  One who looks alike upon death and birth, is pleasing to my God. ||12||<br>
  The Gurmukh, while remaining dead, is respected and approved.<br>
  He realizes that coming and going are according to God's Will.<br>

  He Himself fashioned the Universe, through the Hukam of His Command.<br>

  The body takes the form of a fortress.<br>

  He alone is pure, who eradicates anger.<br>
  He realizes the Shabad, and reforms himself.<br>
  The Creator Himself acts, and inspires all to act; He Himself abides in the mind. ||5||<br>

  The mind and body are washed clean, contemplating the Shabad.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 072</h2></center>
  One who remains forever imbued with His Love, night and day - in His Mercy, the Lord inspires him to perform devotional worship service. ||6||<br>
  In this temple of the mind, the mind wanders around.<br>
  Discarding joy like straw, it suffers in terrible pain.<br>
  Without meeting the True Guru, it finds no place of rest; He Himself has staged this play. ||7||<br>
  He Himself is infinite; He contemplates Himself.<br>
  He Himself bestows Union through actions of excellence.<br>
  What can the poor creatures do? Granting forgiveness, He unites them with Himself. ||8||<br>
  The Perfect Lord Himself unites them with the True Guru.<br>
  Through the True Word of the Shabad, he makes them brave spiritual heroes.<br>

  The treasure of the Naam abides deep within their hearts; they meditate on the Naam with their tongues. ||10||<br>
  He wanders through foreign lands, but does not look within himself.<br>

  The noose of death around his neck will never be untied; in the love of duality, he wanders in reincarnation. ||11||<br>
  There is no real chanting, meditation, penance or self-control,<br>
  as long as one does not live to the Word of the Guru's Shabad.<br>
  Accepting the Word of the Guru's Shabad, one obtains Truth; through Truth, one merges in the True Lord. ||12||<br>
  Sexual desire and anger are very powerful in the world.<br>
  They lead to all sorts of actions, but these only add to all the pain.<br>
  Those who serve the True Guru find peace; they are united with the True Shabad. ||13||<br>
  Air, water and fire make up the body.<br>
  Emotional attachment to Maya rules deep within all.<br>
  When one realizes the One who created him, emotional attachment to Maya is dispelled. ||14||<br>
  Some are engrossed in emotional attachment to Maya and pride.<br>
  They are self-conceited and egotistical.<br>
  They never think about the Messenger of Death; in the end, they leave, regretting and repenting. ||15||<br>
  He alone knows the Way, who created it.<br>
  The Gurmukh, who is blessed with the Shabad, realizes Him.<br>
  Slave Nanak offers ths prayer; O Lord, let my consciousness be attached to the True Name. ||16||2||16||<br>
  Maaroo, Third Mehl:<br>
  From the very beginning of time, and throughout the ages, the Merciful Lord has been the Great Giver.<br>
  Through the Shabad, the Word of the Perfect Guru, He is realized.<br>
  Those who serve You are immersed in You. You unite them in Union with Yourself. ||1||<br>
  You are inaccessible and unfathomable; Your limits cannot be found.<br>
  All beings and creatures seek Your Sanctuary.<br>
  As is pleases Your Will, You guide us along; You Yourself place us on the Path. ||2||<br>
  The True Lord is, and shall always be.<br>
  He Himself creates - there is no other at all.<br>
  The Giver of peace takes care of all; He Himself sustains them. ||3||<br>
  You are inaccessible, unfathomable, invisible and infinite;<br>
  no one knows Your extent.<br>
  You Yourself realize Yourself. Through the Guru's Teachings, You reveal Yourself. ||4||<br>
  Your Almighty Command prevails throughout the nether worlds, realms and worlds of form.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 073</h2></center>
  By the Hukam of Your Command, You create, and by Your Command, You destroy. By Your Command, You unite in Union. ||5||<br>
  One who realizes Your Command, praises Your Command.<br>
  You are Inaccessible, Unfathomable and Self-Sufficient.<br>
  As is the understanding You give, so do I become. You Yourself reveal the Shabad. ||6||<br>
  Night and day, the days of our lives wear away.<br>
  Night and day both bear witness to this loss.<br>
  The blind, foolish, self-willed manmukh is not aware of this; death is hovering over his head. ||7||<br>
  The mind and body are cooled and soothed, holding tight to the Guru's Feet.<br>

  One is in bliss forever, singing the Glorious Praises of the True Lord, and speaking the True Word of His Bani. ||8||<br>
  One who knows You as the Architect of Karma,<br>

  But if they are blessed by God's Grace, they serve the True Guru, and easily obtain peace. ||10||<br>
  He Himself created the 8.4 million species of beings.<br>
  Only in this human life, is devotional worship to the Guru implanted within.<br>
  Without devotion, one lives in manure; he falls into manure again and again. ||11||<br>
  If one is blessed with His Grace, devotional worship to the Guru is implanted within.<br>
  Without God's Grace, how can anyone find Him?<br>
  The Creator Himself acts, and inspires all to act; as He wills, he leads us on. ||12||<br>
  The Simritees and the Shaastras do not know His limits.<br>
  The blind fool does not recognize the essence of reality.<br>
  The Creator Himself acts, and inspires all to act; He Himself deludes with doubt. ||13||<br>
  He Himself causes everything to be done.<br>
  He Himself joins each and every person to his tasks.<br>
  He Himself establishes and disestablishes, and watches over all; He reveals Himself to the Gurmukh. ||14||<br>
  The True Lord and Master is profoundly deep and unfathomable.<br>
  Praising Him forever, the mind is comforted and consoled.<br>
  He is inaccessible and unfathomable; His value cannot be estimated. He dwells in the mind of the Gurmukh. ||15||<br>
  He Himself is detached; all others are entangled in their affairs.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, one comes to understand Him.<br>
  O Nanak, the Naam, the Name of the Lord, comes to dwell deep within the heart; through the Guru's Teachings, one is united in His Union. ||16||3||17||<br>
  Maaroo, Third Mehl:<br>
  For thirty-six ages, utter darkness prevailed.<br>
  Only You Yourself know this, O Creator Lord.<br>
  What can anyone else say? What can anyone explain? Only You Yourself can estimate Your worth. ||1||<br>
  The One Universal Creator created the entire Universe.<br>
  All the plays and dramas are to Your glory and greatness.<br>
  The True Lord Himself makes all distinctions; He Himself breaks and builds. ||2||<br>
  The Juggler has staged His juggling show.<br>
  Through the Perfect Guru, one comes to behold it.<br>
  One who remains forever detached in the Word of the Guru's Shabad - his consciousness is attuned to the True Lord. ||3||<br>
  The musical instruments of the body vibrate and resound.<br>
  The Player Himself plays them.<br>
  The breath flows equally through the hearts of each and every being. Receiving the breath, all the instruments sing. ||4||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 074</h2></center>
  Whatever the Creator does, surely comes to pass.<br>
  Through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, egotism is consumed.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, some are blessed with glorious greatness; they meditate on the Naam, the Name of the Lord. ||5||<br>
  There is no other profit as great as service to the Guru.<br>
  The Naam abides within my mind, and I praise the Naam.<br>
  The Naam is forever the Giver of peace. Through the Naam, we earn the profit. ||6||<br>
  Without the Name, all the world suffers in misery.<br>
  The more actions one does, the more the corruption increases.<br>
  Without serving the Naam, how can anyone find peace? Without the Naam, one suffers in pain. ||7||<br>
  He Himself acts, and inspires all to act.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, He reveals Himself to a few.<br>
  One who becomes Gurmukh breaks his bonds, and attains the home of liberation. ||8||<br>
  One who calculates his accounts, burns in the world.<br>
  His skepticism and corruption are never dispelled.<br>
  One who becomes Gurmukh abandons his calculations; through Truth, we merge in the True Lord. ||9||<br>
  If God grants Truth, then we may attain it.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, it is revealed.<br>
  One who praises the True Name, and remains imbued with the Lord's Love, by Guru's Grace, finds peace. ||10||<br>
  The Beloved Naam, the Name of the Lord, is chanting, meditation, penance and self-control.<br>
  God, the Destroyer, destroys sins.<br>
  Through the Name of the Lord, the body and mind are cooled and soothed, and one is intuitively, easily absorbed into the Celestial Lord. ||11||<br>
  With greed within them, their minds are filthy, and they spread filth around.<br>
  They do filthy deeds, and suffer in pain.<br>
  They deal in falsehood, and nothing but falsehood; telling lies, they suffer in pain. ||12||<br>
  Rare is that person who enshrines the Immaculate Bani of the Guru's Word within his mind.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, his skepticism is removed.<br>
  He walks in harmony with the Guru's Will, day and night; remembering the Naam, the Name of the Lord, he finds peace. ||13||<br>
  The True Lord Himself is the Creator.<br>
  He Himself creates and destroys.<br>
  One who becomes Gurmukh, praises the Lord forever. Meeting the True Lord, he finds peace. ||14||<br>
  Making countless efforts, sexual desire is not overcome.<br>
  Everyone is burning in the fires of sexuality and anger.<br>
  Serving the True Guru, one brings his mind under control; conquering his mind, he merges in the Mind of God. ||15||<br>
  You Yourself created the sense of 'mine' and 'yours.'<br>
  All creatures are Yours; You created all beings.<br>
  O Nanak, contemplate the Naam forever; through the Guru's Teachings, the Lord abides in the mind. ||16||4||18||<br>
  Maaroo, Third Mehl:<br>
  The Dear Lord is the Giver, inaccessible and unfathomable.<br>
  He does not have even an iota of greed; He is self-sufficient.<br>
  No one can reach up to Him; He Himself unites in His Union. ||1||<br>
  Whatever He does, surely comes to pass.<br>
  There is no other Giver, except for Him.<br>
  Whoever the Lord blesses with His gift, obtains it. Through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, He unites him with Himself. ||2||<br>
  The fourteen worlds are Your markets.<br>
  The True Guru reveals them, along with one's inner being.<br>
  One who deals in the Name, through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, obtains it. ||3||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 075</h2></center>
  Serving the True Guru, one obtains intuitive bliss.<br>
  The Lord of the Universe comes to dwell within the heart.<br>
  He intuitively practices devotional worship day and night; God Himself practices devotional worship. ||4||<br>
  Those who are separated from the True Guru, suffer in misery.<br>
  Night and day, they are punished, and they suffer in total agony.<br>
  Their faces are blackened, and they do not obtain the Mansion of the Lord's Presence. They suffer in sorrow and agony. ||5||<br>
  Those who serve the True Guru are very fortunate.<br>
  They intuitively enshrine love for the True Lord.<br>
  They practice Truth, forever Truth; they are united in Union with the True Lord. ||6||<br>
  He alone obtains the Truth, unto whom the True Lord gives it.<br>
  His inner being is filled with Truth, and his doubt is dispelled.<br>
  The True Lord Himself is the Giver of Truth; he alone obtains the Truth, unto whom He gives it. ||7||<br>
  He Himself is the Creator of all.<br>
  Only one whom He instructs, understands Him.<br>
  He Himself forgives, and grants glorious greatness. He himself unites in His Union. ||8||<br>
  Acting egotistically, one loses his life.<br>
  Even in the world hereafter, emotioal attachment to Maya does not leave him.<br>
  In the world hereafter, the Messenger of Death calls him to account, and crushes him like sesame seeds in the oil-press. ||9||<br>
  By perfect destiny, one serves the Guru.<br>
  If God grants His Grace, then one serves.<br>
  The Messenger of Death cannot even approach him, and in the Mansion of the True Lord's Presence, he finds peace. ||10||<br>
  They alone find peace, who are pleasing to Your Will.<br>
  By perfect destiny, they are attached to the Guru's service.<br>
  All glorious greatness rests in Your Hands; he alone obtains it, unto whom You give it. ||11||<br>
  Through the Guru, one's inner being is enlightened and illumined.<br>
  The wealth of the Naam, the Name of the Lord, comes to dwell in the mind.<br>
  The jewel of spiritual wisdom ever illumines the heart, and the darkness of spiritual ignorance is dispelled. ||12||<br>
  The blind and ignorant are attached to duality.<br>
  The unfortunates are drowned without water, and die.<br>
  When they depart from the world, they do not find the Lord's door and home; bound and gagged at Death's door, they suffer in pain. ||13||<br>
  Without serving the True Guru, no one finds liberation.<br>
  Go ask any spiritual teacher or meditator.<br>
  Whoever serves the True Guru is blessed with glorious greatness, and honored in the Court of the True Lord. ||14||<br>
  One who serves the True Guru, the Lord merges into Himself.<br>
  Cutting away attachment, one lovingly focuses on the True Lord.<br>
  The merchants deal forever in Truth; they earn the profit of the Naam. ||15||<br>
  The Creator Himself acts, and inspires all to act.<br>
  He alone is liberated, who dies in the Word of the Shabad.<br>
  O Nanak, the Naam dwells deep within the mind; meditate on the Naam, the Name of the Lord. ||16||5||19||<br>
  Maaroo, Third Mehl:<br>
  Whatever You do, is done.<br>
  How rare are those who walk in harmony with the Lord's Will.<br>
  One who surrenders to the Lord's Will finds peace; he finds peace in the Lord's Will. ||1||<br>
  Your Will is pleasing to the Gurmukh.<br>
  Practicing Truth, he intuitively finds peace.<br>
  Many long to walk in harmony with the Lord's Will; He Himself inspires us to surrender to His Will. ||2||<br>
  One who surrenders to Your Will, meets with You, Lord.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 076</h2></center>
  One who is pleased with Your Will is immersed in You.<br>
  Glorious greatness rests in God's Will; rare are those who accept it. ||3||<br>
  When it pleases His Will, He leads us to meet the Guru.<br>
  The Gurmukh finds the treasure of the Naam, the Name of the Lord.<br>
  By Your Will, You created the whole Universe; those whom You bless with Your favor are pleased with Your Will. ||4||<br>
  The blind, self-willed manmukhs practice cleverness.<br>
  They do not surrender to the Lord's Will, and suffer terrible pain.<br>
  Deluded by doubt, they come and go in reincarnation; they never find the Mansion of the Lord's Presence. ||5||<br>
  The True Guru brings Union, and grants glorious greatness.<br>
  The Primal Lord ordained service to the True Guru.<br>
  Serving the True Guru, the Naam is obtained. Through the Naam, one finds peace. ||6||<br>
  Everything wells up from the Naam, and through the Naam, perishes.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, the mind and body are pleased with the Naam.<br>
  Meditating on the Naam, the tongue is drenched with the Lord's sublime essence. Through this essence, the Essence is obtained. ||7||<br>
  Rare are those who find the Mansion of the Lord's Presence within the mansion of their own body.<br>
  Through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, they lovingly focus their consciousness on the True Lord.<br>
  Whoever the Lord blesses with Truth obtains Truth; he merges in Truth, and only Truth. ||8||<br>
  Forgetting the Naam, the Name of the Lord, the mind and body suffer in pain.<br>
  Attached to the love of Maya, he earns nothing but disease.<br>
  Without the Name, his mind and body are afflicted with leprosy, and he obtains his home in hell. ||9||<br>
  Those who are imbued with the Naam - their bodies are immaculate and pure.<br>
  Their soul-swan is immaculate, and in the Lord's Love, they find eternal peace.<br>
  Praising the Naam, they find eternal peace, and dwell in the home of their own inner being. ||10||<br>
  Everyone deals and trades.<br>
  Without the Name, all the world loses.<br>
  Naked they come, and naked they go; without the Name, they suffer in pain. ||11||<br>
  He alone obtains the Naam, unto whom the Lord gives it.<br>
  Through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, the Lord comes to dwell in the mind.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, the Naam dwells deep within the heart, and one meditates upon the Naam, the Name of the Lord. ||12||<br>
  Everyone who comes into the world, longs for the Name.<br>
  They alone are blessed with the Name, whose past actions were so ordained by the Primal Lord.<br>
  Those who obtain the Name are very fortunate. Through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, they are united with God. ||13||<br>
  Utterly incomparable is the fortress of the body.<br>
  Within it, God sits in contemplation.<br>
  He administers true justice, and trades in Truth; through Him, one finds the eternal, unchanging dwelling. ||14||<br>
  Deep within the inner self are glorious homes and beautiful places.<br>
  But rare is that person who, as Gurmukh, finds these places.<br>
  If one stays in these places, and praises the True Lord, the True Lord comes to dwell in the mind. ||15||<br>
  My Creator Lord has formed this formation.<br>
  He has placed everything within this body.<br>
  O Nanak, those who deal in the Naam are imbued with His Love. The Gurmukh obtains the Naam, the Name of the Lord. ||16||6||20||<br>
  Maaroo, Third Mehl:<br>
  Contemplating the Word of the Shabad, the body becomes golden.<br>
  The Lord abides there; He has no end or limitation.<br>
  Night and day, serve the Lord, and chant the True Word of the Guru's Bani. Through the Shabad, meet the Dear Lord. ||1||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 077</h2></center>
  I am a sacrifice to those who remember the Lord.<br>
  Through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, I unite in Union with the Lord.<br>
  I touch the dust of their feet to my face and forehead; sitting in the Society of the Saints, I sing His Glorious Praises. ||2||<br>
  I sing the Glorious Praises of the Lord, as I am pleasing to the Lord God.<br>
  With the Lord's Name deep within my inner being, I am adorned with the Word of the Shabad.<br>
  The Word of the Guru's Bani is heard throughout the four corners of the world; through it, we merge in the True Name. ||3||<br>
  That humble being, who searches within himself, through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, sees the Lord with his eyes.<br>
  Through the Guru's Shabad, he applies the ointment of spiritual wisdom to his eyes; the Gracious Lord, in His Grace, unites him with Himself. ||4||<br>
  By great good fortune, I obtained this body;<br>
  in this human life, I have focused my consciousness on the Word of the Shabad.<br>
  Without the Shabad, everything is enveloped in utter darkness; only the Gurmukh understands. ||5||<br>
  Some merely waste away their lives - why have they even come into the world?<br>
  The self-willed manmukhs are attached to the love of duality.<br>
  This opportunity shall not into their hands again; their foot slips, and they come to regret and repent. ||6||<br>
  Through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, the body is sanctified.<br>
  The True Lord, the ocean of virtue, dwells within it.<br>
  One who sees the Truest of the True everywhere, hears the Truth, and enshrines it within his mind. ||7||<br>
  Egotism and mental calculations are relieved through the Word of the Guru's Shabad.<br>
  Keep the Dear Lord close, and enshrine Him in your heart.<br>
  One who praises the Lord forever, through the Guru's Shabad, meets with the True Lord, and finds peace. ||8||<br>
  He alone remembers the Lord, whom the Lord inspires to remember.<br>
  Through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, He comes to dwell in the mind.<br>
  He Himself sees, and He Himself understands; He merges all into Himself. ||9||<br>
  He alone knows, who has placed the object within his mind.<br>
  Through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, he comes to understand himself.<br>
  That humble being who understands himself is immaculate. He proclaims the Guru's Bani, and the Word of the Shabad. ||10||<br>
  This body is sanctified and purified;<br>
  through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, it contemplates the Lord, the ocean of virtue.<br>
  One who chants the Glorious Praises of the Lord night and day, and remains attuned to His Love, chants His Glorious Virtues, immersed in the Glorious Lord. ||11||<br>
  This body is the source of all Maya;<br>
  in love with duality, it is deluded by doubt.<br>
  It does not remember the Lord, and suffers in eternal pain. Without remembering the Lord, it suffers in pain. ||12||<br>
  One who serves the True Guru is approved and respected.<br>
  His body and soul-swan are immaculate and pure; in the Court of the Lord, he is known to be true.<br>
  He serves the Lord, and enshrines the Lord in his mind; he is exalted, singing the Glorious Praises of the Lord. ||13||<br>
  Without good destiny, no one can serve the True Guru.<br>
  The self-willed manmukhs are deluded, and die weeping and wailing.<br>
  Those who are blessed by the Guru's Glance of Grace - the Dear Lord unites them with Himself. ||14||<br>
  In the body fortress, are the solidly-constructed markets.<br>
  The Gurmukh purchases the object, and takes care of it.<br>
  Meditating on the Name of the Lord, day and night, he attains the sublime, exalted status. ||15||<br>
  The True Lord Himself is the Giver of peace.<br>
  Through the Shabad of the Perfect Guru, He is realized.<br>
  Nanak praises the Naam, the True Name of the Lord; through perfect destiny, He is found. ||16||7||21||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 078</h2></center>
  Maaroo, Third Mehl:<br>
  The Formless Lord created the universe of form.<br>
  By the Hukam of His Command, He created attachment to Maya.<br>
  The Creator Himself stages all the plays; hearing of the True Lord, enshrine Him in your mind. ||1||<br>
  Maya, the mother, gave birth to the three gunas, the three qualities,<br>
  and proclaimed the four Vedas to Brahma.<br>
  Creating the years, months, days and dates, He infused intelligence into the world. ||2||<br>
  Service to the Guru is the most excellent action.<br>
  Enshrine the Lord's Name within your heart.<br>
  The Word of the Guru's Bani prevails throughout the world; through this Bani, the Lord's Name is obtained. ||3||<br>
  He reads the Vedas, but he starts arguments night and day.<br>
  He does not remember the Naam, the Name of the Lord; he is bound and gagged by the Messenger of Death.<br>
  In the love of duality, he suffers in pain forever; he is deluded by doubt, and confused by the three gunas. ||4||<br>
  The Gurmukh is in love with the One Lord alone;<br>
  he submerges in his mind the three-phased desire.<br>
  Through the True Word of the Shabad, he is liberated forever; he renounces emotional attachment to Maya. ||5||<br>
  Those who are so pre-ordained to be imbued, are imbued with love for the Lord.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, they are intuitively intoxicated.<br>
  Serving the True Guru forever, they find God; He Himself unites them with Himself. ||6||<br>
  In attachment to Maya and doubt, the Lord is not found.<br>
  Attached to the love of duality, one suffers in pain.<br>
  The crimson color lasts for only a few days; all too soon, it fades away. ||7||<br>
  So color this mind in the Fear and the Love of God.<br>
  Dyed in this color, one merges in the True Lord.<br>
  By perfect destiny, some may obtain this color. Through the Guru's Teachings, this color is applied. ||8||<br>
  The self-willed manmukhs take great pride in themselves.<br>
  In the Court of the Lord, they are never honored.<br>
  Attached to duality, they waste their lives; without understanding, they suffer in pain. ||9||<br>
  My God has hidden Himself deep within the self.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, one is united in the Lord's Union.<br>
  God is True, and True is His trade, through which the priceless Naam is obtained. ||10||<br>
  No one has found this body's value.<br>
  My Lord and Master has worked His handiwork.<br>
  One who becomes Gurmukh purifies his body, and then the Lord unites him with Himself. ||11||<br>
  Within the body, one loses, and within the body, one wins.<br>
  The Gurmukh seeks the self-sustaining Lord.<br>
  The Gurmukh trades, and finds peace forever; he intuitively merges in the Celestial Lord. ||12||<br>
  True is the Lord's Mansion, and True is His treasure.<br>
  The Great Giver Himself gives.<br>
  The Gurmukh praises the Giver of peace; his mind is united with the Lord, and he comes to know His worth. ||13||<br>
  Within the body is the object; its value cannot be estimated.<br>
  He Himself grants glorious greatness to the Gurmukh.<br>
  He alone knows this object, to whom this store belongs; the Gurmukh is blessed with it, and does not come to regret. ||14||<br>
  The Dear Lord is pervading and permeating all.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, He is found.<br>
  He Himself unites in His Union; through the Word of the Shabad, one intuitively merges with Him. ||15||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 079</h2></center>
  The True Lord Himself unites us in the Word of His Shabad.<br>
  Within the Shabad, doubt is driven out.<br>
  O Nanak, He blesses us with His Naam, and throgh the Naam, peace is found. ||16||8||22||<br>
  Maaroo, Third Mehl:<br>
  He is inaccessible, unfathomable and self-sustaining.<br>
  He Himself is merciful, inaccessible and unlimited.<br>
  No one can reach up to Him; through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, He is met. ||1||<br>
  He alone serves You, who pleases You.<br>
  Through the Guru's Shabad, he merges in the True Lord.<br>
  Night and day, he chants the Lord's Praises, day and night; his tongue savors and delights in the sublime essence of the Lord. ||2||<br>
  Those who die in the Shabad - their death is exalted and glorified.<br>
  They enshrine the Lord's Glories in their hearts.<br>
  Holding tight to the Guru's feet, their lives becomes prosperous, and they are rid of the love of duality. ||3||<br>
  The Dear Lord unites them in Union with Himself.<br>
  Through the Guru's Shabad, self-conceit is dispelled.<br>
  Those who remain attuned to devotional worship to the Lord, night and day, earn the profit in this world. ||4||<br>
  What Glorious Virtues of Yours should I describe? I cannot describe them.<br>
  You have no end or limitation. Your value cannot be estimated.<br>
  When the Giver of peace Himself bestows His Mercy, the virtuous are absorbed in virtue. ||5||<br>
  In this world, emotional attachment is spread all over.<br>
  The ignorant, self-willed manmukh is immersed in utter darkness.<br>
  Chasing after worldly affairs, he wastes away his life in vain; without the Name, he suffers in pain. ||6||<br>
  If God grants His Grace, then one finds the True Guru.<br>
  Through the Shabad, the filth of egotism is burned away.<br>
  The mind becomes immaculate, and the jewel of spiritual wisdom brings enlightenment; the darkness of spiritual ignorance is dispelled. ||7||<br>
  Your Names are countless; Your value cannot be estimated.<br>
  I enshrine the Lord's True Name within my heart.<br>
  Who can estimate Your value, God? You are immersed and absorbed in Yourself. ||8||<br>
  The Naam, the Name of the Lord, is priceless, inaccessible and infinite.<br>
  No one can weigh it.<br>
  You Yourself weigh, and estimate all; through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, You unite, when the weight is perfect. ||9||<br>
  Your servant serves, and offers this prayer.<br>
  Please, let me sit near You, and unite me with Yourself.<br>
  You are the Giver of peace to all beings; by perfect karma, we meditate on You. ||10||<br>
  Chastity, truth and self-control come by practicing and living the Truth.<br>
  This mind becomes immaculate and pure, singing the Glorious Praises of the Lord.<br>
  In this world of poison, the Ambrosial Nectar is obtained, if it pleases my Dear Lord. ||11||<br>
  He alone understands, whom God inspires to understand.<br>
  Singing the Glorious Praises of the Lord, one's inner being is awakened.<br>
  Egotism and possessiveness are silenced and subdued, and one intuitively finds the True Lord. ||12||<br>
  Without good karma, countless others wander around.<br>
  They die, and die again, only to be reborn; they cannot escape the cycle of reincarnation.<br>
  Imbued with poison, they practice poison and corruption, and they never find peace. ||13||<br>
  Many disguise themselves with religious robes.<br>
  Without the Shabad, no one has conquered egotism.<br>
  One who remains dead while yet alive is liberated, and merges in the True Name. ||14||<br>
  Spiritual ignorance and desire burn this human body.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 080</h2></center>
  He alone puts out this fire, who practices and lives the Guru's Shabad.<br>
  His body and mind are cooled and soothed, and his anger is silenced; conquering egotism, he merges in the Lord. ||15||<br>
  True is the Lord and Master, and True is His glorious greatness.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, a rare few attain this.<br>
  Nanak offers this one prayer: through the Naam, the Name of the Lord, may I merge in the Lord. ||16||1||23||<br>
  Maaroo, Third Mehl:<br>
  By Your Grace, please unite with Your devotees.<br>
  Your devotees ever praise You, lovingly focusing on You.<br>
  In Your Sanctuary, they are saved, O Creator Lord; You unite them in Union with Yourself. ||1||<br>
  Sublime and exalted is devotion to the Perfect Word of the Shabad.<br>
  Peace prevails within; they are pleasing to Your Mind.<br>
  One whose mind and body are imbued with true devotion, focuses his consciousness on the True Lord. ||2||<br>
  In egotism, the body is forever burning.<br>
  When God grants His Grace, one meets the Perfect Guru.<br>
  The Shabad dispels the spiritual ignorance within, and through the True Guru, one finds peace. ||3||<br>
  The blind, self-willed manmukh acts blindly.<br>
  He is in terrible trouble, and wanders in reincarnation.<br>
  He can never snap the noose of Death, and in the end, he suffers in horrible pain. ||4||<br>
  Through the Shabad, one's comings and goings in reincarnation are ended.<br>
  He keeps the True Name enshrined within his heart.<br>
  He dies in the Word of the Guru's Shabad, and conquers his mind; stilling his egotism, he merges in the Lord. ||5||<br>
  Coming and going, the people of the world are wasting away.<br>
  Without the True Guru, no one finds permanence and stability.<br>
  The Shabad shines its Light deep within the self, and one dwells in peace; one's light merges into the Light. ||6||<br>
  The five demons think of evil and corruption.<br>
  The expanse is the manifestation of emotional attachment to Maya.<br>
  Serving the True Guru, one is liberated, and the five demons are put under his control. ||7||<br>
  Without the Guru, there is only the darkness of attachment.<br>
  Over and over, time and time again, they are drowned.<br>
  Meeting the True Guru, Truth is implanted within, and the True Name becomes pleasing to the mind. ||8||<br>
  True is His Door, and True is His Court, His Royal Darbaar.<br>
  The true ones serve Him, through the Beloved Word of the Shabad.<br>
  Singing the Glorious Praises of the True Lord, in the true melody, I am immersed and absorbed in Truth. ||9||<br>
  Deep within the home of the self, one finds the home of the Lord.<br>
  Through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, one easily, intuitively finds it.<br>
  There, one is not afflicted with sorrow or separation; merge into the Celestial Lord with intuitive ease. ||10||<br>
  The evil people live in the love of duality.<br>
  They wander around, totally attached and thirsty.<br>
  They sit in evil gatherings, and suffer in pain forever; they earn pain, nothing but pain. ||11||<br>
  Without the True Guru, there is no Sangat, no Congregation.<br>
  Without the Shabad, no one can cross over to the other side.<br>
  One who intuitively chants God's Glorious Praises day and night - his light merges into the Light. ||12||<br>
  The body is the tree; the bird of the soul dwells within it.<br>
  It drinks in the Ambrosial Nectar, resting in the Word of the Guru's Shabad.<br>
  It never flies away, and it does not come or go; it dwells within the home of its own self. ||13||<br>
  Purify the body, and contemplate the Shabad.<br>
  Remove the poisonous drug of emotional attachment, and eradicate doubt.<br>
  The Giver of peace Himself bestows His Mercy, and unites us in Union with Himself. ||14||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 081</h2></center>
  He is always near at hand; He is never far away.<br>
  Through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, realize that He is very near.<br>
  Your heart-lotus shall blossom forth, and the ray of God's Divine Light shall illuminate your heart; He shall be revealed to You. ||15||<br>
  The True Lord is Himself the Creator.<br>
  He Himself kills, and gives life; there is no other at all.<br>
  O Nanak, through the Naam, the Name of the Lord, glorious greatness is obtained. Eradicating self-conceit, peace is found. ||16||2||24||<br>
  Maaroo, Solahas, Fourth Mehl:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  The Lord Lord Himself is the One who exalts and embellishes.<br>
  Do not consider any other work.<br>
  The True Lord abides deep within the heart of the Gurmukh, who intuitively merges in the True Lord. ||1||<br>
  The True Lord dwells within the minds of all.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, they are intuitively absorbed in Him.<br>
  Calling out, "Guru, Guru", I have found eternal peace; my consciousness is focused on the Guru's feet. ||2||<br>
  The True Guru is spiritual wisdom; the True Guru is worship and adoration.<br>
  I serve the True Guru, and no other.<br>
  From the True Guru, I have obtained the wealth, the jewel of the Naam. Service to the True Guru is pleasing to me. ||3||<br>
  Without the True Guru, those who are attached to duality<br>
  come and go, and wander in reincarnation; these unfortunate ones die.<br>
  O Nanak, even after they are emancipated, those who become Gurmukh remain in the Guru's Sanctuary. ||4||<br>
  The love of the Gurmukh is forever true.<br>
  I beg for the invaluable Naam, the Name of the Lord, from the Guru.<br>
  O Dear Lord, please be kind, and grant Your Grace; please keep me in the Guru's Sanctuary. ||5||<br>
  The True Guru trickles the Ambrosial Nectar into my mouth.<br>
  My Tenth Gate has been opened and revealed.<br>
  The unstruck sound current of the Shabad vibrates and resounds there, with the melody of the Guru's Bani; one is easily, intuitively absorbed in the Lord. ||6||<br>
  Those who are so pre-ordained by the Creator,<br>
  pass their nights and days calling on the Guru.<br>
  Without the True Guru, no one understands; focus your consciousness on the Guru's Feet. ||7||<br>
  The Lord Himself blesses those with whom He is pleased.<br>
  The Gurmukh receives the wealth of the Naam.<br>
  When the Lord grants His Grace, He bestows the Naam; Nanak is immersed and absorbed in the Naam. ||8||<br>
  The jewel of spiritual wisdom is revealed within the mind.<br>
  The wealth of the Naam is easily, intuitively received.<br>
  This glorious greatness is obtained from the Guru; I am forever a sacrifice to the True Guru. ||9||<br>
  With the rising of the sun, the darkness of the night is dispelled.<br>
  Spiritual ignorance is eradicated, by the priceless jewel of the Guru.<br>
  The True Guru is the fantastically valuable jewel of spiritual wisdom; blessed by God's Mercy, peace is found. ||10||<br>
  The Gurmukh obtains the Naam, and his good reputation increases.<br>
  In all four ages he is considered to be pure and good.<br>
  Imbued with the Naam, the Name of the Lord, he finds peace. He remains lovingly focused on the Naam. ||11||<br>
  The Gurmukh receives the Naam.<br>
  In intuitive peace he wakes, and in intuitive peace he sleeps.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 082</h2></center>
  The Gurmukh is immersed and absorbed in the Naam; Nanak meditates on the Naam. ||12||<br>
  The Ambrosial Nectar of the Guru's Bani is in the mouth of the devotees.<br>
  The Gurmukhs chant and repeat the Lord's Name.<br>
  Chanting the Name of the Lord, Har, Har, their minds forever blossom forth; they focus their minds on the Lord's Feet. ||13||<br>
  I am foolish and ignorant; I have no wisdom at all.<br>
  From the True Guru, I have obtained understanding in my mind.<br>
  O Dear Lord, please be kind to me, and grant Your Grace; let me be committed to serving the True Guru. ||14||<br>
  Those who know the True Guru realize the One Lord.<br>
  The Giver of peace is all-pervading, permeating everywhere.<br>
  Understanding my own soul, I have obtained the Supreme Status; my awareness is immersed in selfless service. ||15||<br>
  Those who are blessed with glorious greatness by the Primal Lord God<br>
  are lovingly focused on the True Guru, who dwells within their minds.<br>
  The Giver of life to the world Himself meets them; O Nanak, they are absorbed in His Being. ||16||1||<br>
  Maaroo, Fourth Mehl:<br>
  The Lord is inaccessible and unfathomable; He is eternal and imperishable.<br>
  He dwells in the heart, and is all-pervading, permeating everywhere.<br>
  There is no other Giver except Him; worship the Lord, O mortals. ||1||<br>
  No one can kill anyone who is saved by the Savior Lord.<br>
  So serve such a Lord, O Saints, whose Bani is exalted and sublime. ||2||<br>
  When it seems that a place is empty and void,<br>
  there, the Creator Lord is permeating and pervading.<br>
  He causes the dried-up branch to blossom forth in greenery again; so meditate on the Lord - wondrous are His ways! ||3||<br>
  The One who knows the anguish of all beings<br>
  - unto that Lord and Master, I am a sacrifice.<br>
  Offer your prayers to the One who is the Giver of all peace and joy. ||4||<br>
  But one who does not know the state of the soul<br>
  - do not say anything to such an ignorant person.<br>
  Do not argue with fools, O mortals. Meditate on the Lord, in the state of Nirvaanaa. ||5||<br>
  Don't worry - let the Creator take care of it.<br>
  The Lord gives to all creatures in the water and on the land.<br>
  My God bestows His blessings without being asked, even to worms in soil and stones. ||6||<br>
  Do not place your hopes in friends, children and siblings.<br>
  Do not place your hopes in kings or the business of others.<br>
  Without the Lord's Name, no one will be your helper; so meditate on the Lord, the Lord of the world. ||7||<br>
  Night and day, chant the Naam.<br>
  All your hopes and desires shall be fulfilled.<br>
  O servant Nanak, chant the Naam, the Name of the Destroyer of fear, and your life-night shall pass in intuitive peace and poise. ||8||<br>
  Those who serve the Lord find peace.<br>
  They are intuitively absorbed in the Lord's Name.<br>
  The Lord preserves the honor of those who seek His Sanctuary; go and consult the Vedas and the Puraanas. ||9||<br>
  That humble being is attached to the Lord's service, whom the Lord so attaches.<br>
  Through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, doubt and fear are dispelled.<br>
  In his own home, he remains unattached, like the lotus flower in the water. ||10||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 083</h2></center>
  One who serves in egotism is not accepted or approved.<br>
  Such a person is born, only to die again, and come and go in reincarnation.<br>
  Perfect is that penance and that service, which is pleasing to the Mind of my Lord. ||11||<br>
  What Glorious Virtues of Yours should I chant, O my Lord and Master?<br>
  You are the Inner-knower, the Searcher of all souls.<br>
  I beg for blessings from You, O Creator Lord; I repeat Your Name night and day. ||12||<br>
  Some speak in egotistical power.<br>
  Some have the power of authority and Maya.<br>
  I have no other Support at all, except the Lord. O Creator Lord, please save me, meek and dishonored. ||13||<br>
  You bless the meek and dishonored with honor, as it pleases You, O Lord.<br>
  Many others argue in conflict, coming and going in reincarnation.<br>
  Those people, whose side You take, O Lord and Master, are elevated and successful. ||14||<br>
  Those who meditate forever on the Name of the Lord, Har, Har,<br>
  by Guru's Grace, obtain the supreme status.<br>
  Those who serve the Lord find peace; without serving Him, they regret and repent. ||15||<br>
  You are pervading all, O Lord of the world.<br>
  He alone meditates on the Lord, upon whose forehead the Guru places His hand.<br>
  Entering the Sanctuary of the Lord, I meditate on the Lord; servant Nanak is the slave of His slaves. ||16||2||<br>
  Maaroo, Solahas, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  He infused His power into the earth.<br>
  He suspends the heavens upon the feet of His Command.<br>
  He created fire and locked it into wood. That God protects all, O Siblings of Destiny. ||1||<br>
  He gives nourishment to all beings and creatures.<br>
  He Himself is the all-powerful Creator, the Cause of causes.<br>
  In an instant, He establishes and disestablishes; He is your help and support. ||2||<br>
  He cherished you in your mother's womb.<br>
  With every breath and morsel of food, He is with you, and takes care of you.<br>
  Forever and ever, meditate on that Beloved; Great is His glorious greatness! ||3||<br>
  The sultans and nobles are reduced to dust in an instant.<br>
  God cherishes the poor, and makes them into rulers.<br>
  He is the Destroyer of egotistical pride, the Support of all. His value cannot be estimated. ||4||<br>
  He alone is honorable, and he alone is wealthy,<br>
  within whose mind the Lord God abides.<br>
  He alone is my mother, father, child, relative and sibling, who created this Universe. ||5||<br>
  I have come to God's Sanctuary, and so I fear nothing.<br>
  In the Saadh Sangat, the Company of the Holy, I am sure to be saved.<br>
  One who adores the Creator in thought, word and deed, shall never be punished. ||6||<br>
  One whose mind and body are permeated with the Lord, the treasure of virtue,<br>
  does not wander in birth, death and reincarnation.<br>
  Pain vanishes and peace prevails, when one is satisfied and fulfilled. ||7||<br>
  My Lord and Master is my best friend.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 084</h2></center>
  The Inner-knower, the Searcher of hearts, is in all places and interspaces.<br>
  Meditating, meditating in remembrance on the Perfect Transcendent Lord, I am rid of all anxieties and calculations. ||8||<br>
  One who has the Name of the Lord has hundreds of thousands and millions of arms.<br>
  The wealth of the Kirtan of the Lord's Praises is with him.<br>
  In His Mercy, God has blessed me with the sword of spiritual wisdom; I have attacked and killed the demons. ||9||<br>
  Chant the Chant of the Lord, the Chant of Chants.<br>
  Be a winner of the game of life and come to abide in your true home.<br>
  You shall not see the 8.4 million types of hell; sing His Glorious Praises and remain saturated with loving devotion||10||<br>
  He is the Savior of worlds and galaxies.<br>
  He is lofty, unfathomable, inaccessible and infinite.<br>
  That humble being, unto whom God grants His Grace, meditates on Him. ||11||<br>
  God has broken my bonds, and claimed me as His own.<br>
  In His Mercy, He has made me the slave of His home.<br>
  The unstruck celestial sound current resounds and vibrates, when one performs acts of true service. ||12||<br>
  O God, I have enshrined faith in You within my mind.<br>
  My egotistical intellect has been driven out.<br>
  God has made me His own, and now I have a glorious reputation in this world. ||13||<br>
  Proclaim His Glorious Victory, and meditate on the Lord of the Universe.<br>
  I am a sacrifice, a sacrifice to my Lord God.<br>
  I do not see any other except Him. The One Lord pervades the whole world. ||14||<br>
  True, True, True is God.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, my mind is attuned to Him forever.<br>
  Your humble servants live by meditating, meditating in remembrance on You, merging in You, O One Universal Creator. ||15||<br>
  The Dear Lord is the Beloved of His humble devotees.<br>
  My Lord and Master is the Savior of all.<br>
  Meditating in remembrance on the Naam, the Name of the Lord, all desires are fulfilled. He has saved the honor of servant Nanak. ||16||1||<br>
  Maaroo, Solahas, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  The body-bride is attached to the Yogi, the husband-soul.<br>
  She is involved with him, enjoying pleasure and delights.<br>
  As a consequence of past actions, they have come together, enjoying pleasurable play. ||1||<br>
  Whatever the husband does, the bride willingly accepts.<br>
  The husband adorns his bride, and keeps her with himself.<br>
  Joining together, they live in harmony day and night; the husband comforts his wife. ||2||<br>
  When the bride asks, the husband runs around in all sorts of ways.<br>
  Whatever he finds, he brings to show his bride.<br>
  But there is one thing he cannot reach, and so his bride remains hungry and thirsty. ||3||<br>
  With her palms pressed together, the bride offers her prayer,<br>
  "O my beloved, do not leave me and go to foreign lands; please stay here with me.<br>
  Do such business within our home, that my hunger and thirst may be relieved."||4||<br>
  All sorts of religious rituals are performed in this age,<br>
  but without the sublime essence of the Lord, not an iota of peace is found.<br>
  When the Lord becomes Merciful, O Nanak, then in the Sat Sangat, the True Congregation, the bride and the husband enjoy ecstasy and bliss. ||5||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 085</h2></center>
  The body-bride is blind, and the groom is clever and wise.<br>
  The creation was created of the five elements.<br>
  That merchandise, for which you have come into the world, is received only from the True Guru. ||6||<br>
  The body-bride says, "Please live with me,<br>
  O my beloved, peaceful, young lord.<br>
  Without you, I am of no account. Please give me your word, that you will not leave me". ||7||<br>
  The soul-husband says, "I am the slave of my Commander.<br>
  He is my Great Lord and Master, who is fearless and independent.<br>
  As long as He wills, I will remain with you. When He summons me, I shall arise and depart."||8||<br>
  The husband speaks words of Truth to the bride,<br>
  but the bride is restless and inexperienced, and she does not understand anything.<br>
  Again and again, she begs her husband to stay; she thinks that he is just joking when he answers her. ||9||<br>
  The Order comes, and the husband-soul is called.<br>
  He does not consult with his bride, and does not ask her opinion.<br>
  He gets up and marches off, and the discarded body-bride mingles with dust. O Nanak, behold the illusion of emotional attachment and hope. ||10||<br>
  O greedy mind - listen, O my mind!<br>
  Serve the True Guru day and night forever.<br>
  Without the True Guru, the faithless cynics rot away and die. The noose of Death is around the necks of those who have no guru. ||11||<br>
  The self-willed manmukh comes, and the self-willed manmukh goes.<br>
  The manmukh suffers beatings again and again.<br>
  The manmukh endures as many hells as there are; the Gurmukh is not even touched by them. ||12||<br>
  He alone is Gurmukh, who is pleasing to the Dear Lord.<br>
  Who can destroy anyone who is robed in honor by the Lord?<br>
  The blissful one is forever in bliss; he is dressed in robes of honor. ||13||<br>
  I am a sacrifice to the Perfect True Guru.<br>
  He is the Giver of Sanctuary, the Heroic Warrior who keeps His Word.<br>
  Such is the Lord God, the Giver of peace, whom I have met; He shall never leave me or go anywhere else. ||14||<br>
  He is the treasure of virtue; His value cannot be estimated.<br>
  He is perfectly permeating each and every heart, prevailing everywhere.<br>
  Nanak seeks the Sanctuary of the Destroyer of the pains of the poor; I am the dust of the feet of Your slaves. ||15||1||2||<br>
  Maaroo, Solahas, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  My Blissful Lord is forever in bliss.<br>
  He fills each and every heart, and judges each and everyone.<br>
  The True Lord and Master is above the heads of all kings; there is none other than Him. ||1||<br>
  He is joyful, blissful and merciful.<br>
  God's Light is manifest everywhere.<br>
  He creates forms, and gazing upon them, He enjoys them; He Himself worships Himself. ||2||<br>
  He contemplates His own creative power.<br>
  The True Lord Himself creates the expanse of the Universe.<br>
  He Himself stages the play, day and night; He Himself listens, and hearing, rejoices. ||3||<br>
  True is His throne, and True is His kingdom.<br>
  True is the treasure of the True Banker.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 086</h2></center>
  He Himself is True, and true is all that He has established. True is the prevailing Order of the True Lord. ||4||<br>
  True is the justice of the True Lord.<br>
  Your place is forever True, O God.<br>
  True is Your Creative Power, and True is the Word of Your Bani. True is the peace which You give, O my Lord and Master. ||5||<br>
  You alone are the greatest king.<br>
  By the Hukam of Your Command, O True Lord, our affairs are fulfilled.<br>
  Inwardly and outwardly, You know everything; You Yourself are pleased with Yourself. ||6||<br>
  You are the great party-goer, You are the great enjoyer.<br>
  You are detached in Nirvaanaa, You are the Yogi.<br>
  All celestial comforts are in Your home; Your Glance of Grace rains Nectar. ||7||<br>
  You alone give Your gifts.<br>
  You grant Your gifts unto all the beings of the world.<br>
  Your treasures are overflowing, and are never exhausted; through them, we remain satisfied and fulfilled. ||8||<br>
  The Siddhas, seekers and forest-dwellers beg from You.<br>
  The celibates and abstainers, and those who abide in peace beg from You.<br>
  You alone are the Great Giver; all are beggars of You. You bless all the world with Your gifts. ||9||<br>
  Your devotees worship You with infinite love.<br>
  In an instant, You establish and disestablish.<br>
  Your weight is so heavy, O my infinite Lord and Master. Your devotees surrender to the Hukam of Your Command. ||10||<br>
  They alone know You, whom You bless with Your Glance of Grace.<br>
  Through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, they enjoy Your Love forever.<br>
  They alone are clever, handsome and wise, who are pleasing to Your Mind. ||11||<br>
  One who keeps You in his consciousness, becomes carefree and independent.<br>
  One who keeps You in his consciousness, is the true king.<br>
  One who keeps You in his consciousness - what does he have to fear? And what else does he need to do? ||12||<br>
  Thirst and desire are quenched, and one's inner being is cooled and soothed.<br>
  The True Guru has mended the broken one.<br>
  Awareness of the Word of the Shabad has awakened within my heart. Shaking it and vibrating it, I drink in the Ambrosial Nectar. ||13||<br>
  I shall not die; I shall live forever and ever.<br>
  I have become immortal; I am eternal and imperishable.<br>
  I do not come, and I do not go. The Guru has driven out my doubts. ||14||<br>
  Perfect is the Word of the Perfect Guru.<br>
  One who is attached to the Perfect Lord, is immersed in the Perfect Lord.<br>
  His love increases day by day, and when it is weighed, it does not decrease. ||15||<br>
  When the gold is made one hundred percent pure,<br>
  its color is true to the jeweller's eye.<br>
  Assaying it, it is placed in the treasury by God the Jeweller, and it is not melted down again. ||16||<br>
  Your Naam is Ambrosial Nectar, O my Lord and Master.<br>
  Nanak, Your slave, is forever a sacrifice to You.<br>
  In the Society of the Saints, I have found great peace; gazing upon the Blessed Vision of the Lord's Darshan, this mind is pleased and satisfied. ||17||1||3||<br>
  Maaroo, Fifth Mehl, Solhas:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  The Guru is the Lord of the World, the Guru is the Master of the Universe.<br>
  The Guru is merciful, and always forgiving.<br>
  The Guru is the Shaastras, the Simritees and the six rituals. The Guru is the Holy Shrine. ||1||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 087</h2></center>
  Meditating in remembrance on the Guru, all the sins are erased.<br>
  Meditating in remembrance on the Guru, one is not strangled by the noose of Death.<br>
  Meditating in remembrance on the Guru, the mind becomes immaculate; the Guru eliminates egotistical pride. ||2||<br>
  The Guru's servant is not consigned to hell.<br>
  The Guru's servant meditates on the Supreme Lord God.<br>
  The Guru's servant joins the Saadh Sangat, the Company of the Holy; the Guru ever gives the life of the soul. ||3||<br>
  At the Gurdwara, the Guru's Gate, the Kirtan of the Lord's Praises are sung.<br>
  Meeting with the True Guru, one chants the Lord's Praises.<br>
  The True Guru eradicates sorrow and suffering, and bestows honor in the Court of the Lord. ||4||<br>
  The Guru has revealed the inaccessible and unfathomable Lord.<br>
  The True Guru returns to the Path, those who have wandered away.<br>
  No obstacles stand in the way of devotion to the Lord, for one who serves the Guru. The Guru implants perfect spiritual wisdom. ||5||<br>
  The Guru has revealed the Lord everywhere.<br>
  The Lord of the Universe is permeating and pervading the water and the land.<br>
  The high and the low are all the same to Him. Focus your mind's meditation intuitively on Him. ||6||<br>
  Meeting with the Guru, all thirst is quenched.<br>
  Meeting with the Guru, one is not watched by Maya.<br>
  The Perfect Guru bestows truth and contentment; I drink in the Ambrosial Nectar of the Naam, the Name of the Lord. ||7||<br>
  The Word of the Guru's Bani is contained in all.<br>
  He Himself hears it, and He Himself repeats it.<br>
  Those who meditate on it, are all emancipated; they attain the eternal and unchanging home. ||8||<br>
  The Glory of the True Guru is known only to the True Guru.<br>
  Whatever He does, is according to the Pleasure of His Will.<br>
  Your humble servants beg for the dust of the feet of the Holy; Nanak is forever a sacrifice to You. ||9||1||4||<br>
  Maaroo, Solahas, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  The Primal, Immaculate Lord God is formless.<br>
  The Detached Lord is Himself prevailing in all.<br>
  He has no race or social class, no identifying mark. By the Hukam of His Will, He created the entire universe. ||1||<br>
  Out of all the 8.4 million species of beings,<br>
  God blessed mankind with glory.<br>
  That human who misses this chance, shall suffer the pains of coming and going in reincarnation. ||2||<br>
  What should I say, to one who has been created.<br>
  The Gurmukh receives the treasure of the Naam, the Name of the Lord.<br>
  He alone is confused, whom the Lord Himself confuses. He alone understands, whom the Lord inspires to understand. ||3||<br>
  This body has been made the village of joy and sorrow.<br>
  They alone are emancipated, who seek the Sanctuary of the True Guru.<br>
  One who remains untouched by the three qualities, the three gunas - such a Gurmukh is blessed with glory. ||4||<br>
  You can do anything, but whatever you do, only serves to tie your feet.<br>
  The seed which is planted out of season does not sprout, and all one's capital and profits are lost. ||5||<br>
  In this Dark Age of Kali Yuga, the Kirtan of the Lord's Praises are most sublime and exalted.<br>
  Become Gurmukh, chant and focus your meditation.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 088</h2></center>
  You shall save yourself, and save all your generations as well. You shall go to the Court of the Lord with honor. ||6||<br>
  All the continents, nether worlds, islands and worlds<br>
  - God Himself has made them all subject to death.<br>
  The One Imperishable Lord Himself is unmoving and unchanging. Meditating on Him, one becomes unchanging. ||7||<br>
  The Lord's servant becomes like the Lord.<br>
  Do not think that, because of his human body, he is different.<br>
  The waves of the water rise up in various ways, and then the water merges again in water. ||8||<br>
  A beggar begs for charity at His Door.<br>
  When God pleases, He takes pity on him.<br>
  Please bless me with the Blessed Vision of Your Darshan, to satisfy my mind, O Lord. Through the Kirtan of Your Praises, my mind is held steady. ||9||<br>
  The Beauteous Lord and Master is not controlled in any way.<br>
  The Lord does that which pleases the Saints of the Lord.<br>
  He does whatever they wish to be done; nothing blocks their way at His Door. ||10||<br>
  Wherever the mortal is confronted with difficulty,<br>
  there he should meditate on the Lord of the Universe.<br>
  Where there are no children, spouse or friends, there the Lord Himself comes to the rescue. ||11||<br>
  The Great Lord and Master is inaccessible and unfathomable.<br>
  How can anyone meet with God, the self-suficient One?<br>
  Those who have had the noose cut away from around their necks, whom God has set back upon the Path, obtain a place in the Sangat, the Congregation. ||12||<br>
  One who realizes the Hukam of the Lord's Command is said to be His servant.<br>
  He endures both bad and good equally.<br>
  When egotism is silenced, then one comes to know the One Lord. Such a Gurmukh intuitively merges in the Lord. ||13||<br>
  The devotees of the Lord dwell forever in peace.<br>
  With a child-like, innocent nature, they remain detached, turning away from the world.<br>
  They enjoy various pleasures in many ways; God caresses them, like a father caressing his son. ||14||<br>
  He is inaccessible and unfathomable; His value cannot be estimated.<br>
  We meet Him, only when He causes us to meet.<br>
  The Lord is revealed to those humble Gurmukhs, who have such pre-ordained destiny inscribed upon their foreheads. ||15||<br>
  You Yourself are the Creator Lord, the Cause of causes.<br>
  You created the Universe, and You support the whole earth.<br>
  Servant Nanak seeks the Sanctuary of Your Door, O Lord; if it is Your Will, please preserve his honor. ||16||1||5||<br>
  Maaroo, Solahas, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  Whatever is seen is You, O One Lord.<br>
  What the ears hear is the Word of Your Bani.<br>
  There is nothing else to be seen at all. You give support to all. ||1||<br>
  You Yourself are conscious of Your Creation.<br>
  You Yourself established Yourself, O God.<br>
  Creating Yourself, You formed the expanse of the Universe; You Yourself cherish and sustain each and every heart. ||2||<br>
  You created some to hold great and royal courts.<br>
  Some turn away from the world in renunciation, and some maintain their households.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 089</h2></center>
  Some are hungry and some are satisfied and satiated, but all lean on Your Support. ||3||<br>
  The True Lord Himself is True, True, True.<br>
  He is woven into the essence of His devotees, through and through.<br>
  He Himself is hidden, and He Himself is revealed. He Himself spreads Himself out. ||4||<br>
  Forever, forever and ever, He shall always exist.<br>
  He is lofty, inaccessible, unfathomable and infinite.<br>
  He fills the empty, and empties out the filled; such are the plays and dramas of my Lord and Master. ||5||<br>
  With my mouth, I praise my True Lord King.<br>
  With my eyes, I behold the inaccessible and unfathomable Lord.<br>
  Listening, listening with my ears, my mind and body are rejuvenated; my Lord and Master saves all. ||6||<br>
  He created the creation, and gazes upon what He has created.<br>
  All beings and creatures meditate on Him.<br>
  He Himself knows His creative power; He blesses with His Glance of Grace. ||7||<br>
  Where the Saints gather together and sit, God dwells close at hand.<br>
  They abide in bliss and joy, beholding the Lord's wondrous play.<br>
  They sing the Glories of the Lord, and the unstruck sound current of His Bani; O Nanak, His slaves remain conscious of Him. ||8||<br>
  Coming and going is all Your wondrous play.<br>
  Creating the Creation, You gaze upon Your infinite play.<br>
  Creating the Creation, You Yourself cherish and nurture it. ||9||<br>
  Listening, listening to Your Glory, I live.<br>
  Forever and ever, I am a sacrifice to You.<br>
  With my palms pressed together, I meditate in remembrance on You, day and night, O my inaccessible, infinite Lord and Master. ||10||<br>
  Other than You, who else should I praise?<br>
  I meditate on the One and Only Lord within my mind.<br>
  Realizing the Hukam of Your Will, Your humble servants are enraptured; this is the achievement of Your devotees. ||11||<br>
  Following the Guru's Teachings, I meditate on the True Lord within my mind.<br>
  Following the Guru's Teachings, I am immersed in the Lord's Love.<br>
  Following the Guru's Teachings, all bonds are broken, and this doubt and emotional attachment are burnt away. ||12||<br>
  Wherever He keeps me, is my place of rest.<br>
  Whatever naturally happens, I accept that as good.<br>
  Hatred is gone - I have no hatred at all; I see the One Lord in all. ||13||<br>
  Fear has been removed, and darkness has been dispelled.<br>
  The all-powerful, primal, detached Lord God has been revealed.<br>
  Forsaking self-conceit, I have entered His Sanctuary, and I work for Him. ||14||<br>
  Rare are those few, very blessed people, who come into the world,<br>
  and meditate on their Lord and Master, twenty-four hours a day.<br>
  Associating with such humble people, all are saved, and their families are saved as well. ||15||<br>
  This is the blessing which I have received from my Lord and Master.<br>
  Twenty-four hours a day, with my palms pressed together, I meditate on Him.<br>
  I chant the Naam, and through the Naam, I intuitively merge into the Lord; O Nanak, may I be blessed with the Naam, and ever repeat it. ||16||1||6||<br>
  Maaroo, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Do not be fooled by appearances, you fool.<br>
  This is a false attachment to the expanse of an illusion.<br>
  No one can remain in this world; only the One Lord is permanent and unchanging. ||1||<br>
  Seek the Sanctuary of the Perfect Guru.<br>
  He shall eradicate all emotional attachment, sorrow and doubt.<br>
  He shall administer the medicine, the Mantra of the One Name. Sing the True Name within your heart. ||2||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 090</h2></center>
  So many gods yearn for the Naam, the Name of the Lord.<br>
  All the devotees serve Him.<br>
  He is the Master of the masterless, the Destroyer of the pains of the poor. His Name is obtained from the Perfect Guru. ||3||<br>
  I cannot conceive of any other door.<br>
  One who wanders through the three worlds, understands nothing.<br>
  The True Guru is the banker, with the treasure of the Naam. This jewel is obtained from Him. ||4||<br>
  The dust of His feet purifies.<br>
  Even the angelic beings and gods cannot obtain it, O friend.<br>
  The True Guru is the True Primal Being, the Transcendent Lord God; meeting with Him, one is carried across to the other side. ||5||<br>
  O my beloved mind, if you wish for the 'tree of life';<br>
  if you wish for Kaamadhayna, the wish-fulfilling cow to adorn your court;<br>
  if you wish to be satisfied and contented, then serve the Perfect Guru, and practice the Naam, the source of nectar. ||6||<br>
  Through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, the five thieves of desire are conquered.<br>
  In the Fear of the Supreme Lord God, you shall become immaculate and pure.<br>
  When one meets the Perfect Guru, the Philosopher's Stone, His touch reveals the Lord, the Philosopher's Stone. ||7||<br>
  Myriads of heavens do not equal the Lord's Name.<br>
  The spiritually wise forsake mere liberation.<br>
  The One Universal Creator Lord is found through the True Guru. I am a sacrifice, a sacrifice to the Blessed Vision of the Guru's Darshan. ||8||<br>
  No one knows how to serve the Guru.<br>
  The Guru is the unfathomable, Supreme Lord God.<br>
  He alone is the Guru's servant, whom the Guru Himself links to His service, and upon whose forehead such blessed destiny is inscribed. ||9||<br>
  Even the Vedas do not know the Guru's Glory.<br>
  They narrate only a tiny bit of what is heard.<br>
  The True Guru is the Supreme Lord God, the Incomparable One; meditating in remembrance on Him, the mind is cooled and soothed. ||10||<br>
  Hearing of Him, the mind comes to life.<br>
  When He dwells within the heart, one becomes peaceful and cool.<br>
  Chanting the Guru's Name with the mouth, one obtains glory, and does not have to walk on the Path of Death. ||11||<br>
  I have entered the Sanctuary of the Saints,<br>
  and placed before them my soul, my breath of life and wealth.<br>
  I know nothing about service and awareness; please take pity upon this worm. ||12||<br>
  I am unworthy; please merge me into Yourself.<br>
  Please bless me with Your Grace, and link me to Your service.<br>
  I wave the fan, and grind the corn for the Saints; washing their feet, I find peace. ||13||<br>
  After wandering around at so many doors, I have come to Yours, O Lord.<br>
  By Your Grace, I have entered Your Sanctuary.<br>
  Forever and ever, keep me in the Company of the Saints; please bless me with this Gift of Your Name. ||14||<br>
  My World-Lord has become merciful,<br>
  and I have obtained the Blessed Vision of the Darshan of the Perfect True Guru.<br>
  I have found eternal peace, poise and bliss; Nanak is the slave of Your slaves. ||15||2||7||<br>
  Maaroo, Solahas, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  The earth and the Akaashic ethers meditate in remembrance.<br>
  The moon and the sun meditate in remembrance on You, O treasure of virtue.<br>
  Air, water and fire meditate in remembrance. All creation meditates in remembrance. ||1||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 091</h2></center>
  All the continents, islands and worlds meditate in remembrance.<br>
  The nether worlds and spheres meditate in remembrance on that True Lord.<br>
  The sources of creation and speech meditate in remembrance; all the Lord's humble servants meditate in remembrance. ||2||<br>
  Brahma, Vishnu and Shiva meditate in remembrance.<br>
  The three hundred thirty million gods meditate in remembrance.<br>
  The titans and demons all meditate in remembrance; Your Praises are uncountable - they cannot be counted. ||3||<br>
  All the beasts, birds and demons meditate in remembrance.<br>
  The forests, mountains and hermits meditate in remembrance.<br>
  All the vines and branches meditate in remembrance; O my Lord and Master, You are permeating and pervading all minds. ||4||<br>
  All beings, both subtle and gross, meditate in remembrance.<br>
  The Siddhas and seekers meditate in remembrance on the Lord's Mantra.<br>
  Both the visible and the invisible meditate in remembrance on my God; God is the Master of all worlds. ||5||<br>
  Men and women, throughout the four stages of life, meditate in remembrance on You.<br>
  All social classes and souls of all races meditate in remembrance on You.<br>
  All the virtuous, clever and wise people meditate in remembrance; night and day meditate in remembrance. ||6||<br>
  Hours, minutes and seconds meditate in remembrance.<br>
  Death and life, and thoughts of purification, meditate in remembrance.<br>
