  The Shaastras, with their lucky signs and joinings, meditate in remembrance; the invisible cannot be seen, even for an instant. ||7||<br>
  The Lord and Master is the Doer, the Cause of causes.<br>
  He is the Inner-knower, the Searcher of all hearts.<br>
  That person, whom You bless with Your Grace, and link to Your devotional service, wins this invaluable human life. ||8||<br>
  He, within whose mind God dwells,<br>
  has perfect karma, and chants the Chant of the Guru.<br>
  One who realizes God pervading deep within all, does not wander crying in reincarnation again. ||9||<br>
  Pain, sorrow and doubt run away from that one, within whose mind the Word of the Guru's Shabad abides.<br>
  Intuitive peace, poise and bliss come from the sublime essence of the Naam; the unstruck sound current of the Guru's Bani intuitively vibrates and resounds. ||10||<br>
  He alone is wealthy, who meditates on God.<br>
  He alone is honorable, who joins the Saadh Sangat, the Company of the Holy.<br>
  That person, within whose mind the Supreme Lord God abides, has perfect karma, and becomes famous. ||11||<br>
  The Lord and Master is pervading the water, land and sky.<br>
  There is no other said to be so.<br>
  The ointment of the Guru's spiritual wisdom has eradicated all doubts; except the One Lord, I do not see any other at all. ||12||<br>
  The Lord's Court is the highest of the high.<br>
  His limit and extent cannot be described.<br>
  The Lord and Master is profoundly deep, unfathomable and unweighable; how can He be measured? ||13||<br>
  You are the Creator; all is created by You.<br>
  Without You, there is no other at all.<br>
  You alone, God, are in the beginning, the middle and the end. You are the root of the entire expanse. ||14||<br>
  The Messenger of Death does not even approach that person<br>
  who sings the Kirtan of the Lord's Praises in the Saadh Sangat, the Company of the Holy.<br>
  All desires are fulfilled, for one who listens with his ears to the Praises of God. ||15||<br>
  You belong to all, and all belong to You, O my true, deep and profound Lord and Master.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 092</h2></center>
  Says Nanak, those humble beings are exalted, who are pleasing to Your Mind, O my Lord and Master. ||16||1||8||<br>
  Maaroo, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  God is the almighty Giver of all peace and joy.<br>
  Be merciful to me, that I may meditate in remembrance on Your Name.<br>
  The Lord is the Great Giver; all beings and creatures are beggars; His humble servants yearn to beg from Him. ||1||<br>
  I beg for the dust of the feet of the humble, that I may be blessed with the supreme status,<br>
  and the filth of countless lifetimes may be erased.<br>
  The chronic diseases are cured by the medicine of the Lord's Name; I beg to be imbued with the Immaculate Lord. ||2||<br>
  With my ears, I listen to the Pure Praises of my Lord and Master.<br>
  With the Support of the One Lord, I have abandoned corruption, sexuality and desire.<br>
  I humbly bow and fall at the feet of Your slaves; I do not hesitate to do good deeds. ||3||<br>
  O Lord, with my tongue I sing Your Glorious Praises.<br>
  The sins which I have committed are erased.<br>
  Meditating, meditating in remembrance on my Lord and Master, my mind lives; I am rid of the five oppressive demons. ||4||<br>
  Meditating on Your lotus feet, I have come aboard Your boat.<br>
  Joining the Society of the Saints, I cross over the world-ocean.<br>
  My flower-offering and worship is to realize that the Lord is dwelling alike in all; I shall not be reincarnated naked again. ||5||<br>
  Please make me the slave of Your slaves, O Lord of the world.<br>
  You are the treasure of Grace, merciful to the meek.<br>
  Meet with your companion and helper, the Perfect Transcendent Lord God; you shall never be separated from Him again. ||6||<br>
  I dedicate my mind and body, and place them in offering before the Lord.<br>
  Asleep for countless lifetimes, I have awakened.<br>
  He, to whom I belong, is my cherisher and nurturer. I have killed and discarded my murderous self-conceit. ||7||<br>
  The Inner-knower, the Searcher of hearts, is pervading the water and the land.<br>
  The undeceivable Lord and Master is permeating each and every heart.<br>
  The Perfect Guru has demolished the wall of doubt, and now I see the One Lord pervading everywhere. ||8||<br>
  Wherever I look, there I see God, the ocean of peace.<br>
  The Lord's treasure is never exhausted; He is the storehouse of jewels.<br>
  He cannot be seized; He is inaccessible, and His limits cannot be found. He is realized when the Lord bestows His Grace. ||9||<br>
  My heart is cooled, and my mind and body are calmed and soothed.<br>
  The craving for birth and death is quenched.<br>
  Grasping hold of my hand, He has lifted me up and out; He has blessed me with His Ambrosial Glance of Grace. ||10||<br>
  The One and Only Lord is permeating and pervading everywhere.<br>
  There is none other than Him at all.<br>
  God permeates the beginning, the middle and the end; He has subdued my desires and doubts. ||11||<br>
  The Guru is the Transcendent Lord, the Guru is the Lord of the Universe.<br>
  The Guru is the Creator, the Guru is forever forgiving.<br>
  Meditating, chanting the Guru's Chant, I have obtained the fruits and rewards; in the Company of the Saints, I have been blessed with the lamp of spiritual wisdom. ||12||<br>
  Whatever I see, is my Lord and Master God.<br>
  Whatever I hear, is the Bani of God's Word.<br>
  Whatever I do, You make me do; You are the Sanctuary, the help and support of the Saints, Your children. ||13||<br>
  The beggar begs, and worships You in adoration.<br>
  You are the Purifier of the sinners, O Perfectly Holy Lord God.<br>
  Please bless me with this one gift, O treasure of all bliss and virtue; I do not ask for anything else. ||14||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 093</h2></center>
  God is the Creator of the body-vessel.<br>
  In the Society of the Saints, the dye is produced.<br>
  Through the Word of the Lord's Bani, one's reputation becomes immaculate, and the mind is colored by the dye of the Naam, the Name of the Lord. ||15||<br>
  The sixteen powers, absolute perfection and fruitful rewards are obtained,<br>
  when the Lord and Master of infinite power is revealed.<br>
  The Lord's Name is Nanak's bliss, play and peace; he drinks in the Ambrosial Nectar of the Lord. ||16||2||9||<br>
  Maaroo, Solhas, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  You are my Lord and Master; You have made me Your servant.<br>
  My soul and body are all gifts from You.<br>
  You are the Creator, the Cause of causes; nothing belongs to me. ||1||<br>
  When You sent me, I came into the world.<br>
  Whatever is pleasing to Your Will, I do.<br>
  Without You, nothing is done, so I am not anxious at all. ||2||<br>
  In the world hereafter, the Hukam of Your Command is heard.<br>
  In this world, I chant Your Praises, Lord.<br>
  You Yourself write the account, and You Yourself erase it; no one can argue with You. ||3||<br>
  You are our father; we are all Your children.<br>
  We play as You cause us to play.<br>
  The wilderness and the path are all made by You. No one can take the wrong path. ||4||<br>
  Some remain seated within their homes.<br>
  Some wander across the country and through foreign lands.<br>
  Some are grass-cutters, and some are kings. Who among these can be called false? ||5||<br>
  Who is liberated, and who will land in hell?<br>
  Who is worldly, and who is a devotee?<br>
  Who is wise, and who is shallow? Who is aware, and who is ignorant? ||6||<br>
  By the Hukam of the Lord's Command, one is liberated, and by His Hukam, one falls into hell.<br>
  By His Hukam, one is worldly, and by His Hukam, one is a devotee.<br>
  By His Hukam, one is shallow, and by His Hukam, one is wise. There is no other side except His. ||7||<br>
  You made the ocean vast and huge.<br>
  You made some into foolish self-willed manmukhs, and dragged them into hell.<br>
  Some are carried across, in the ship of Truth of the True Guru. ||8||<br>
  You issue Your Command for this amazing thing, death.<br>
  You create all beings and creatures, and absorb them back into Yourself.<br>
  You gaze in delight upon the one arena of the world, and enjoy all the pleasures. ||9||<br>
  Great is the Lord and Master, and Great is His Name.<br>
  He is the Great Giver; Great is His place.<br>
  He is inaccessible and unfathomable, infinite and unweighable. He cannot be measureed. ||10||<br>
  No one else knows His value.<br>
  Only You Yourself, O Immaculate Lord, are equal to Yourself.<br>
  You Yourself are the spiritual teacher, You Yourself are the One who meditates. You Yourself are the great and immense Being of Truth. ||11||<br>
  For so many days, You remained invisible.<br>
  For so many days, You were absorbed in silent absorption.<br>
  For so many days, there was only pitch darkness, and then the Creator revealed Himself. ||12||<br>
  You Yourself are called the God of Supreme Power.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 094</h2></center>
  You Yourself are the hero, exerting Your regal power.<br>
  You Yourself spread peace within; You are cool and icy calm. ||13||<br>
  One whom You bless and make Gurmukh<br>
  - the Naam abides within him, and the unstruck sound current vibrates for him.<br>
  He is peaceful, and he is the master of all; the Messenger of Death does not even approach him. ||14||<br>
  His value cannot be described on paper.<br>
  Says Nanak, the Lord of the world is infinite.<br>
  In the beginning, in the middle and in the end, God exists. Judgement is in His Hands alone. ||15||<br>
  No one is equal to Him.<br>
  No one can stand up against Him by any means.<br>
  Nanak's God is Himself all-in-all. He creates and stages and watches His wondrous plays. ||16||1||10||<br>
  Maaroo, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  The Supreme Lord God is imperishable, the Transcendent Lord, the Inner-knower, the Searcher of hearts.<br>
  He is the Slayer of demons, our Supreme Lord and Master.<br>
  The Supreme Rishi, the Master of the sensory organs, the uplifter of mountains, the joyful Lord playing His enticing flute. ||1||<br>
  The Enticer of Hearts, the Lord of wealth, Krishna, the Enemy of ego.<br>
  The Lord of the Universe, the Dear Lord, the Destroyer of demons.<br>
  The Life of the World, our eternal and ever-stable Lord and Master dwells within each and every heart, and is always with us. ||2||<br>
  The Support of the Earth, the man-lion, the Supreme Lord God.<br>
  The Protector who tears apart demons with His teeth, the Upholder of the earth.<br>
  O Creator, You assumed the form of the pygmy to humble the demons; You are the Lord God of all. ||3||<br>
  You are the Great Raam Chand, who has no form or feature.<br>
  Adorned with flowers, holding the chakra in Your hand, Your form is incomparably beautiful.<br>
  You have thousands of eyes, and thousands of forms. You alone are the Giver, and all are beggars of You. ||4||<br>
  You are the Lover of Your devotees, the Master of the masterless.<br>
  The Lord and Master of the milk-maids, You are the companion of all.<br>
  O Lord, Immacuate Great Giver, I cannot describe even an iota of Your Glorious Virtues. ||5||<br>
  Liberator, Enticing Lord, Lord of Lakshmi, Supreme Lord God.<br>
  Savior of Dropadi's honor.<br>
  Lord of Maya, miracle-worker, absorbed in delightful play, unattached. ||6||<br>
  The Blessed Vision of His Darshan is fruitful and rewarding; He is not born, He is self-existent.<br>
  His form is undying; it is never destroyed.<br>
  O imperishable, eternal, unfathomable Lord, everything is attached to You. ||7||<br>
  The Lover of greatness, who dwells in heaven.<br>
  By the Pleasure of His Will, He took incarnation as the great fish and the tortoise.<br>
  The Lord of beauteous hair, the Worker of miraculous deeds, whatever He wishes, comes to pass. ||8||<br>
  He is beyond need of any sustenance, free of hate and all-pervading.<br>
  He has staged His play; He is called the four-armed Lord.<br>
  He assumed the beautiful form of the blue-skinned Krishna; hearing His flute, all are fascinated and enticed. ||9||<br>
  He is adorned with garlands of flowers, with lotus eyes.<br>
  His ear-rings, crown and flute are so beautiful.<br>
  He carries the conch, the chakra and the war club; He is the Great Charioteer, who stays with His Saints. ||10||<br>
  The Lord of yellow robes, the Master of the three worlds.<br>
  The Lord of the Universe, the Lord of the world; with my mouth, I chant His Name.<br>
  The Archer who draws the bow, the Beloved Lord God; I cannot count all His limbs. ||11||<br>
  He is said to be free of anguish, and absolutely immaculate.<br>
  The Lord of prosperity, pervading the water, the land and the sky.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 095</h2></center>
  He is near this world and the nether regions of the underworld; His Place is permanent, ever-stable and imperishable. ||12||<br>
  The Purifier of sinners, the Destroyer of pain and fear.<br>
  The Eliminator of egotism, the Eradicator of coming and going.<br>
  He is pleased with devotional worship, and merciful to the meek; He cannot be appeased by any other qualities. ||13||<br>
  The Formless Lord is undeceivable and unchanging.<br>
  He is the Embodiment of Light; through Him, the whole world blossoms forth.<br>
  He alone unites with Him, whom He unites with Himself. No one can attain the Lord by himself. ||14||<br>
  He Himself is the milk-maid, and He Himself is Krishna.<br>
  He Himself grazes the cows in the forest.<br>
  You Yourself create, and You Yourself destroy. Not even a particle of filth attaches to You. ||15||<br>
  Which of Your Glorious Virtues can I chant with my one tongue?<br>
  Even the thousand-headed serpent does not know Your limit.<br>
  One may chant new names for You day and night, but even so, O God, no one can describe even one of Your Glorious Virtues. ||16||<br>
  I have grasped the Support, and entered the Sanctuary of the Lord, the Father of the world.<br>
  The Messenger of Death is terrifying and horrendous, and sea of Maya is impassable.<br>
  Please be merciful, Lord, and save me, if it is Your Will; please lead me to join with the Saadh Sangat, the Company of the Holy. ||17||<br>
  All that is seen is an illusion.<br>
  I beg for this one gift, for the dust of the feet of the Saints, O Lord of the Universe.<br>
  Applying it to my forehead, I obtain the supreme status; he alone obtains it, unto whom You give it. ||18||<br>
  Those, unto whom the Lord, the Giver of peace, grants His Mercy,<br>
  grasp the feet of the Holy, and weave them into their hearts.<br>
  They obtain all the wealth of the Naam, the Name of the Lord; the unstruck sound current of the Shabad vibrates and resounds within their minds. ||19||<br>
  With my tongue I chant the Names given to You.<br>
  'Sat Naam' is Your perfect, primal Name.<br>
  Says Nanak, Your devotees have entered Your Sanctuary. Please bestow the Blessed Vision of Your Darshan; their minds are filled with love for You. ||20||<br>
  You alone know Your state and extent.<br>
  You Yourself speak, and You Yourself describe it.<br>
  Please make Nanak the slave of Your slaves, O Lord; as it pleases Your Will, please keep him with Your slaves. ||21||2||11||<br>
  Maaroo, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  O slave of the inaccessible Lord God Allah,<br>
  forsake thoughts of worldly entanglements.<br>
  Become the dust of the feet of the humble fakeers, and consider yourself a traveller on this journey. O saintly dervish, you shall be approved in the Court of the Lord. ||1||<br>
  Let Truth be your prayer, and faith your prayer-mat.<br>
  Subdue your desires, and overcome your hopes.<br>
  Let your body be the mosque, and your mind the priest. Let true purity be God's Word for you. ||2||<br>
  Let your practice be to live the spiritual life.<br>
  Let your spiritual cleansing be to renounce the world and seek God.<br>
  Let control of the mind be your spiritual wisdom, O holy man; meeting with God, you shall never die again. ||3||<br>
  Practice within your heart the teachings of the Koran and the Bible;<br>
  restrain the ten sensory organs from straying into evil.<br>
  Tie up the five demons of desire with faith, charity and contentment, and you shall be acceptable. ||4||<br>
  Let compassion be your Mecca, and the dust of the feet of the holy your fast.<br>
  Let Paradise be your practice of the Prophet's Word.<br>
  God is the beauty, the light and the fragrance. Meditation on Allah is the secluded meditation chamber. ||5||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 096</h2></center>
  He alone is a Qazi, who practices the Truth.<br>
  He alone is a Haji, a pilgrim to Mecca, who purifies his heart.<br>
  He alone is a Mullah, who banishes evil; he alone is a saintly dervish, who takes the Support of the Lord's Praise. ||6||<br>
  Always, at every moment, remember God, the Creator within your heart.<br>
  Let your meditation beads be the subjugation of the ten senses. Let good conduct and self-restraint be your circumcision. ||7||<br>
  You must know in your heart that everything is temporary.<br>
  Family, household and siblings are all entanglements.<br>
  Kings, rulers and nobles are mortal and transitory; only God's Gate is the permanent place. ||8||<br>
  First, is the Lord's Praise; second, contentment;<br>
  third, humility, and fourth, giving to charities.<br>
  Fifth is to hold one's desires in restraint. These are the five most sublime daily prayers. ||9||<br>
  Let your daily worship be the knowledge that God is everywhere.<br>
  Let renunciation of evil actions be the water-jug you carry.<br>
  Let realization of the One Lord God be your call to prayer; be a good child of God - let this be your trumpet. ||10||<br>
  Let what is earned righteously be your blessed food.<br>
  Wash away pollution with the river of your heart.<br>
  One who realizes the Prophet attains heaven. Azraa-eel, the Messenger of Death, does not cast him into hell. ||11||<br>
  Let good deeds be your body, and faith your bride.<br>
  Play and enjoy the Lord's love and delight.<br>
  Purify what is impure, and let the Lord's Presence be your religious tradition. Let your total awareness be the turban on your head. ||12||<br>
  To be Muslim is to be kind-hearted,<br>
  and wash away pollution from within the heart.<br>
  He does not even approach worldly pleasures; he is pure, like flowers, silk, ghee and the deer-skin. ||13||<br>
  One who is blessed with the mercy and compassion of the Merciful Lord,<br>
  is the manliest man among men.<br>
  He alone is a Shaykh, a preacher, a Haji, and he alone is God's slave, who is blessed with God's Grace. ||14||<br>
  The Creator Lord has Creative Power; the Merciful Lord has Mercy.<br>
  The Praises and the Love of the Merciful Lord are unfathomable.<br>
  Realize the True Hukam, the Command of the Lord, O Nanak; you shall be released from bondage, and carried across. ||15||3||12||<br>
  Maaroo, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  The Abode of the Supreme Lord God is above all.<br>
  He Himself establishes, establishes and creates.<br>
  Holding tight to the Sanctuary of God, peace is found, and one is not afflicted by the fear of Maya. ||1||<br>
  He saved you from the fire of the womb,<br>
  and did not destroy you, when you were an egg in your mother's ovary.<br>
  Blessing you with meditative remembrance upon Himself, He nurtured you and cherished you; He is the Master of all hearts. ||2||<br>
  I have come to the Sanctuary of His lotus feet.<br>
  In the Saadh Sangat, the Company of the Holy, I sing the Praises of the Lord.<br>
  I have erased all the pains of birth and death; meditating on the Lord, Har, Har, I have no fear of death. ||3||<br>
  God is all-powerful, indescribable, unfathomable and divine.<br>
  All beings and creatures serve Him.<br>
  In so many ways, He cherishes those born from eggs, from the womb, from sweat and from the earth. ||4||<br>
  He alone obtains this wealth,<br>
  who savors and enjoys, deep within his mind, the Name of the Lord.<br>
  Grasping hold of his arm, God lifts him up and pulls him out of the deep, dark pit. Such a devotee of the Lord is very rare. ||5||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 097</h2></center>
  God exists in the beginning, in the middle and in the end.<br>
  Whatever the Creator Lord Himself does, comes to pass.<br>
  Doubt and fear are erased, in the Saadh Sangat, the Company of the Holy, and then one is not afflicted by deadly pain. ||6||<br>
  I sing the most Sublime Bani, the Word of the Lord of the Universe.<br>
  I beg for the dust of the feet of the Saadh Sangat.<br>
  Eradicating desire, I have become free of desire; I have burnt away all my sins. ||7||<br>
  This is the unique way of the Saints;<br>
  they behold the Supreme Lord God with them.<br>
  With each and every breath, they worship and adore the Lord, Har, Har. How could anyone be too lazy to meditate on Him? ||8||<br>
  Wherever I look, there I see the Inner-knower, the Searcher of hearts.<br>
  I never forget God, my Lord and Master, even for an instant.<br>
  Your slaves live by meditating, meditating in remembrance on the Lord; You are permeating the woods, the water and the land. ||9||<br>
  Even the hot wind does not touch one<br>
  who remains awake in meditative remembrance, night and day.<br>
  He delights and enjoys meditative remembrance on the Lord; he has no attachment to Maya. ||10||<br>
  Disease, sorrow and pain do not affect him;<br>
  he sings the Kirtan of the Lord's Praises in the Saadh Sangat, the Company of the Holy.<br>
  Please bless me with Your Name, O my Beloved Lord God; please listen to my prayer, O Creator. ||11||<br>
  Your Name is a jewel, O my Beloved Lord.<br>
  Your slaves are imbued with Your Infinite Love.<br>
  Those who are imbued with Your Love, become like You; it is so rare that they are found. ||12||<br>
  My mind longs for the dust of the feet of those<br>
  who never forget the Lord.<br>
  Associating with them, I obtain the supreme status; the Lord, my Companion, is always with me. ||13||<br>
  He alone is my beloved friend and companion,<br>
  who implants the Name of the One Lord within, and eradicates evil-mindedness.<br>
  Immaculate are the teachings of that humble servant of the Lord, who casts out sexual desire, anger and egotism. ||14||<br>
  Other than You, O Lord, no one is mine.<br>
  The Guru has led me to grasp the feet of God.<br>
  I am a sacrifice to the Perfect True Guru, who has destroyed the illusion of duality. ||15||<br>
  With each and every breath, I never forget God.<br>
  Twenty-four hours a day, I meditate on the Lord, Har, Har.<br>
  O Nanak, the Saints are imbued with Your Love; You are the great and all-powerful Lord. ||16||4||13||<br>
  Maaroo, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  I enshrine the Lord's lotus feet continually within my heart.<br>
  Each and every moment, I humbly bow to the Perfect Guru.<br>
  I dedicate my body, mind and everything, and place it in offering before the Lord. His Name is the most beautiful in this world. ||1||<br>
  Why forget the Lord and Master from your mind?<br>
  He blessed you with body and soul, creating and embellishing you.<br>
  With every breath and morsel of food, the Creator takes care of His beings, who receive according to what they have done. ||2||<br>
  No one returns empty-handed from Him;<br>
  twenty-four hours a day, keep the Lord in your mind.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 098</h2></center>
  In the Saadh Sangat, the Company of the Holy, meditate and vibrate upon your imperishable Lord and Master, and you shall be honored in the Court of the Lord. ||3||<br>
  The four great blessings, and the eighteen miraculous spiritual powers,<br>
  are found in the treasure of the Naam, which brings celestial peace and poise, and the nine treasures.<br>
  If you yearn in your mind for all joys, then join the Saadh Sangat, and dwell upon your Lord and Master. ||4||<br>
  The Shaastras, the Simritees and the Vedas proclaim<br>
  that the mortal must be victorious in this priceless human life.<br>
  Forsaking sexual desire, anger and slander, sing of the Lord with your tongue, O Nanak. ||5||<br>
  He has no form or shape, no ancestry or social class.<br>
  The Perfect Lord is perfectly pervading day and night.<br>
  Whoever meditates on Him is very fortunate; he is not consigned to reincarnation again. ||6||<br>
  One who forgets the Primal Lord, the Architect of karma,<br>
  wanders around burning, and remains tormented.<br>
  No one can save such an ungrateful person; he is thrown into the most horrible hell. ||7||<br>
  He blessed you with your soul, the breath of life, your body and wealth;<br>
  He preserved and nurtured you in your mother's womb.<br>
  Forsaking His Love, you are imbued with another; you shall never achieve your goals like this. ||8||<br>
  Please shower me with Your Merciful Grace, O my Lord and Master.<br>
  You dwell in each and every heart, and are near everyone.<br>
  Nothing is in my hands; he alone knows, whom You inspire to know. ||9||<br>
  One who has such pre-ordained destiny inscribed upon his forehead,<br>
  that person is not afflicted by Maya.<br>
  Slave Nanak seeks Your Sanctuary forever; there is no other equal to You. ||10||<br>
  In His Will, He made all pain and pleasure.<br>
  How rare are those who remember the Ambrosial Naam, the Name of the Lord.<br>
  His value cannot be described. He is prevailing everywhere. ||11||<br>
  He is the devotee; He is the Great Giver.<br>
  He is the Perfect Primal Lord, the Architect of karma.<br>
  He is your help and support, since infancy; He fulfills your mind's desires. ||12||<br>
  Death, pain and pleasure are ordained by the Lord.<br>
  They do not increase or decrease by anyone's efforts.<br>
  That alone happens, which is pleasing to the Creator; speaking of himself, the mortal ruins himself. ||13||<br>
  He lifts us up and pulls us out of the deep dark pit;<br>
  He unites with Himself, those who were separated for so many incarnations.<br>
  Showering them with His Mercy, He protects them with His own hands. Meeting with the Holy Saints, they meditate on the Lord of the Universe. ||14||<br>
  Your worth cannot be described.<br>
  Wondrous is Your form, and Your glorious greatness.<br>
  Your humble servant begs for the gift of devotional worship. Nanak is a sacrifice, a sacrifice to You. ||15||1||14||22||24||2||14||62||<br>
  Vaar Of Maaroo, Third Mehl:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  Shalok, First Mehl:<br>
  If virtue is sold when there is no buyer, then it is sold very cheap.<br>
  But if one meets a buyer of virtue, then virtue sells for hundreds of thousands.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 099</h2></center>
  Meeting with a virtuous person, virtue is obtained, and one is immersed in the True Guru.<br>
  Priceless virtues are not obtained for any price; they cannot be purchased in a store.<br>
  O Nanak, their weight is full and perfect; it never decreases at all. ||1||<br>
  Fourth Mehl:<br>
  Without the Naam, the Name of the Lord, they wander around, continually coming and going in reincarnation.<br>
  Some are in bondage, and some are set free; some are happy in the Love of the Lord.<br>
  O Nanak, believe in the True Lord, and practice Truth, through the lifestyle of Truth. ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  From the Guru, I have obtained the supremely powerful sword of spiritual wisdom.<br>
  I have cut down the fortress of duality and doubt, attachment, greed and egotism.<br>
  The Name of the Lord abides within my mind; I contemplate the Word of the Guru's Shabad.<br>
  Through Truth, self-discipline and sublime understanding, the Lord has become very dear to me.<br>
  Truly, truly, the True Creator Lord is all-pervading. ||1||<br>
  Shalok, Third Mehl:<br>
  Among the ragas, Kaydaaraa Raga is known as good, O Siblings of Destiny, if through it, one comes to love the Word of the Shabad,<br>
  and if one remains in the Soceity of the Saints, and enshrines love for the True Lord.<br>
  Such a person washes away the pollution from within, and saves his generations as well.<br>
  He gathes in the capital of virtue, and destroys and drives out unvirtuous sins.<br>
  O Nanak, he alone is known as united, who does not forsake his Guru, and who does not love duality. ||1||<br>
  Fourth Mehl:<br>
  Gazing upon the world-ocean, I am afraid of death; but if I live in the Fear of You, God, then I am not afraid.<br>
  Through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, I am content; O Nanak, I blossom forth in the Name. ||2||<br>
  Fourth Mehl:<br>
  I get on board the boat and set out, but the ocean is churning with waves.<br>
  The boat of Truth encounters no obstruction, if the Guru gives encouragement.<br>
  He takes us across to the door on the other side, as the Guru keeps watch.<br>
  O Nanak, if I am blessed with His Grace, I shall go to His Court with honor. ||3||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  Enjoy your kingdom of bliss; as Gurmukh, practice Truth.<br>
  Sitting upon the throne of Truth, the Lord administers justice; He unites us in Union with the Society of the Saints.<br>
  Meditating on the Lord, through the True Teachings, we become just like the Lord.<br>
  If the Lord, the Giver of peace, abides in the mind, in this world, then in the end, He becomes our help and support.<br>
  Love for the Lord wells up, when the Guru imparts understanding. ||2||<br>
  Shalok, First Mehl:<br>
  Confused and deluded, I wander around, but no one shows me the way.<br>
  I go and ask the clever people, if there is there anyone who can rid me of my pain.<br>
  If the True Guru abides within my mind, then I see the Lord, my best friend, there.<br>
  O Nanak, my mind is satisfied and fulfilled, contemplating the Praises of the True Name. ||1||<br>
  Third Mehl:<br>
  He Himself is the Doer, and He is the deed; He Himself issues the Command.<br>
  He Himself forgives some, and He Himself does the deed.<br>
  O Nanak, receiving the Divine Light from the Guru, suffering and corruption are burnt away, through the Name. ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  Don't be fooled by gazing at the riches of Maya, you foolish self-willed manmukh.<br>
  It shall not go along with you when you must depart; all the wealth you see is false.<br>
  The blind and ignorant do not understand, that the sword of death is hanging over their heads.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, those who drink in the sublime essence of the Lord are saved.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 100</h2></center>
  He Himself is the Doer, and He Himself is the Cause; the Lord Himself is our Saving Grace. ||3||<br>
  Shalok, Third Mehl:<br>
  Those who do not meet with the Guru, who have no Fear of God at all,<br>
  continue coming and going in reincarnation, and suffer terrible pain; their anxiety is never relieved.<br>
  They are beaten like clothes being washed on the rocks, and struck every hour like chimes.<br>
  O Nanak, without the True Name, these entanglements are not removed from hanging over one's head. ||1||<br>
  Third Mehl:<br>
  I have searched throughout the three worlds, O my friend; egotism is bad for the world.<br>
  Don't worry, O my soul; speak the Truth, O Nanak, the Truth, and only the Truth. ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  The Lord Himself forgives the Gurmukhs; they are absorbed and immersed in the Lord's Name.<br>
  He Himself links them to devotional worship; they bear the Insignia of the Guru's Shabad.<br>
  Those who turn towards the Guru, as sunmukh, are beautiful. They are famous in the Court of the True Lord.<br>
  In this world, and in the world hereafter, they are liberated; they realize the Lord.<br>
  Blessed, blessed are those humble beings who serve the Lord. I am a sacrifice to them. ||4||<br>
  Shalok, First Mehl:<br>
  The rude, ill-mannered bride is encased in the body-tomb; she is blackened, and her mind is impure.<br>
  She can enjoy her Husband Lord, only if she is virtuous. O Nanak, the soul-bride is unworthy, and without virtue. ||1||<br>
  First Mehl:<br>
  She has good conduct, true self-discipline, and a perfect family.<br>
  O Nanak, day and night, she is always good; she loves her Beloved Husband Lord. ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  One who realizes his own self, is blessed with the treasure of the Naam, the Name of the Lord.<br>
  Granting His Mercy, the Guru merges him in the Word of His Shabad.<br>
  The Word of the Guru's Bani is immaculate and pure; through it, one drinks in the sublime essence of the Lord.<br>
  Those who taste the sublime essence of the Lord, forsake other flavors.<br>
  Drinking in the sublime essence of the Lord, they remain satisfied forever; their hunger and thirst are quenched. ||5||<br>
  Shalok, Third Mehl:<br>
  Her Husband Lord is pleased, and He enjoys His bride; the soul-bride adorns her heart with the Naam, the Name of the Lord.<br>
  O Nanak, that bride who stands before Him, is the most noble and respected woman. ||1||<br>
  First Mehl:<br>
  In her father-in-law's home hereafter, and in her parents' home in this world, she belongs to her Husband Lord. Her Husband is inaccessible and unfathomable.<br>
  O Nanak, she is the happy soul-bride, who is pleasing to her carefree, independent Lord. ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  That king sits upon the throne, who is worthy of that throne.<br>
  Those who realize the True Lord, they alone are the true kings.<br>
  These mere earthly rulers are not called kings; in the love of duality, they suffer.<br>
  Why should someone praise someone else who is also created? They depart in no time at all.<br>
  The One True Lord is eternal and imperishable. One who, as Gurmukh, understands becomes eternal as well. ||6||<br>
  Shalok, Third Mehl:<br>
  The One Lord is the Husband of all. No one is without the Husband Lord.<br>
  O Nanak, they are the pure soul-brides, who merge in the True Guru. ||1||<br>
  Third Mehl:<br>
  The mind is churning with so many waves of desire. How can one be emancipated in the Court of the Lord?<br>
  Be absorbed in the Lord's True Love, and imbued with the deep color of the Lord's Infinite Love.<br>
  O Nanak, by Guru's Grace, one is emancipated, if the consciousness is attached to the True Lord. ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  The Name of the Lord is priceless. How can its value be estimated?<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 101</h2></center>
  He Himself created the entire universe, and He Himself is pervading it.<br>
  The Gurmukhs praise the Lord forever, and through the Truth, they assess Him.<br>
  Through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, the heart-lotus blossoms forth, and in this way, one drinks in the sublime essence of the Lord.<br>
  Coming and going in reincarnation ceases, and one sleeps in peace and poise. ||7||<br>
  Shalok, First Mehl:<br>
  Neither dirty, nor dull, nor saffron, nor any color that fades.<br>
  O Nanak, crimson - deep crimson is the color of one who is imbued with the True Lord. ||1||<br>
  Third Mehl:<br>
  The bumble bee intuitively and fearlessly dwells among the vegetation, flowers and fruits.<br>
  O Nanak, there is only one tree, one flower, and one bumble bee. ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  Those humble beings who struggle with their minds are brave and distinguished heroes.<br>
  Those who realize their own selves, remain forever united with the Lord.<br>
  This is the glory of the spiritual teachers, that they remain absorbed in their mind.<br>
  They attain the Mansion of the Lord's Presence, and focus their meditation on the True Lord.<br>
  Those who conquer their own minds, by Guru's Grace, conquer the world. ||8||<br>
  Shalok, Third Mehl:<br>
  If I were to become a Yogi, and wander around the world, begging from door to door,<br>
  then, when I am summoned to the Court of the Lord, what answer could I give?<br>
  The Naam, the Name of the Lord, is the charity I beg for; contentment is my temple. The True Lord is always with me.<br>
  Nothing is obtained by wearing religious robes; all will be seized by the Messenger of Death.<br>
  O Nanak, talk is false; contemplate the True Name. ||1||<br>
  Third Mehl:<br>
  Through that door, you will be called to account; do not serve at that door.<br>
  Seek and find such a True Guru, who has no equal in His greatness.<br>
  In His Sanctuary, one is released, and no one calls him to account.<br>
  Truth is implanted within Him, and He implants Truth within others. He bestows the blessing of the True Shabad.<br>
  One who has Truth within his heart - his body and mind are also true.<br>
  O Nanak, if one submits to the Hukam, the Command of the True Lord God, he is blessed with true glory and greatness.<br>
  He is immersed and merged in the True Lord, who blesses him with His Glance of Grace. ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  They are not called heroes, who die of egotism, suffering in pain.<br>
  The blind ones do not realize their own selves; in the love of duality, they rot.<br>
  They struggle with great anger; here and hereafter, they suffer in pain.<br>
  The Dear Lord is not pleased by egotism; the Vedas proclaim this clearly.<br>
  Those who die of egotism, shall not find salvation. They die, and are reborn in reincarnation. ||9||<br>
  Shalok, Third Mehl:<br>
  The crow does not become white, and an iron boat does not float across.<br>
  One who puts his faith in the treasure of his Beloved Lord is blessed; he exalts and embellishes others as well.<br>
  One who realizes the Hukam of God's Command - his face is radiant and bright; he floats across, like iron upon wood.<br>
  Forsake thirst and desire, and abide in the Fear of God; O Nanak, these are the most excellent actions. ||1||<br>
  Third Mehl:<br>
  The ignorant people who go to the desert to conquer their minds, are not able to conquer them.<br>
  O Nanak, if this mind is to be conquered, one must contemplate the Word of the Guru's Shabad.<br>
  This mind is not conquered by conquering it, even though everyone longs to do so.<br>
  O Nanak, the mind itself conquers the mind, if one meets with the True Guru. ||2||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 102</h2></center>
  Pauree:<br>
  He created both sides; Shiva dwells within Shakti (the soul dwells within the material universe).<br>
  Through the material universe of Shakti, no one has ever found the Lord; they continue to be born and die in reincarnation.<br>
  Serving the Guru, peace is found, meditating on the Lord with every breath and morsel of food.<br>
  Searching and looking through the Simritees and the Shaastras, I have found that the most sublime person is the slave of the Lord.<br>
  O Nanak, without the Naam, nothing is permanent and stable; I am a sacrifice to the Naam, the Name of the Lord. ||10||<br>
  Shalok, Third Mehl:<br>
  I might become a Pandit, a religious scholar, or an astrologer, and recite the four Vedas with my mouth;<br>
  I might be worshipped throughout the nine regions of the earth for my wisdom and thought;<br>
  let me not forget the Word of Truth, that no one can touch my sacred cooking square.<br>
  Such cooking squares are false, O Nanak; only the One Lord is True. ||1||<br>
  Third Mehl:<br>
  He Himself creates and He Himself acts; He bestows His Glance of Grace.<br>
  He Himself grants glorious greatness; says Nanak, He is the True Lord. ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  Only death is painful; I cannot conceive of anything else as painful.<br>
  It is unstoppable; it stalks and pervades the world, and fights with the sinners.<br>
  Through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, one is immersed in the Lord. Meditating on the Lord, one comes to realize the Lord.<br>
  He alone is emancipated in the Sanctuary of the Lord, who struggles with his own mind.<br>
  One who contemplates and meditates on the Lord in his mind, succeeds in the Court of the Lord. ||11||<br>
  Shalok, First Mehl:<br>
  Submit to the Will of the Lord Commander; in His Court, only Truth is accepted.<br>
  Your Lord and Master shall call you to account; do not go astray on beholding the world.<br>
  One who keeps watch over his heart, and keeps his heart pure, is a dervish, a saintly devotee.<br>
  Love and affection, O Nanak, are in the accounts placed before the Creator. ||1||<br>
  First Mehl:<br>
  One who is unattached like the bumble bee, sees the Lord of the world everywhere.<br>
  The diamond of his mind is pierced through with the Diamond of the Lord's Name; O Nanak, his neck is embellished with it. ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  The self-willed manmukhs are afflicted by death; they cling to Maya in emotional attachment.<br>
  In an instant, they are thrown to the ground and killed; in the love of duality, they are deluded.<br>
  This opportunity shall not come into their hands again; they are beaten by the Messenger of Death with his stick.<br>
  But Death's stick does not even strike those who remain awake and aware in the Love of the Lord.<br>
  All are Yours, and cling to You; only You can save them. ||12||<br>
  Shalok, First Mehl:<br>
  See the imperishable Lord everywhere; attachment to wealth brings only great pain.<br>
  Loaded with dust, you have to cross over the world-ocean; you are not carrying the profit and capital of the Name with you. ||1||<br>
  First Mehl:<br>
  My capital is Your True Name, O Lord; this wealth is inexhaustible and infinite.<br>
  O Nanak, this merchandise is immaculate; blessed is the banker who trades in it. ||2||<br>
  First Mehl:<br>
  Know and enjoy the primal, eternal Love of the Great Lord and Master.<br>
  Blessed with the Naam, O Nanak, you shall strike down the Messenger of Death, and push his face to the ground. ||3||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  He Himself has embellished the body, and placed the nine treasures of the Naam within it.<br>
  He confuses some in doubt; fruitless are their actions.<br>
  Some, as Gurmukh, realize their Lord, the Supreme Soul.<br>
  Some listen to the Lord, and obey Him; sublime and exalted are their actions.<br>
  Love for the Lord wells up deep within, singing the Glorious Praises of the Lord's Name. ||13||<br>
  Shalok, First Mehl:<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 103</h2></center>
  The Fear of God abides in the mind of the innocent; this is the straight path to the One Lord.<br>
  Jealousy and envy bring terrible pain, and one is cursed throughout the three worlds. ||1||<br>
  First Mehl:<br>
  The drum of the Vedas vibrates, bringing dispute and divisiveness.<br>
  O Nanak, contemplate the Naam, the Name of the Lord; there is none except Him. ||2||<br>
  First Mehl:<br>
  The world-ocean of the three qualities is unfathomably deep; how can its bottom be seen?<br>
  If I meet with the great, self-sufficient True Guru, then I am carried across.<br>
  This ocean is filled up with pain and suffering.<br>
  O Nanak, without the True Name, no one's hunger is appeased. ||3||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  Those who search their inner beings, through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, are exalted and adorned.<br>
  They obtain what they wish for, meditating on the Lord's Name.<br>
  One who is blessed by God's Grace, meets with the Guru; he sings the Glorious Praises of the Lord.<br>
  The Righteous Judge of Dharma is his friend; he does not have to walk on the Path of Death.<br>
  He meditates on the Lord's Name, day and night; he is absorbed and immersed in the Lord's Name. ||14||<br>
  Shalok, First Mehl:<br>
  Listen to and speak the Name of the One Lord, who permeates the heavens, this world and the nether regions of the underworld.<br>
  The Hukam of His Command cannot be erased; whatever He has written, shall go with the mortal.<br>
  Who has died, and who kills? Who comes and who goes?<br>
  Who is enraptured, O Nanak, and whose consciousness merges in the Lord? ||1||<br>
  First Mehl:<br>
  In egotism, he dies; possessiveness kills him, and the breath flows out like a river.<br>
  Desire is exhausted, O Nanak, only when the mind is imbued with the Name.<br>
  His eyes are imbued with the eyes of the Lord, and his ears ring with celestial consciousness.<br>
  His tongue drinks in the sweet nectar, dyed crimson by chanting the Name of the Beloved Lord.<br>
  His inner being is drenched with the Lord's fragrance; his worth cannot be described. ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  In this age, the Naam, the Name of the Lord, is the treasure. Only the Naam goes along in the end.<br>
  It is inexhaustible; it is never empty, no matter how much one may eat, consume or spend.<br>
  The Messenger of Death does not even approach the humble servant of the Lord.<br>
  They alone are the true bankers and traders, who have the wealth of the Lord in their laps.<br>
  By the Lord's Mercy, one finds the Lord, only when the Lord Himself sends for him. ||15||<br>
  Shalok, Third Mehl:<br>
  The self-willed manmukh does not appreciate the excellence of trading in Truth. He deals in poison, collects poison, and is in love with poison.<br>
  Outwardly, they call themselves Pandits, religious scholars, but in their minds they are foolish and ignorant.<br>
  They do not focus their consciousness on the Lord; they love to engage in arguments.<br>
  They speak to cause arguments, and earn their living by telling lies.<br>
  In this world, only the Lord's Name is immaculate and pure. All other objects of creation are polluted.<br>
  O Nanak, those who do not remember the Naam, the Name of the Lord, are polluted; they die in ignorance. ||1||<br>
  Third Mehl:<br>
  Without serving the Lord, he suffers in pain; accepting the Hukam of God's Command, pain is gone.<br>
  He Himself is the Giver of peace; He Himself awards punishment.<br>
  O Nanak, know this well; all that happens is according to His Will. ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  Without the Lord's Name, the world is poor. Without the Name, no one is satisfied.<br>
  He is deluded by duality and doubt. In egotism, he suffers in pain.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 104</h2></center>
  Without good karma, he does not obtain anything, no matter how much he may wish for it.<br>
  Coming and going in reincarnation, and birth and death are ended, through the Word of the Guru's Shabad.<br>
  He Himself acts, so unto whom should we complain? There is no other at all. ||16||<br>
  Shalok, Third Mehl:<br>
  In this world, the Saints earn the wealth; they come to meet God through the True Guru.<br>
  The True Guru implants the Truth within; the value of this wealth cannot be described.<br>
  Obtaining this wealth, hunger is relieved, and peace comes to dwell in the mind.<br>
  Only those who have such pre-ordained destiny, come to receive this.<br>
  The world of the self-willed manmukh is poor, crying out for Maya.<br>
  Night and day, it wanders continually, and its hunger is never relieved.<br>
  It never finds calm tranquility, and peace never comes to dwell in its mind.<br>
  It is always plagued by anxiety, and its cynicism never departs.<br>
  O Nanak, without the True Guru, the intellect is perverted; if one meets the True Guru, then one practices the Word of the Shabad.<br>
  Forever and ever, he dwells in peace, and merges in the True Lord. ||1||<br>
  Third Mehl:<br>
  The One who created the world, takes care of it.<br>
  Meditate in remembrance on the One Lord, O Siblings of Destiny; there is none other than Him.<br>
  So eat the food of the Shabad and goodness; eating it, you shall remain satisfied forever.<br>
  Dress yourself in the Praise of the Lord. Forever and ever, it is radiant and bright; it is never polluted.<br>
  I have intuitively earned the true wealth, which never decreases.<br>
  The body is adorned with the Shabad, and is at peace forever and ever.<br>
  O Nanak, the Gurmukh realizes the Lord, who reveals Himself. ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  Deep within the self are meditation and austere self-discipline, when one realizes the Word of the Guru's Shabad.<br>
  Meditating on the Name of the Lord, Har, Har, egotism and ignorance are eliminated.<br>
  One's inner being is overflowing with Ambrosial Nectar; tasting it, the flavor is known.<br>
  Those who taste it become fearless; they are satisfied with the sublime essence of the Lord.<br>
  Those who drink it in, by the Grace of the Lord, are never again afflicted by death. ||17||<br>
  Shalok, Third Mehl:<br>
  People tie up bundles of demerits; no one deals in virtue.<br>
  Rare is that person, O Nanak, who purchases virtue.<br>
  By Guru's Grace, one is blessed with virtue, when the Lord bestows His Glance of Grace. ||1||<br>
  Third Mehl:<br>
  Merits and demerits are the same; they are both created by the Creator.<br>
  O Nanak, one who obeys the Hukam of the Lord's Command, finds peace, contemplating the Word of the Guru's Shabad. ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  The King sits on the throne within the self; He Himself administers justice.<br>
  Through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, the Lord's Court is known; within the self is the Sanctuary, the Mansion of the Lord's Presence.<br>
  The coins are assayed, and the genuine coins are placed in His treasury, while the counterfeit ones find no place.<br>
  The Truest of the True is all-pervading; His justice is forever True.<br>
  One comes to enjoy the Ambrosial essence, when the Name is enshrined in the mind. ||18||<br>
  Shalok, First Mehl:<br>
  When one acts in egotism, then You are not there, Lord. Wherever You are, there is no ego.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 105</h2></center>
  O spiritual teachers, understand this: the Unspoken Speech is in the mind.<br>
  Without the Guru, the essence of reality is not found; the Invisible Lord dwells everywhere.<br>
  One meets the True Guru, and then the Lord is known, when the Word of the Shabad comes to dwell in the mind.<br>
  When self-conceit departs, doubt and fear also depart, and the pain of birth and death is removed.<br>
  Following the Guru's Teachings, the Unseen Lord is seen; the intellect is exalted, and one is carried across.<br>
  O Nanak, chant the chant of 'Sohang hansaa' - 'He is me, and I am Him.' The three worlds are absorbed in Him. ||1||<br>
  Third Mehl:<br>
  Some assay their mind-jewel, and contemplate the Word of the Guru's Shabad.<br>
  Only a few of those humble beings are known in this world, in this Dark Age of Kali Yuga.<br>
  One's self remains blended with the Lord's Self, when egotism and duality are conquered.<br>
  O Nanak, those who are imbued with the Naam cross over the difficult, treacherous and terrifying world-ocean. ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  The self-willed manmukhs do not search within their own selves; they are deluded by their egotistical pride.<br>
  Wandering in the four directions, they grow weary, tormented by burning desire within.<br>
  They do not study the Simritees and the Shaastras; the manmukhs waste away and are lost.<br>
  Without the Guru, no one finds the Naam, the Name of the True Lord.<br>
  One who contemplates the essence of spiritual wisdom and meditates on the Lord is saved. ||19||<br>
  Shalok, Second Mehl:<br>
  He Himself knows, He Himself acts, and He Himself does it right.<br>
  So stand before Him, O Nanak, and offer your prayers. ||1||<br>
  First Mehl:<br>
  He who created the creation, watches over it; He Himself knows.<br>
  Unto whom should I speak, O Nanak, when everything is contained within the home of the heart? ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  Forget everything, and be friends with the One Lord alone.<br>
  Your mind and body shall be enraptured, and the Lord shall burn away your sins.<br>
  Your comings and goings in reincarnation shall cease; you shall not be reborn and die again.<br>
  The True Name shall be your Support, and you shall not burn in sorrow and attachment.<br>
  O Nanak, gather in the treasure of the Naam, the Name of the Lord, within your mind. ||20||<br>
  Shalok, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  You do not forget Maya from your mind; you beg for it with each and every breath.<br>
  You do not even think of that God; O Nanak, it is not in your karma. ||1||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Maya and its wealth shall not go along with you, so why do you cling to it - are you blind?<br>
  Meditate on the Guru's Feet, and the bonds of Maya shall be cut away from you. ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  By the Pleasure of His Will, the Lord inspires us to obey the Hukam of His Command; by the Pleasure of His Will, we find peace.<br>
  By the Pleasure of His Will, He leads us to meet the True Guru; by the Pleasure of His Will, we meditate on the Truth.<br>
  There is no other gift as great as the Pleasure of His Will; this Truth is spoken and proclaimed.<br>
  Those who have such pre-ordained destiny, practice and live the Truth.<br>
  Nanak has entered His Sanctuary; He created the world. ||21||<br>
  Shalok, Third Mehl:<br>
  Those who do not have spiritual wisdom within, do not have even an iota of the Fear of God.<br>
  O Nanak, why kill those who are already dead? The Lord of the Universe Himself has killed them. ||1||<br>
  Third Mehl:<br>
  To read the horoscope of the mind, is the most sublime joyful peace.<br>
  He alone is called a good Brahmin, who understands God in contemplative meditation.<br>
  He praises the Lord, and reads of the Lord, and contemplates the Word of the Guru's Shabad.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 106</h2></center>
  Celebrated and approved is the coming into the world of such a person, who saves all his generations as well.<br>
  Hereafter, no one is questioned about social status; excellent and sublime is the practice of the Word of the Shabad.<br>
  Other study is false, and other actions are false; such people are in love with poison.<br>
  They do not find any peace within themselves; the self-willed manmukhs waste away their lives.<br>
  O Nanak, those who are attuned to the Naam are saved; they have infinite love for the Guru. ||2||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  He Himself creates the creation, and gazes upon it; He Himself is totally True.<br>
  One who does not understand the Hukam, the Command of his Lord and Master, is false.<br>
  By the Pleasure of His Will, the True Lord joins the Gurmukh to Himself.<br>
  He is the One Lord and Master of all; through the Word of the Guru's Shabad, we are blended with Him.<br>
  The Gurmukhs praise Him forever; all are beggars of Him.<br>
  O Nanak, as He Himself makes us dance, we dance. ||22||1||<br>
  Sudh||<br>
  Vaar Of Maaroo, Fifth Mehl, Dakhanay, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  If You tell me to, O my Friend, I will cut off my head and give it to You.<br>
  My eyes long for You; when will I see Your Vision? ||1||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  I am in love with You; I have seen that other love is false.<br>
  Even clothes and food are frightening to me, as long as I do not see my Beloved. ||2||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  I rise early, O my Husband Lord, to behold Your Vision.<br>
  Eye make-up, garlands of flowers, and the flavor of betel leaf, are all nothing but dust, without seeing You. ||3||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  You are True, O my True Lord and Master; You uphold all that is true.<br>
  You created the world, making a place for the Gurmukhs.<br>
  By the Will of the Lord, the Vedas came into being; they discriminate between sin and virtue.<br>
  You created Brahma, Vishnu and Shiva, and the expanse of the three qualities.<br>
  Creating the world of the nine regions, O Lord, You have embellished it with beauty.<br>
  Creating the beings of various kinds, You infused Your power into them.<br>
  No one knows Your limit, O True Creator Lord.<br>
  You Yourself know all ways and means; You Yourself save the Gurmukhs. ||1||<br>
  Dakhanay, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  If You are my friend, then don't separate Yourself from me, even for an instant.<br>
  My soul is fascinated and enticed by You; when will I see You, O my Love? ||1||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Burn in the fire, you evil person; O separation, be dead.<br>
  O my Husband Lord, please sleep upon my bed, that all my sufferings may be gone. ||2||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  The evil person is engrossed in the love of duality; through the disease of egotism, he suffers separation.<br>
  The True Lord King is my friend; meeting with Him, I am so happy. ||3||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  You are inaccessible, merciful and infinite; who can estimate Your worth?<br>
  You created the entire universe; You are the Master of all the worlds.<br>
  No one knows Your creative power, O my all-pervading Lord and Master.<br>
  No one can equal You; You are imperishable and eternal, the Savior of the world.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 107</h2></center>
  You established the four ages; You are the Creator of all worlds.<br>
  You created the comings and goings of reincarnation; not even a particle of filth sticks to You.<br>
  As you are merciful, You attach us to the Feet of the True Guru.<br>
  You cannot be found by any other efforts; You are the eternal, imperishable Creator of the Universe. ||2||<br>
  Dakhanay, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  If You come into my courtyard, all the earth becomes beautiful.<br>
  Other than the One Lord, my Husband, no one else cares for me. ||1||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  All my adornments become beautiful, when You, O Lord, sit in my courtyard and make it Yours.<br>
  Then no traveller who comes to my home shall leave empty-handed. ||2||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  I have spread out my bed for You, O my Husband Lord, and applied all my decorations.<br>
  But even this is not pleasing to me, to wear a garland around my neck. ||3||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  O Supreme Lord God, O Transcendent Lord, You do not take birth.<br>
  By the Hukam of Your Command, You formed the Universe; forming it, You merge into it.<br>
  Your Form cannot be known; how can one meditate on You?<br>
  You are pervading and permeating all; You Yourself reveal Your creative potency.<br>
  Your treasures of devotional worship are overflowing; they never decrease.<br>
  These gems, jewels and diamonds - their value cannot be estimated.<br>
  As You Yourself become merciful, Lord, You link us to the service of the True Guru.<br>
  One who sings the Glorious Praises of the Lord, never suffers any deficiency. ||3||<br>
  Dakhanay, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  When I look within my being, I find that my Beloved is with me.<br>
  All pains are relieved, O Nanak, when He bestows His Glance of Grace. ||1||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Nanak sits, waiting for news of the Lord, and stands at the Lord's Door; serving Him for so long.<br>
  O my Beloved, only You know my objective; I stand, waiting to see the Lord's face. ||2||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  What should I say to you, you fool? Don't look at the vines of others - be a true husband.<br>
  O Nanak, the entire world is blooming, like a garden of flowers. ||3||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  You are Wise, all-knowing and beautiful; You are pervading and permeating all.<br>
  You Yourself are the Lord and Master, and the servant; You worship and adore Yourself.<br>
  You are all-wise and all-seeing; You Yourself are true and pure.<br>
  The Immaculate Lord, my Lord God, is celibate and True.<br>
  God spreads out the expanse of the entire universe, and He Himself plays in it.<br>
  He created this coming and going of reincarnation; creating the wondrous play, He gazes upon it.<br>
  One who is blessed with the Guru's Teachings, is not consigned to the womb of reincarnation, ever again.<br>
  All walk as He makes them walk; nothing is under the control of the created beings. ||4||<br>
  Dakhanay, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  You are walking along the river-bank, but the land is giving way beneath you.<br>
  Watch out! Your foot might slip, and you'll fall in and die. ||1||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  You believe what is false and temporary to be true, and so you run on and on.<br>
  O Nanak, like butter in the fire, it shall melt away; it shall fade away like the water-lily. ||2||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  O my foolish and silly soul, why are you too lazy to serve?<br>
  Such a long time has passed. When will this opportunity come again? ||3||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 108</h2></center>
  Pauree:<br>
  You have no form or shape, no social class or race.<br>
  These humans believe that You are far away; but You are quite obviously apparent.<br>
  You enjoy Yourself in every heart, and no filth sticks to You.<br>
  You are the blissful and infinite Primal Lord God; Your Light is all-pervading.<br>
  Among all divine beings, You are the most divine, O Creator-architect, Rejuvenator of all.<br>
  How can my single tongue worship and adore You? You are the eternal, imperishable, infinite Lord God.<br>
  One whom You Yourself unite with the True Guru - all his generations are saved.<br>
  All Your servants serve You; Nanak is a humble servant at Your Door. ||5||<br>
  Dakhanay, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  He builds a hut of straw, and the fool lights a fire in it.<br>
  Only those who have such pre-ordained destiny on their foreheads, find Shelter with the Master. ||1||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  O Nanak, he grinds the corn, cooks it and places it before himself.<br>
  But without his True Guru, he sits and waits for his food to be blessed. ||2||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  O Nanak, the loaves of bread are baked and placed on the plate.<br>
  Those who obey their Guru, eat and are totally satisfied. ||3||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  You have staged this play in the world, and infused egotism into all beings.<br>
  In the one temple of the body are the five thieves, who continually misbehave.<br>
  The ten brides, the sensory organs were created, and the one husband, the self; the ten are engrossed in flavors and tastes.<br>
  This Maya fascinates and entices them; they wander continually in doubt.<br>
  You created both sides, spirit and matter, Shiva and Shakti.<br>
  Matter loses out to spirit; this is pleasing to the Lord.<br>
  You enshrined spirit within, which leads to merger with the Sat Sangat, the True Congregation.<br>
  Within the bubble, You formed the bubble, which shall once again merge into the water. ||6||<br>
  Dakhanay, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Look ahead; don't turn your face backwards.<br>
  O Nanak, be successful this time, and you shall not be reincarnated again. ||1||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  My joyful friend is called the friend of all.<br>
  All think of Him as their own; He never breaks anyone's heart. ||2||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  The hidden jewel has been found; it has appeared on my forehead.<br>
  Beautiful and exalted is that place, O Nanak, where You dwell, O my Dear Lord. ||3||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  When You are on my side, Lord, what do I need to worry about?<br>
  You entrusted everything to me, when I became Your slave.<br>
  My wealth is inexhaustible, no matter how much I spend and consume.<br>
  The 8.4 million species of beings all work to serve me.<br>
  All these enemies have become my friends, and no one wishes me ill.<br>
  No one calls me to account, since God is my forgiver.<br>
  I have become blissful, and I have found peace, meeting with the Guru, the Lord of the Universe.<br>
  All my affairs have been resolved, since You are pleased with me. ||7||<br>
  Dakhanay, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  I am so eager to see You, O Lord; what does Your face look like?<br>
  I wandered around in such a miserable state, but when I saw You, my mind was comforted and consoled. ||1||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 109</h2></center>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  The miserable endure so much suffering and pain; You alone know their pain, Lord.<br>
  I may know hundreds of thousands of remedies, but I shall live only if I see my Husband Lord. ||2||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  I have seen the river-bank washed away by the raging waters of the river.<br>
  They alone remain intact, who meet with the True Guru. ||3||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  No pain afflicts that humble being who hungers for You, Lord.<br>
  That humble Gurmukh who understands, is celebrated in the four directions.<br>
  Sins run away from that man, who seeks the Sanctuary of the Lord.<br>
  The filth of countless incarnations is washed away, bathing in the dust of the Guru's feet.<br>
  Whoever submits to the Lord's Will does not suffer in sorrow.<br>
  O Dear Lord, You are the friend of all; all believe that You are theirs.<br>
  The glory of the Lord's humble servant is as great as the Glorious Radiance of the Lord.<br>
  Among all, His humble servant is pre-eminent; through His humble servant, the Lord is known. ||8||<br>
  Dakhanay, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Those whom I followed, now follow me.<br>
  Those in whom I placed my hopes, now place their hopes in me. ||1||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  The fly flies around, and comes to the wet lump of molasses.<br>
  Whoever sits on it, is caught; they alone are saved, who have good destiny on their foreheads. ||2||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  I see Him within all. No one is without Him.<br>
  Good destiny is inscribed on the forehead of that companion, who who enjoys the Lord, my Friend. ||3||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  I am a minstrel at His Door, singing His Glorious Praises, to please to my Lord God.<br>
  My God is permanent and stable; others continue coming and going.<br>
  I beg for that gift from the Lord of the World, which will satisfy my hunger.<br>
  O Dear Lord God, please bless Your minstrel with the Blessed Vision of Your Darshan, that I might be satisfied and fulfilled.<br>
  God, the Great Giver, hears the prayer, and summons the minstrel to the Mansion of His Presence.<br>
  Gazing upon God, the minstrel is rid of pain and hunger; he does not think to ask for anything else.<br>
  All desires are fulfilled, touching the feet of God.<br>
  I am His humble, unworthy minstrel; the Primal Lord God has forgiven me. ||9||<br>
  Dakhanay, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  When the soul leaves, you shall become dust, O vacant body; why do you not realize your Husband Lord?<br>
  You are in love with evil people; by what virtues will you enjoy the Lord's Love? ||1||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  O Nanak, without Him, you cannot survive, even for an instant; you cannot afford to forget Him, even for a moment.<br>
  Why are you alienated from Him, O my mind? He takes care of you. ||2||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Those who are imbued with the Love of the Supreme Lord God, their minds and bodies are colored deep crimson.<br>
  O Nanak, without the Name, other thoughts are polluted and corrupt. ||3||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  O Dear Lord, when You are my friend, what sorrow can afflict me?<br>
  You have beaten off and destroyed the cheats that cheat the world.<br>
  The Guru has carried me across the terrifying world-ocean, and I have won the battle.<br>
  Through the Guru's Teachings, I enjoy all the pleasures in the great world-arena.<br>
  The True Lord has brought all my senses and organs under my control.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 110</h2></center>
  Wherever I join them, there they are joined; they do not struggle against me.<br>
  I obtain the fruits of my desires; the Guru has directed me within.<br>
  When Guru Nanak is pleased, O Siblings of Destiny, the Lord is seen to be dwelling near at hand. ||10||<br>
  Dakhanay, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  When You come into my consciousness, then I obtain all peace and comfort.<br>
  Nanak: with Your Name within my mind, O my Husband Lord, I am filled with delight. ||1||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Enjoyment of clothes and corrupt pleasures - all these are nothing more than dust.<br>
  I long for the dust of the feet of those who are imbued with the Lord's Vision. ||2||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Why do you look in other directions? O my heart, take the Support of the Lord alone.<br>
  Become the dust of the feet of the Saints, and find the Lord, the Giver of peace. ||3||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  Without good karma, the Dear Lord is not found; without the True Guru, the mind is not joined to Him.<br>
  Only the Dharma remains stable in this Dark Age of Kali Yuga; these sinners will not last at all.<br>
  Whatever one does with this hand, he obtains with the other hand, without a moment's delay.<br>
  I have examined the four ages, and without the Sangat, the Holy Congregation, egotism does not depart.<br>
  Egotism is never eradicated without the Saadh Sangat, the Company of the Holy.<br>
  As long as one's mind is torn away from his Lord and Master, he finds no place of rest.<br>
  That humble being, who, as Gurmukh, serves the Lord, has the Support of the Imperishable Lord in the home of his heart.<br>
  By the Lord's Grace, peace is obtained, and one is attached to the feet of the Guru, the True Guru. ||11||<br>
  Dakhanay, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  I have searched everywhere for the King over the heads of kings.<br>
  That Master is within my heart; I chant His Name with my mouth. ||1||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  O my mother, the Master has blessed me with the jewel.<br>
  My heart is cooled and soothed, chanting the True Name with my mouth. ||2||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  I have become the bed for my Beloved Husband Lord; my eyes have become the sheets.<br>
  If You look at me, even for an instant, then I obtain peace beyond all price. ||3||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  My mind longs to meet the Lord; how can I obtain the Blessed Vision of His Darshan?<br>
  I obtain hundreds of thousands, if my Lord and Master speaks to me, even for an instant.<br>
  I have searched in four directions; there is no other as great as You, Lord.<br>
  Show me the Path, O Saints. How can I meet God?<br>
  I dedicate my mind to Him, and renounce my ego. This is the Path which I shall take.<br>
  Joining the Sat Sangat, the True Congregation, I serve my Lord and Master continually.<br>
  All my hopes are fulfilled; the Guru has ushered me into the Mansion of the Lord's Presence.<br>
  I cannot conceive of any other as great as You, O my Friend, O Lord of the World. ||12||<br>
  Dakhanay, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  I have become the throne for my Beloved Lord King.<br>
  If You place Your foot on me, I blossom forth like the lotus flower. ||1||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  If my Beloved becomes hungry, I will become food, and place myself before Him.<br>
  I may be crushed, again and again, but like sugarcane, I do not stop yielding sweet juice. ||2||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Break off your love with the cheaters; realize that it is a mirage.<br>
  Your pleasure lasts for only two moments; this traveller wanders through countless homes. ||3||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  God is not found by intellectual devices; He is unknowable and unseen.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 111</h2></center>
  The followers of the six orders wander and roam around wearing religious robes, but they do not meet God.<br>
  They keep the lunar fasts, but they are of no account.<br>
  Those who read the Vedas in their entirety, still do not see the sublime essence of reality.<br>
  They apply ceremonial marks to their foreheads, and take cleansing baths, but they are blackened within.<br>
  They wear religious robes, but without the True Teachings, God is not found.<br>
  One who had strayed, finds the Path again, if such pre-ordained destiny is written on his forehead.<br>
  One who sees the Guru with his eyes, embellishes and exalts his human life. ||13||<br>
  Dakhanay, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Focus on that which will not pass away.<br>
  Abandon your false actions, and meditate on the True Master. ||1||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  God's Light is permeating all, like the moon reflected in the water.<br>
  He Himself is revealed, O Nanak, to one who has such destiny inscribed upon his forehead. ||2||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  One's face becomes beautiful, chanting the Naam, the Name of the Lord, and singing His Glorious Praises, twenty-four hours a day.<br>
  O Nanak, in the Court of the Lord, you shall be accepted; even the homeless find a home there. ||3||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  By wearing religious robes outwardly, God, the Inner-knower is not found.<br>
  Without the One Dear Lord, all wander around aimlessly.<br>
  Their minds are imbued with attachment to family, and so they continually wander around, puffed up with pride.<br>
  The arrogant wander around the world; why are they so proud of their wealth?<br>
  Their wealth shall not go with them when they depart; in an instant, it is gone.<br>
  They wander around in the world, according to the Hukam of the Lord's Command.<br>
  When one's karma is activated, one finds the Guru, and through Him, the Lord and Master is found.<br>
  That humble being, who serves the Lord, has his affairs resolved by the Lord. ||14||<br>
  Dakhanay, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  All speak with their mouths, but rare are those one who realize death.<br>
  Nanak is the dust of the feet of those who have faith in the One Lord. ||1||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Know that He dwells within all; rare are those who realize this.<br>
  There is no obscuring veil on the body of that one, O Nanak, who meets the Guru. ||2||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  I drink in the water which has washed the feet of those who share the Teachings.<br>
  My body is filled with infinite love to see my True Master. ||3||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  Forgetting the Naam, the Name of the Fearless Lord, he becomes attached to Maya.<br>
  He comes and goes, and wanders, dancing in countless incarnations.<br>
  He gives his word, but then backs out. All that he says is false.<br>
  The false person is hollow within; he is totally engrossed in falsehood.<br>
  He tries to take vengeance upon the Lord, who bears no vengeance; such a person is trapped by falsehood and greed.<br>
  The True King, the Primal Lord God, kills him when He sees what he has done.<br>
  The Messenger of Death sees him, and he rots away in pain.<br>
  Even-handed justice is administered, O Nanak, in the Court of the True Lord. ||15||<br>
  Dakhanay, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  In the early hours of the morning, chant the Name of God, and meditate on the Feet of the Guru.<br>
  The filth of birth and death is erased, singing the Glorious Praises of the True Lord. ||1||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  The body is dark, blind and empty, without the Naam, the Name of the Lord.<br>
  O Nanak, fruitful is the birth of one, within whose heart the True Master dwells. ||2||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  With my eyes, I have seen the Light; my great thirst for Him is not quenched.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 112</h2></center>
  O Nanak, these are not the eyes which can see my Beloved Husband Lord. ||3||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  That humble being, who, as Gurmukh, serves the Lord, obtains all peace and pleasure.<br>
  He Himself is saved, along with his family, and all the world is saved as well.<br>
  He collects the wealth of the Lord's Name, and all his thirst is quenched.<br>
  He renounces worldly greed, and his inner being is lovingly attuned to the Lord.<br>
  Forever and ever, the home of his heart is filled with bliss; the Lord is his companion, help and support.<br>
  He looks alike upon enemy and friend, and wishes well to all.<br>
  He alone is fulfilled in this world, who meditates on the spiritual wisdom of the Guru.<br>
  He obtains what is pre-ordained for him, according to the Lord. ||16||<br>
  Dakhanay, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  The true person is said to be beautiful; false is the reputation of the false.<br>
  O Nanak, rare are those who have Truth in their laps. ||1||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  The face of my friend, the Lord, is incomparably beautiful; I would watch Him, twenty-four hours a day.<br>
  In sleep, I saw my Husband Lord; I am a sacrifice to that dream. ||2||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  O my friend, realize the True Lord. Just to talk about Him is useless.<br>
  See Him within your mind; your Beloved is not far away. ||3||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  The earth, the Akaashic ethers of the sky, the nether regions of the underworld, the moon and the sun shall pass away.<br>
  Emperors, bankers, rulers and leaders shall depart, and their homes shall be demolished.<br>
  The poor and the rich, the humble and the intoxicated, all these people shall pass away.<br>
  The Qazis, Shaykhs and preachers shall all arise and depart.<br>
  The spiritual teachers, prophets and disciples - none of these shall remain permanently.<br>
  Fasts, calls to prayer and sacred scriptures - without understanding, all these shall vanish.<br>
  The 8.4 million species of beings of the earth shall all continue coming and going in reincarnation.<br>
  The One True Lord God is eternal and unchanging. The Lord's slave is also eternal. ||17||<br>
  Dakhanay, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  I have seen and examined all; without the One Lord, there is none at all.<br>
  Come, and show me Your face, O my friend, so that my body and mind may be cooled and soothed. ||1||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  The lover is without hope, but within my mind, there is great hope.<br>
  In the midst of hope, only You, O Lord, remain free of hope; I am a sacrifice, a sacrifice, a sacrifice to You. ||2||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Even if I just hear of separation from You, I am in pain; without seeing You, O Lord, I die.<br>
  Without her Beloved, the separated lover takes no comfort. ||3||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  River-banks, sacred shrines, idols, temples, and places of pilgrimage like Kaydarnaat'h, Mat'huraa and Benares,<br>
  the three hundred thirty million gods, along with Indra, shall all pass away.<br>
  The Simritees, Shaastras, the four Vedas and the six systems of philosophy shall vanish.<br>
  Prayer books, Pandits, religious scholars, songs, poems and poets shall also depart.<br>
  Those who are celibate, truthful and charitiable, and the Sannyaasee hermits are all subject to death.<br>
  The silent sages, the Yogis and the nudists, along with the Messengers of Death, shall pass away.<br>
  Whatever is seen shall perish; all will dissolve and disappear.<br>
  Only the Supreme Lord God, the Transcendent Lord, is permanent. His servant becomes permanent as well. ||18||<br>
  Shalok Dakhanay, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Hundreds of times naked does not make the person naked; tens of thousands of hungers do not make him hungry;<br>
  millions of pains do not cause him pain. O Nanak, the Husband Lord blesses him with his Glance of Grace. ||1||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 113</h2></center>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Even if one were to enjoy all pleasures, and be master of the entire earth,<br>
  O Nanak, all of that is just a disease. Without the Naam, he is dead. ||2||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Yearn for the One Lord, and make Him your friend.<br>
  O Nanak, He alone fulfills your hopes; you should feel embarrassed, visiting other places. ||3||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  The One and only Lord is eternal, imperishable, inaccessible and incomprehensible.<br>
  The treasure of the Naam is eternal and imperishable. Meditating in remembrance on Him, the Lord is attained.<br>
  The Kirtan of His Praises is eternal and imperishable; the Gurmukh sings the Glorious Praises of the Lord of the Universe.<br>
  Truth, righteousness, Dharma and intense meditation are eternal and imperishable. Day and night, worship the Lord in adoration.<br>
  Compassion, righteousness, Dharma and intense meditation are eternal and imperishable; they alone obtain these, who have such pre-ordained destiny.<br>
  The inscription inscribed upon one's forehead is eternal and imperishable; it cannot be avoided by avoidance.<br>
  The Congregation, the Company of the Holy, and the word of the humble, are eternal and imperishable. The Holy Guru is eternal and imperishable.<br>
