  Those who have such pre-ordained destiny worship and adore the Lord, forever and ever. ||19||<br>
  Shalok, Dakhanay, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  One who himself has drowned - how can he carry anyone else across?<br>
  One who is imbued with the Love of the Husband Lord - O Nanak, he himself is saved, and he saves others as well. ||1||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Wherever someone speaks and hears the Name of my Beloved Lord,<br>
  that is where I go, O Nanak, to see Him, and blossom forth in bliss. ||2||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  You are in love with your children and your wife; why do you keep calling them your own?<br>
  O Nanak, without the Naam, the Name of the Lord, the human body has no foundation. ||3||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  With my eyes, I gaze upon the Blessed Vision of the Guru's Darshan; I touch my forehead to the Guru's feet.<br>
  With my feet I walk on the Guru's Path; with my hands, I wave the fan over Him.<br>
  I meditate on Akaal Moorat, the undying form, within my heart; day and night, I meditate on Him.<br>
  I have renounced all possessiveness, and have placed my faith in the all-powerful Guru.<br>
  The Guru has blessed me with the treasure of the Naam; I am rid of all sufferings.<br>
  Eat and enjoy the Naam, the Name of the indescribable Lord, O Siblings of Destiny.<br>
  Confirm your faith in the Naam, charity and self-purification; chant the Guru's sermon forever.<br>
  Blessed with intuitive poise, I have found God; I am rid of the fear of the Messenger of Death. ||20||<br>
  Shalok, Dakhanay, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  I am centered and focused on my Beloved, but I am not satisfied, even by seeing Him.<br>
  The Lord and Master is within all; I do not see any other. ||1||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  The sayings of the Saints are the paths of peace.<br>
  O Nanak, they alone obtain them, upon whose foreheads such destiny is written. ||2||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  He is totally permeating the mountains, oceans, deserts, lands, forests, orchards, caves,<br>
  the nether regions of the underworld, the Akaashic ethers of the skies, and all hearts.<br>
  Nanak sees that they are all strung on the same thread. ||3||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  The Dear Lord is my mother, the Dear Lord is my father; the Dear Lord cherishes and nurtures me.<br>
  The Dear Lord takes care of me; I am the child of the Lord.<br>
  Slowly and steadily, He feeds me; He never fails.<br>
  He does not remind me of my faults; He hugs me close in His embrace.<br>
  Whatever I ask for, He give me; the Lord is my peace-giving father.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 114</h2></center>
  He has blessed me with the capital, the wealth of spiritual wisdom; He has made me worthy of this merchandise.<br>
  He has made me a partner with the Guru; I have obtained all peace and comforts.<br>
  He is with me, and shall never separate from me; the Lord, my father, is potent to do everything. ||21||<br>
  Shalok, Dakhanay, Fifth Mehl:<br>
  O Nanak, break away from the false, and seek out the Saints, your true friends.<br>
  The false shall leave you, even while you are still alive; but the Saints shall not forsake you, even when you are dead. ||1||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  O Nanak, the lightning flashes, and thunder echoes in the dark black clouds.<br>
  The downpour from the clouds is heavy; O Nanak, the soul-brides are exalted and embellished with their Beloved. ||2||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  The ponds and the lands are overflowing with water, and the cold wind is blowing.<br>
  Her bed is adorned with gold, diamonds and rubies;<br>
  she is blessed with beautiful gowns and delicacies, O Nanak, but without her Beloved, she burns in agony. ||3||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  He does the dees which the Creator causes him to do.<br>
  Even if you run in hundreds of directions, O mortal, you shall still receive what you are pre-destined to receive.<br>
  Without good karma, you shall obtain nothing, even if you wander across the whole world.<br>
  Meeting with the Guru, you shall know the Fear of God, and other fears shall be taken away.<br>
  Through the Fear of God, the attitude of detachment wells up, and one sets out in search of the Lord.<br>
  Searching and searching, intuitive wisdom wells up, and then, one is not born to die again.<br>
  Practicing meditation within my heart, I have found the Sanctuary of the Holy.<br>
  Whoever the Lord places on the boat of Guru Nanak, is carried across the terrifying world-ocean. ||22||<br>
  Shalok, Dakhanay Fifth Mehl:<br>
  First, accept death, and give up any hope of life.<br>
  Become the dust of the feet of all, and then, you may come to me. ||1||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  See, that only one who has died, truly lives; one who is alive, consider him dead.<br>
  Those who are in love with the One Lord, are the supreme people. ||2||<br>
  Fifth Mehl:<br>
  Pain does not even approach that person, within whose mind God abides.<br>
  Hunger and thirst do not affect him, and the Messenger of Death does not approach him. ||3||<br>
  Pauree:<br>
  Your worth cannot be estimated, O True, Unmoving Lord God.<br>
  The Siddhas, seekers, spiritual teachers and meditators - who among them can measure You?<br>
  You are all-powerful, to form and break; You create and destroy all.<br>
  You are all-powerful to act, and inspire all to act; You speak through each and every heart.<br>
  You give sustanance to all; why should mankind waver?<br>
  You are deep, profound and unfathomable; Your virtuous spiritual wisdom is priceless.<br>
  They do the deeds which they are pre-ordained to do.<br>
  Without You, there is nothing at all; Nanak chants Your Glorious Praises. ||23||1||2||<br>
  Raag Maaroo, The Word Of Kabeer Jee:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  O Pandit, O religious scholar, in what foul thoughts are you engaged?<br>
  You shall be drowned, along with your family, if you do not meditate on the Lord, you unfortunate person. ||1||Pause||<br>
  What is the use of reading the Vedas and the Puraanas? It is like loading a donkey with sandalwood.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 115</h2></center>
  You do not know the exalted state of the Lord's Name; how will you ever cross over? ||1||<br>
  You kill living beings, and call it a righteous action. Tell me, brother, what would you call an unrighteous action?<br>
  You call yourself the most excellent sage; then who would you call a butcher? ||2||<br>
  You are blind in your mind, and do not understand your own self; how can you make others understand, O brother?<br>
  For the sake of Maya and money, you sell knowledge; your life is totally worthless. ||3||<br>
  Naarad and Vyaasa say these things; go and ask Suk Dayv as well.<br>
  Says Kabeer, chanting the Lord's Name, you shall be saved; otherwise, you shall drown, brother. ||4||1||<br>
  Living in the forest, how will you find Him? Not until you remove corruption from your mind.<br>
  Those who look alike upon home and forest, are the most perfect people in the world. ||1||<br>
  You shall find real peace in the Lord,<br>
  if you lovingly dwell on the Lord within your being. ||1||Pause||<br>
  What is the use of wearing matted hair, smearing the body with ashes, and living in a cave?<br>
  Conquering the mind, one conquers the world, and then remains detached from corruption. ||2||<br>
  They all apply make-up to their eyes; there is little difference between their objectives.<br>
  But those eyes, to which the ointment of spiritual wisdom is applied, are approved and supreme. ||3||<br>
  Says Kabeer, now I know my Lord; the Guru has blessed me with spiritual wisdom.<br>
  I have met the Lord, and I am emancipated within; now, my mind does not wander at all. ||4||2||<br>
  You have riches and miraculous spiritual powers; so what business do you have with anyone else?<br>
  What should I say about the reality of your talk? I am embarrassed even to speak to you. ||1||<br>
  One who has found the Lord,<br>
  does not wander from door to door. ||1||Pause||<br>
  The false world wanders all around, in hopes of finding wealth to use for a few days.<br>
  That humble being, who drinks in the Lord's water, never becomes thirsty again. ||2||<br>
  Whoever understands, by Guru's Grace, becomes free of hope in the midst of hope.<br>
  One comes to see the Lord everywhere, when the soul becomes detached. ||3||<br>
  I have tasted the sublime essence of the Lord's Name; the Lord's Name carries everyone across.<br>
  Says Kabeer, I have become like gold; doubt is dispelled, and I have crossed over the world-ocean. ||4||3||<br>
  Like drops of water in the water of the ocean, and like waves in the stream, I merge in the Lord.<br>
  Merging my being into the Absolute Being of God, I have become impartial and transparent, like the air. ||1||<br>
  Why should I come into the world again?<br>
  Coming and going is by the Hukam of His Command; realizing His Hukam, I shall merge in Him. ||1||Pause||<br>
  When the body, formed of the five elements, perishes, then any such doubts shall end.<br>
  Giving up the different schools of philosophy, I look upon all equally; I meditate only on the One Name. ||2||<br>
  Whatever I am attached to, to that I am attached; such are the deeds I do.<br>
  When the Dear Lord grants His Grace, then I am merged in the Word of the Guru's Shabad. ||3||<br>
  Die while yet alive, and by so dying, be alive; thus you shall not be reborn again.<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 116</h2></center>
  Says Kabeer, whoever is absorbed in the Naam remains lovingly absorbed in the Primal, Absolute Lord. ||4||4||<br>
  If You keep me far away from You, then tell me, what is liberation?<br>
  The One has many forms, and is contained within all; how can I be fooled now? ||1||<br>
  O Lord, where will You take me, to save me?<br>
  Tell me where, and what sort of liberation shall You give me? By Your Grace, I have already obtained it. ||1||Pause||<br>
  People talk of salvation and being saved, as long as they do not understand the essence of reality.<br>
  I have now become pure within my heart, says Kabeer, and my mind is pleased and appeased. ||2||5||<br>
  Raawan made castles and fortresses of gold, but he had to abandon them when he left. ||1||<br>
  Why do you act only to please your mind?<br>
  When Death comes and grabs you by the hair, then only the Name of the Lord will save you. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Death, and deathlessness are the creations of our Lord and Master; this show, this expanse, is only an entanglement.<br>
  Says Kabeer, those who have the sublime essence of the Lord in their hearts - in the end, they are liberated. ||2||6||<br>
  The body is a village, and the soul is the owner and farmer; the five farm-hands live there.<br>
  The eyes, nose, ears, tongue and sensory organs of touch do not obey any order. ||1||<br>
  O father, now I shall not live in this village.<br>
  The accountants summoned Chitar and Gupat, the recording scribes of the conscious and the unconscious, to ask for an account of each and every moment. ||1||Pause||<br>
  When the Righteous Judge of Dharma calls for my account, there shall be a very heavy balance against me.<br>
  The five farm-hands shall then run away, and the bailiff shall arrest the soul. ||2||<br>
  Says Kabeer, listen, O Saints: settle your accounts in this farm.<br>
  O Lord, please forgive Your slave now, in this life, so that he may not have to return again to this terrifying world-ocean. ||3||7||<br>
  Raag Maaroo, The Word Of Kabeer Jee:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  No one has seen the Fearless Lord, O renunciate.<br>
  Without the Fear of God, how can the Fearless Lord be obtained? ||1||<br>
  If one sees the Presence of his Husband Lord near at hand, then he feels the Fear of God, O renunciate.<br>
  If he realizes the Hukam of the Lord's Command, then he becomes fearless. ||2||<br>
  Don't practice hypocrisy with the Lord, O renunciate!<br>
  The whole world is filled with hypocrisy. ||3||<br>
  Thirst and desire do not just go away, O renunciate.<br>
  The body is burning in the fire of worldly love and attachment. ||4||<br>
  Anxiety is burned, and the body is burned, O renunciate,<br>
  only if one lets his mind become dead. ||5||<br>
  Without the True Guru, there can be no renunciation,<br>
  even though all the people may wish for it. ||6||<br>
  When God grants His Grace, one meets the True Guru, O renunciate,<br>
  and automatically, intuitively finds that Lord. ||7||<br>
  Says Kabeer, I offer this one prayer, O renunciate.<br>
  Carry me across the terrifying world-ocean. ||8||1||8||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 117</h2></center>
  O king, who will come to you?<br>
  I have seen such love from Bidur, that the poor man is pleasing to me. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Gazing upon your elephants, you have gone astray in doubt; you do not know the Great Lord God.<br>
  I judge Bidur's water to be like ambrosial nectar, in comparison with your milk. ||1||<br>
  I find his rough vegetables to be like rice pudding; the night of my life passes singing the Glorious Praises of the Lord.<br>
  Kabeer's Lord and Master is joyous and blissful; He does not care about anyone's social class. ||2||9||<br>
  Shalok, Kabeer:<br>
  The battle-drum beats in the sky of the mind; aim is taken, and the wound is inflicted.<br>
  The spiritual warriors enter the field of battle; now is the time to fight! ||1||<br>
  He alone is known as a spiritual hero, who fights in defense of religion.<br>
  He may be cut apart, piece by piece, but he never leaves the field of battle. ||2||2||<br>
  Shabad Of Kabeer, Raag Maaroo, The Word Of Naam Dayv Jee:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  I have obtained the four kinds of liberation, and the four miraculous spiritual powers, in the Sanctuary of God, my Husband Lord.<br>
  I am liberated, and famous throughout the four ages; the canopy of praise and fame waves over my head. ||1||<br>
  Meditating on the Sovereign Lord God, who has not been saved?<br>
  Whoever follows the Guru's Teachings and joins the Saadh Sangat, the Company of the Holy, is called the most devoted of the devotees. ||1||Pause||<br>
  He is adorned with the conch, the chakra, the mala and the ceremonial tilak mark on his forehead; gazing upon his radiant glory, the Messenger of Death is scared away.<br>
  He becomes fearless, and the power of the Lord thunders through him; the pains of birth and death are taken away. ||2||<br>
  The Lord blessed Ambreek with fearless dignity, and elevated Bhabhikhan to become king.<br>
  Sudama's Lord and Master blessed him with the nine treasures; he made Dhroo permanent and unmoving; as the north star, he still hasn't moved. ||3||<br>
  For the sake of His devotee Prahlaad, God assumed the form of the man-lion, and killed Harnaakhash.<br>
  Says Naam Dayv, the beautiful-haired Lord is in the power of His devotees; He is standing at Balraja's door, even now! ||4||1||<br>
  Maaroo, Kabeer Jee:<br>
  You have forgotten your religion, O madman; you have forgotten your religion.<br>
  You fill your belly, and sleep like an animal; you have wasted and lost this human life. ||1||Pause||<br>
  You never joined the Saadh Sangat, the Company of the Holy. You are engrossed in false pursuits.<br>
  You wander like a dog, a pig, a crow; soon, you shall have to get up and leave. ||1||<br>
  You believe that you yourself are great, and that others are small.<br>
  Those who are false in thought, word and deed, I have seen them going to hell. ||2||<br>
  The lustful, the angry, the clever, the deceitful and the lazy<br>
  waste their lives in slander, and never remember their Lord in meditation. ||3||<br>
  Says Kabeer, the fools, the idiots and the brutes do not remember the Lord.<br>
  They do not know the Lord's Name; how can they be carried across? ||4||1||<br>
 <center><h2>Section 25 - Raag Maaroo - Part 118</h2></center>
  Raag Maaroo, The Word Of Jai Dayv Jee:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  The breath is drawn in through the left nostril; it is held in the central channel of the Sushmanaa, and exhaled through the right nostril, repeating the Lord's Name sixteen times.<br>
  I am powerless; my power has been broken. My unstable mind has been stabliized, and my unadorned soul has been adorned. I drink in the Ambrosial Nectar. ||1||<br>
  Within my mind, I chant the Name of the Primal Lord God, the Source of virtue.<br>
  My vision, that You are I are separate, has melted away. ||1||Pause||<br>
  I worship the One who is worthy of being worshipped. I trust the One who is worthy of being trusted. Like water merging in water, I merge in the Lord.<br>
  Says Jai Dayv, I meditate and contemplate the Luminous, Triumphant Lord. I am lovingly absorbed in the Nirvaanaa of God. ||2||1||<br>
  Kabeer, Maaroo:<br>
  Meditate in remembrance on the Lord, or else you will regret it in the end, O mind.<br>
  O sinful soul, you act in greed, but today or tomorrow, you will have to get up and leave. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Clinging to greed, you have wasted your life, deluded in the doubt of Maya.<br>
  Do not take pride in your wealth and youth; you shall crumble apart like dry paper. ||1||<br>
  When the Messenger of Death comes and grabs you by the hair, and knocks you down, on that day, you shall be powerless.<br>
  You do not remember the Lord, or vibrate upon Him in meditation, and you do not practice compassion; you shall be beaten on your face. ||2||<br>
  When the Righteous Judge of Dharma calls for your account, what face will you show Him then?<br>
  Says Kabeer, listen, O Saints: in the Saadh Sangat, the Company of the Holy, you shall be saved. ||3||1||<br>
  Raag Maaroo, The Word Of Ravi Daas Jee:<br>
  One Universal Creator God. By The Grace Of The True Guru:<br>
  O Love, who else but You could do such a thing?<br>
  O Patron of the poor, Lord of the World, You have put the canopy of Your Grace over my head. ||1||Pause||<br>
  Only You can grant Mercy to that person whose touch pollutes the world.<br>
  You exalt and elevate the lowly, O my Lord of the Universe; You are not afraid of anyone. ||1||<br>
  Naam Dayv, Kabeer, Trilochan, Sadhana and Sain crossed over.<br>
  Says Ravi Daas, listen, O Saints, through the Dear Lord, all is accomplished. ||2||1||<br>
  MAAROO:<br>
  The Lord is the ocean of peace; the miraculous tree of life, the jewel of miracles and the wish-fulfilling cow are all under His power.<br>
  The four great blessings, the eight great miraculous spiritual powers and the nine treasures are in the palm of His hand. ||1||<br>
  Why don't you chant the Lord's Name, Har, Har, Har?<br>
  Abandon all other devices of words. ||1||Pause||<br>
  The many epics, the Puraanas and the Vedas are all composed out of the letters of the alphabet.<br>
  After careful thought, Vyaasa spoke the supreme truth, that there is nothing equal to the Lord's Name. ||2||<br>
  In intuitive Samaadhi, their troubles are eliminated; the very fortunate ones lovingly focus on the Lord.<br>
  Says Ravi Daas, the Lord's slave remains detached from the world; the fear of birth and death runs away from his mind. ||3||2||15||<br>
